“Not bad, your progress with refining the body is even faster than I expected.” Yun Zhi clapped lightly, giving Lu Yang an immense confidence boost.

Despite rarely being present, Yun Zhi had actually been observing Lu Yang’s progress all this while.

Lu Yang placed the vats down and asked in excitement, “Can I cultivate now?” He quietly waited for the answer, not even daring to breathe out.

During this period, Meng Jingzhou had looked for him but was quickly chased away by the puppet before he could say much. Lu Yang heard that Meng Jingzhou, Man Gu, and the others from his batch had already drawn qi into their bodies, becoming true cultivators. They would sit meditatively and cultivate every day, transcending the mundane world.

He was the only one still struggling to refine his body. He couldn’t help but feel anxious, worried that he would fall behind.

Yun Zhi did not answer him but took out a piece of tofu from her storage space instead. The tofu was extremely soft, jiggling on Yun Zhi’s palm as if it was a balloon filled with water.

“Face your palm down and grab it.”

Lu Yang thought that there was nothing hard about it and followed her instructions. However, as soon as his fingers twitched slightly, the tofu got crushed and fell to the ground.

Yun Zhi passed another tofu to Lu Yang, indicating for him to continue.

Lu Yang was highly skeptical. The first time was just an accident, the second time will surely be fine.

However, he still squashed the tofu, unable to hold it.

When he failed yet again the third time, Lu Yang figured out the problem. His strength was overwhelming to control, and he hadn’t realized it previously because all the items around him were designed for cultivators. Had they been normal items, he would even have to be careful while eating, lest he snap the chopsticks into half and break the bowls into smithereens.

Furthermore, his strength had grown too quickly, and his mind still couldn’t keep up with his body, resulting in the problem of his fingers twitching every now and then. Thus, it was not an easy feat for him to grab something as soft as tofu.

Yun Zhi stopped passing pieces of tofu to Lu Yang. With her palm faced down, she grabbed a tofu and shook it casually, but it just wouldn’t fall apart.

Suddenly, she let go and the tofu fell, but she grabbed hold of the tofu again at lightning speed!

Lu Yang widened his eyes. Catching a falling tofu? That’s easier said than done.

With Yun Zhi’s strength, the soft tofu was no different from a block of metal and could be manipulated as she liked.

“You have already achieved lifting heavy like light, but you still have a long road ahead to mastering lifting light like heavy.”

Lu Yang kept silent. He knew that he was still far from the completion of refining his body. I can’t be too impatient with cultivation. Meng Jingzhou had his family clan teaching him since he was a child, that’s why he can directly cultivate.

Catching up with them will certainly not be easy.

Despite having no one to guide me in my early years, I am able to receive personal guidance from Big Senior Sister and even the help of natural treasures; my growth is already astonishing. What reason do I have not to be content?

Lu Yang even recalled what Yun Zhi had mentioned before. She said that cultivation is a lifelong endeavor. A momentary advantage or disadvantage doesn’t matter; the most important thing is who has the last laugh.

Taking in two deep breaths, Lu Yang realized that his previous mindset was wrong. He quickly adjusted his attitude and told himself not to only pursue rapid progress in cultivation.

Then, he saw Yun Zhi instructing the puppet to push over a trolley of tofu.

1. Although bagua or “eight trigrams” is often used in Feng Shui, the Bagua Steps is referring to the Baguazhang footwork which belongs to a major form of fist martial arts. ☜

Chapter 13: Drawing Qi into the Body

When Lu Yang trained his strength, he could consume spirit beast meat to boost his strength and soak in medicinal baths to reinforce his body. However, when it came to controlling his strength, there was no external cheat—he had only himself to rely on.

The whole process required immense concentration. Using Big Senior Sister’s words, I need to “find the right feeling and use my body rather than my psyche to control my strength.”

What Lu Yang had to do was to naturally catch the tofu without any deliberate effort.

After one whole day ended, Lu Yang was covered with the fishy smell of tofu. His eyes had focused on the tofu for so long that his eyes nearly became crossed.

Fortunately, the experienced puppet came over to give him two slaps, returning his eyes to normal.

When it was time to eat, Lu Yang stared silently at the table full of tofu dishes—stir-fried tofu, deep-fried tofu, steamed tofu, tofu pudding,[1] soy tofu boiled in soy milk...

All the ingredients were the tofu Lu Yang crushed during the day. He even heard that the tofu pudding and soy milk were gifted by the warmhearted shop owner.

Lu Yang thanked all eight generations of his ancestors.

The dishes will remain the same until I can control my strength.

In other words, between me and tofu, one of us will definitely be finished.

Tofu was not an ordinary food. Long-term consumption could regulate a cultivator’s balance of the five elements, prolonging their breaths and increasing their stamina during a battle. These were just a few out of the countless other benefits.

But no one can stand eating tofu every single day.

Lu Yang had no choice but to dig into his meal, pondering about how he could better control his strength the next day.

~~~

While still in his slumber, Lu Yang felt a dazzling white light shining on his face, causing his eyelids to stick together and form a contorted expression. Only until he had gradually adapted to the strong light did he try to open his eyes.

He found himself in an immaculately white space. His surroundings were filled with thick fog, limiting his visibility to only a small area around him. But Lu Yang couldn’t find the source of the light.

“Where is this place?” Lu Yang was a little frantic. I’m sleeping right in the Dao-Seeking Sect, where numerous experts congregate, and Big Senior Sister is just next door. Who could have stealthily pulled me into this mysterious space?

Are they a friend or a foe?

An imposing voice emitted from within the fog, distant like it had traveled from the ancient past and dwelled in the river of time. “Young man, this is a temporary space built by yours truly. No one can detect it.”

Lu Yang’s chest tightened. The other party’s methods were unimaginable. He could only hope that they didn’t bear any ill intention toward him.

“I have witnessed the ancient times and seen many experts with unrivaled cultivation, but not a single one of them could escape from the erosion of time. Their passion and ardent desire to overcome challenges ultimately wound up in a final sigh before their last breath.

“No matter how peerless they had been, I remain carefree and exist eternally.” The voice sounded hoarse from the vicissitudes of life, carrying a hint of weariness from everything returning to nothingness.

The existence of this unparalleled expert was beyond Lu Yang’s imagination.

The expert continued, “I had a sudden whim today to do a quick divination, and I calculated that you and I are fated, so I summoned your soul to this temporary space to receive my legacy.

“This space contains all the cultivation techniques required from the Qi Training Stage to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage; it comprises pills, secret manuals, cultivation insights, and more. Every time you reach a stage, you’ll be able to unlock a part of my legacy.”

Lu Yang let out a breath of relief. The other party seems friendly. He cupped his fists and asked politely, “Who are you, Senior?”

The senior laughed three times before strolling out from within the fog.

His face was white, his skin was fair, and his head...was a block of tofu.

Senior Tofu came closer, speaking faster, “I am the Tofu Heavenly Sovereign. This is my life’s learning. The more tofu you eat, the faster your cultivation will rise. With a solid foundation, you can then challenge those above your level and embrace women left and right. Reaching the peak of this continent will be no problem at all...”

Frightened until cold sweat broke out, Lu Yang’s eyes jolted open. He sat up on his bed and surveyed his surroundings blankly. Only upon confirming that there was nothing but darkness and silence did he heave a sigh of relief.

“So it was all just a dream. Luckily, it was a dream.”

Lu Yang could still feel his back soaked in cold sweat, fear lingering in his heart.

~~~

Yun Zhi slowly opened her eyes, a blue light from Lu Yang’s room returning to her fingertip.

She mumbled to herself, “Now, he will probably train even harder.”

Shifu had said that appropriate pressure can be translated to motivation and encourage one to become even more determined to succeed.

Yun Zhi herself was a successful example, so she believed that her master’s words made a lot of sense. As such, she used the Dream-Entering Technique to give Lu Yang a teeny weeny bit of pressure.

“The lines provided by Eighth Elder are a bit embarrassing. I wonder how he usually manages to say them.”

Yun Zhi was adept at consulting others. All the steps and lines played out in the dreamscape were written by Eighth Elder.

Eighth Elder assured me that it’d be effective.

~~~

Some time passed again. Yun Zhi noted that Lu Yang could now effortlessly grab tofu, throw it high up, and even catch it firmly. He even used the tofu as a sandbag, tossing it back and forth with the puppet.

It was as if the smooth and soft tofu had become a part of his body.

“You have achieved lifting light as if heavy. This phase shall end.”

Lu Yang smiled. After relentless practice of grabbing tofu, his impatience had also gradually settled down.

I am no longer the old me. I need no inner cultivation method or mantra to do this.

“What do you want to train next?”

Lu Yang no longer aimed to have the same amount of progress as his peers. I believe that Big Senior Sister must have her reasons for planning my current arrangements in such a manner.

A rare faint smile graced Yun Zhi’s countenance. “Reinforce your Qi Training Stage cultivation.”

Lu Yang was stunned and pointed to himself? “Qi Training Stage? Me?”

He didn’t know when he had turned into a Qi Training cultivator. Didn’t the books say that to succeed in drawing qi into the body, one must receive guidance from seniors, learn their cultivation techniques, shut off the five senses, and organize the meridians?

For those with poorer talent, they would even need the assistance of pills.

Updated from freewebnσvel.cøm.

I haven’t met a single one of these criteria.

Yun Zhi had not taught him how to draw qi into his body, and neither had she passed on any astonishing cultivation techniques. Moreover, he had not closed off his senses and the unknown sixth sense. As for his meridians, he had no memory of having organized it before.

Dao-Seeking Sect disciples didn’t require pills to draw qi into the body; they were all one-in-a-thousand geniuses. If they still required the help of pills to enter the Qi Training Stage, it would be better for them to withdraw from the sect instead.

Lu Yang believed that he couldn’t use pills, but he was bewildered why he had suddenly attained the Qi Training Stage.

“The early morning three days ago,” Yun Zhi hinted.

The memory suddenly came to Lu Yang. That day, he had woken up very early. Facing the light at dawn with his eyes closed, he ruminated about how he could successfully grab the tofu.

As his thoughts wandered deeper, he gradually lost awareness of his surroundings, as if he had transformed into a rising wisp of air floating between the heavens and the earth. After that, his consciousness grew heavy and returned to his body. At that moment, he felt a wave of enlightenment wash over him, and vaguely felt like there was warm air flowing in his dantian.[2]

It was also then that he successfully grabbed the tofu for the first time.

He remembered that Yun Zhi was not present when he was practicing grabbing tofu. So all this while, Big Senior Sister has been observing me from somewhere.

“It seems like that feeling was me drawing qi into the body.” Lu Yang mumbled, caught up in his own thoughts.

That feeling was really amazing. It felt like I was in the clouds and enveloped in warmth. It was so comfortable that I didn’t want to open my eyes.

Without him noticing, he had already achieved a tiny wish of his—drawing qi into the body and becoming a Qi Training cultivator.

1. Fun fact: it is actually called “tofu brain” in Chinese. ☜

2. Dantian is a center of qi in the body. The most common dantian mentioned is usually the lower dantian, situated around the lower abdomen. The upper and middle dantian are between the eyebrows and at the chest area respectively. ☜

Chapter 14: Big Senior Sister, You Are Right

Most cultivators were at the Qi Training Stage. As such, cultivators adopted the practice of dividing this stage into nine levels, while the more advanced cultivation stages were classified into three classes: basic, intermediate, and advanced.

Only the Dao-Seeking Sect was different. The Qi Training Stage was merely an entry-level threshold for disciples. Why bother separating the most basic step into smaller levels?

Lu Yang was curious. “Do others also draw qi into their body like this?” If everyone trained like this, why is my progress the slowest?

Yun Zhi shook her head. “This is the original cultivation method by the ancient forebears. Connecting with nature, they achieved the harmonious state of heaven and man as one, drawing spirit qi into their body and swiftly becoming cultivators.”

The earliest cultivation naturally required neither guidance from a senior nor secret manuals. It was all about constant enlightenment and trial and error with their bodies.

She continued, “As for your meridians, they had been fully opened during your medicinal baths, and now spirit qi runs freely. Under the state of heaven and man as one, the spirit qi will flow through your body according to your feelings. This path of qi flow will be best suited for you, surpassing any other cultivation techniques.”

The cultivation world liked to split the cultivation techniques into five ranks: Yellow, Black, Earth, Heaven, Immortal. However, Yun Zhi only recognized two types of techniques—techniques that were suitable for oneself and techniques not suitable for oneself.

“None of the existing cultivation techniques were designed for you at their creation. There are many cultivation techniques that are suitable for a Sword Spirit Root. In fact, I have a whole box with me, but they’re all not suitable for you.

"From today onward, I will be assigning you a long-term task—create your own cultivation technique.”

When Yun Zhi spoke of creating one’s own technique, she hadn’t meant for Lu Yang to figure it out alone. She intended to guide him by his side. Even then, the challenges within were apparent. Creating cultivation techniques was something only the elders in the cultivation world were capable of doing.

Lu Yang’s mouth twitched. “The seniors who create cultivation techniques are of such high positions. They have the knowledge of all cultivation stages at their fingertips. That’s how they are qualified to create cultivation techniques. As for me, I’m just a novice who just drew qi into my body, isn’t that too...”

Yun Zhi cut Lu Yang off before he could complain further. “Creating cultivation techniques isn’t as hard as you think.

“Did you know that the Dao-Seeking Sect has a rule that after every disciple reaches the Foundation Establishment Stage, they must complete missions issued by the Great Mission Hall to fulfill their obligations as part of the righteous path?”

Lu Yang nodded. He had heard about it.

Other sects had similar systems, requiring their disciples to complete missions. After all, sects were not places for idlers. Only by contributing to the sect could one demonstrate their value.

However, the Five Great Immortal Sects were different. They requested that disciples issue missions not for contributing to the sect but rather the righteous path. Having the Five Great Immortal Sects as the leader of the righteous path was not just for show.

“Most missions require people to go down the mountain to exterminate demons and devils, exorcise ghosts, and more. I don’t like the feeling of the mundane world, so I chose another method to finish the missions.”

"What was it?"

“There is a fixed task in the Great Mission Hall—introduce a new cultivation technique that doesn’t exist in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s records. That also counts as completing a mission.”

“Then Big Senior Sister, you...” Lu Yang had a bold and seemingly ridiculous thought.

Yun Zhi continued, "So to deal with...I mean, complete the mission, I created many cultivation techniques myself and lied to them that I found them in ancient cave ruins.

"Unfortunately, I got caught later."

“How did that happen?” asked Lu Yang.

“Because according to my reports, I had already explored all the ancient cave ruins. I didn’t know how to make up the next location. See, creating cultivation techniques isn't difficult." Yun Zhi presented her argument “logically” and “convincingly.”

Lu Yang opened his mouth, wanting to say, "Big Senior Sister, I thought you were an honest person; I didn’t expect you to lie too" or "Big Senior Sister, we ordinary folks can’t compare to your peerless talent" or "What you call creating techniques is what I call making up techniques."

Faced with Yun Zhi's cold gaze, everything Lu Yang wanted to say was condensed into one sentence: “You are right, Big Senior Sister.”

"You may have become a cultivator now, but you're still far from becoming a qualified sword cultivator. Take this book."

Yun Zhi handed him an ancient book made from the hide of some unknown demon beast. It was large, thick, and heavy.

"Accounts of the Demon Region?" Lu Yang opened the book and was assaulted by a wave of baleful aura. All kinds of demon beasts seemed to leap off the pages, and he could vaguely hear their roars in his ears.

This ancient book is absolutely priceless!

Lu Yang pondered. Sword cultivators need sword intent. I’ve just arrived at the Qi Training Stage. How do I cultivate sword intent?

He had heard that ancient sword cultivators had been enlightened and developed their first sword intent in the moment between life and death during battles with demon beasts.

The answer was now clear. He needed to observe demon beasts, comprehend their ferocity, and encapsulate his enlightenment from experiences with a myriad of demon beasts to discover his own unique sword intent. Although this method was difficult, it was suitable for someone with a Sword Spirit Root like himself.

It also shows Big Senior Sister's high expectations for me.

Tofu again?

Actually, it wasn't that the Qingfeng sword was too light. On the contrary, it was too heavy for cultivators in the first three levels of the Qi Training Stage. They wouldn’t even be able to lift it.

But Lu Yang was different. After his training with the water vats, his strength had grown beyond his own imagination. To say it proudly, he didn't need any techniques. A simple punch from him could easily defeat a cultivator at the first three levels of the Qi Training Stage.

Perhaps because he had entered the Qi Training stage, his talent in swordsmanship began to show. Combined with his newly acquired ability to “lift light as if heavy,” Lu Yang used the Qingfeng sword with ease.

In just over ten days, Lu Yang was able to carve demon beast shapes out of tofu, as well as figures of himself and Yun Zhi. He could even carve the nine lotus-shaped mountain peaks of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Following in the footsteps of folk performers, Lu Yang had learned a new skill, which he could also showcase in the kitchen.

However, he had no choice but to speed up; he simply couldn't eat any more tofu.

After completing this phase, Yun Zhi appeared and offered him some encouragement. Then, she took out a single white sesame seed. "Sword cultivators also need to train their eyesight. Now, I'll throw this sesame seed into the tofu dregs. You need to find it within the shortest time possible."

Lu Yang fell to his knees with a thud and implored, "Big Senior Sister, can we try a different method?!"

Yun Zhi looked at Lu Yang placidly, her eyes unwavering.

"Oh, okay."

Chapter 15: The Great Mission Hall

Ever since then, Lu Yang led a rather fulfilling life. In the early mornings, he would sit at the mountain summit, sitting in a meditative state as he basked in the light of dawn. Later in the mornings, he would put his heart into honing his sword techniques. At noon, he would find himself a tree branch and take a brief nap. When afternoon came around, he would be pumped with energy as he sparred with the puppet and got beaten up. After dinner, he would finish the homework Yun Zhi assigned him by the candlelight.

Just like that, a year had passed, and Lu Yang’s cultivation had steadily risen.

~~~

“Look! Isn’t that the sect leader’s fourth disciple, Sword Spirit Root Lu Yang?”

Inside the Great Mission Hall, Lu Yang was especially conspicuous. He donned white robes, and his gaze was bright. By his waist was a sword, and its hilt had a red tassel tied to it. Anyone who saw him would inevitably praise that he was a fine, talented young man.

Many disciples in the Dao-Seeking Sect knew one another. Especially in a place like the Great Mission Hall where they would sometimes encounter people they didn’t see as often, they would often make a comment or two out of curiosity.

Not only was Lu Yang the top performer in the entrance trials, he also possessed a Sword Spirit Root, provoked the good-natured River Spirit and Dai Bufan, became a disciple of the sect leader, and received the personal guidance of Yun Zhi. With this myriad of reasons, he stood out among the new cohort of disciples and had gained considerable fame.

Despite Tao Yaoye’s celestial-like beauty, she couldn’t compare to Lu Yang.

“Lu Yang, the one personally taught by Big Senior Sister? Dang, it really is him.”

“I heard that it has been a year since he joined the sect, and he just became a Foundation Establishment cultivator a few days ago.”

“Already at the Foundation Establishment Stage? No wonder he’s here at the Great Mission Hall. He is probably going to accept a mission to train and get some experience.”

Lu Yang was no longer a stranger to surrounding gazes that viewed him as if he were a rare and precious breed of animal.

The senior brothers are right. I successfully reached the Foundation Establishment Stage seven days ago, then I used seven more days to reinforce my cultivation before officially emerging from my seclusion. I’m now here according to Big Senior Sister’s instructions to go out more.

Lu Yang couldn’t help but exclaim as he took in the multitude of missions available in the Great Mission Hall, from slaying murderous old Fusion devils to searching for cats and dogs.

A mission that caught Lu Yang’s attention requested a dual cultivation technique[1]—a proper one.

There were two types of dual cultivation techniques—proper and improper ones. Proper dual cultivation techniques needed no further explanation. They were for the purpose of having a male and female helping each other to balance their yin and yang.

Improper dual cultivation techniques needed even less of an explanation.

The mission was posted by a fox demon who had registered with the Dao-Seeking Sect. Although the Dao-Seeking Sect’s responsibilities included subduing demons and devils, it wasn’t done indiscriminately. When it came to the innocent demons who had no ill intentions toward humans, the Dao-Seeking Sect would not subdue them but instead let them register with the sect and be conferred a legal status.

This fox demon was one of them. Her name was Su Yan, and she was an ordinary little fox living in the old mountains and forests. While playing, she got caught in a hunter’s trap. Fortunately, a young noble had gone to the mountains to play and managed to rescue her, successfully wasting the hunter’s efforts for the day.

Later, Su Yan consumed a transformation fruit in a hidden mountain cave. It activated the bloodline in her, and she became a fox demon. She was a grateful one, so she transformed into human form and went to repay that scion.

Although the young master was now the head of the family and had come across numerous women, none of them were as beautiful as Su Yan.

As such, the two naturally got married.

However, a problem soon arose.

As the fox demon was born with a Charming Constitution, she would uncontrollably absorb yang energy. When both husband and wife engaged in bedroom affairs, the husband would always be drained of his yang energy.

The good news was that yang energy could be restored, so it was not fatal as long as they reduced the frequency of their bedroom affairs.

Another problem arose. The two were newlyweds, so how could they possibly be willing to regulate their bedroom affairs? However, if the frequency was too high, the husband would gradually appear wan, which could easily lead to rumors. Hence, Su Yan hoped to cultivate a proper dual cultivation technique to control her Charming Constitution.

This mission had been posted for a long time, but no one accepted it.

The reason was not because dual cultivation techniques were scarce. If a senior brother asks you for improper dual cultivation techniques, what should you do? Should you say that you have them or not? Should you hand it over or not?

And what would the senior and junior sisters think of you?

Both of us have Variant Spirit Roots, and our cultivation talents aren’t really different. It’s a bit unexpected that Lu Yang reached the Foundation Establishment Stage later than me.

“There are signs of diabolic sacrificial rituals in the north. It is recommended that cultivators at the Golden Core Stage or above head over to investigate. The mission rewards are four hundred contribution points, with additional rewards for extra information.

“Daoist Li Hong from the Mountain Sea Pass has lost a pet and needs someone to look for it.” Lu Yang paused. This seems like a decent mission. Searching for some cat or dog is not dangerous.

He continued reading, “The lost pet is a ferocious winged tiger at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage. If found, this mission rewards five thousand contribution points.”

Lu Yang shrunk back. A demon beast, Nascent Soul Stage, and on top of that, a winged ferocious tiger with an ancient bloodline. Is this where the idiom “boost in power like a tiger that has grown wings” came from? I am not even qualified to become the tiger’s toothpick.

Next, next.

The mission rewards are eight thousand contribution points, and there are additional rewards should the cave turn out to be precious.”

Yet another mission unrelated to me.

Had they been in the outside world, Qi Training cultivators could wander across the jianghu and be considered an expert, Foundation Establishment cultivators could rule over a small territory and enjoy fortune for a hundred years, while Golden Core cultivators could address themselves as “True Person (zhenren)”[2] and establish their own sect.

On the contrary, in the Dao-Seeking Sect, any random passer-by could be a Golden Core cultivator. If one were to throw a brick into the crowd here...not only would it easily hit many of them, but the brick would also likely get thrown back.

All disciples in the Dao-Seeking Sect were elites selected from one in a thousand. Before Lu Yang’s batch of disciples, cultivators at the Qi Training and Foundation Establishment stages did not even exist in the sect, with the lowest cultivation of disciples being the Golden Core Stage.

No matter how much one thrived outside, they would have to obediently play their part once they came back to the Dao-Seeking Sect. This was why there weren’t many options for Foundation Establishment cultivators looking for a mission. The ones Lu Yang had gone through minimally required either Golden Core or Nascent Soul cultivation.

“Note: Big Senior Sister Yun Zhi, please don’t accept this mission. The scripture library has already set up a Yun Zhi section. You can directly place the cultivation techniques you have scribed there.”

On the flying vessel, Lu Yang stood up in excitement as he reached a climax. He gestured with his hands as he subjected Tao Yaoye to his speech that knew no boundaries.

Tao Yaoye didn’t know what to say to that.

The two sat inside the cabin of the flying vessel as it flew through the clouds. There was a balancing array mass-produced by an array master at the bottom, so passengers wouldn’t feel a single thing even when traversing tempests and rainstorms.

The weather was clear, perfect for basking in the sun and enjoying the scenery while sitting in a meditative position on the deck. Tao Yaoye had suggested that the two of them go out to the deck, but Lu Yang had adamantly refused.

Tao Yaoye was more curious than the average person. After pressing for answers repeatedly, Lu Yang had no choice but to explain his fear of heights by starting from ancient times and citing various classics with conviction to prove that a fear of heights was a reasonable and age-old mentality. To speak about it more broadly, it could even contribute to human progress.

Fortunately, Tao Yaoye didn’t believe a single word of it.

Chapter 17: Have You Heard Of Earthly Immortals

“Senior Brother Lu, I remember that you have a Sword Spirit Root?” Tao Yaoye glanced at the ancient-looking sword hung at Lu Yang’s waist and the old calluses on his palms. Achieving all this in just a year is enough to show how diligent he has been in practicing his sword.

Lu Yang nodded, humbly admitting, “I’m barely considered a sword cultivator.”

Cultivators were divided into various categories according to what they specialized in. Some included pill cultivators, talisman cultivators, array cultivators, physique cultivators, and sword cultivators. Among them, sword cultivators had the strongest attack power. At the same cultivation stage, no one would want to have a sword cultivator as their opponent.

Sword cultivators were most renowned for “One Sword Breaks All Spells”—no matter how powerful the opponent’s powers were, the sword cultivator could slice through it with a single strike.

Opposite of sword cultivators were Daoist cultivators—no matter how powerful the opponent’s sword technique was, the Daoist cultivator could counter them with “All Spells Break One Sword.”

Apart from “One Sword Breaks All Spells,” there were other famous moves such as “Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate” and “Flying Sword.”

One could imagine how heroic they would appear as they stepped on their flying swords and braved the wind and waves while clad in snow-white.

What did cultivators seek?

Strength and style.

Sword cultivators fit these two criteria perfectly. Countless cultivators aspired to become a sword cultivator, but they were unfortunately limited by their lack of sword cultivation talent.

“So, Senior Brother Lu, what are you going to do after learning how to fly with swords?”

Tao Yaoye had never heard of a sword cultivator with a fear of heights. Others cultivate to soar through the skies and become carefree, but I’m afraid Senior Brother Lu won’t be able to enjoy that.

Lu Yang answered in a proper manner, “Sword immortals don’t have to be synonymous with soaring through the skies. Have you heard of ‘earthly sword immortal,’ Junior Sister Tao Yaoye?”

Tao Yaoye was taken aback. Seeing how serious Lu Yang was and finding the term “earthly immortal”[1] very familiar, she went along and nodded.

“Who said that immortals must be high up? The word immortal contains the word ‘mortal.’ Immortals are in the sky while mortals are on land. Together, immortals traverse both the sky and land freely, as high up as the moon and stars and as deep as the abyss.

“The term ‘earthly sword immortal’ illustrates that sword immortals are not only in the skies. They can also walk the earth. When their sword flies out, they can slay demons and devils from a thousand li away.

“My goal is to become an earthly sword immortal!”

Tao Yaoye was just about to follow along and nod when the cool-headedness she had trained over the years stopped her and let her realize the crux of the problem. “Hold on, I’ve only heard of earthly sword gods. Where did the term ‘earthly sword immortals’ come from?”

Lu Yang stared at Tao Yaoye for three seconds, as if ancient secrets lay hidden within him.

Then, he slowly let out, “I made that up.”

His attitude was so sincere that Tao Yaoye was rendered speechless.

She chose to not dwell on his topic any longer. With only three days of interaction, her image of Senior Brother Lu had completely crumbled.

During the first round of the trials, she had personally witnessed the announcement of Lu Yang’s Sword Spirit Root. At that time, her image of Lu Yang was that of an unyielding and upright sword capable of splitting the heavens. Despite not being a man of many words, he was staunch and unwavering no matter the obstacles.

After the second round ended and she heard of Lu Yang’s unique method of passing, she felt that sword cultivators were quick and flexible with their minds, and she believed that Lu Yang would likely achieve even greater heights in the future.

By the third round of the trials, she had been so exhausted on Heart-Seeking Mountain that she could barely open her eyes. Just when she thought that it was impossible for anyone to reach the fiftieth step, she saw Lu Yang accomplishing just that. Lu Yang’s success had given her a tremendous boost in morale, motivating her to continue climbing up the mountain until she finally passed.

Now, a year had passed, and the Senior Brother Lu she met again had a fear of heights and was extremely talkative.

She finally understood the concept of “distance creates beauty.”

“Based on the timing, we should be disembarking from the boat soon.” Lu Yang laid out a large map. Its drawings were very detailed, marking out places like the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Great Xia Dynasty’s capital, well-known mountains and rivers, important cities, and even cave paradises.

This was a map depicting one-eighth of the Central Continent. There was even a small red dot moving very slowly. If one didn’t pay attention, they would have thought that the small red dot was stationary. This small red dot marked their current location.

The map was not an ordinary one but an essential magical treasure for travel. Although the map was of superior quality, Taiping Village was still too small to be marked on the map. It was hard to have even Quhe Commandery marked out.

This flying vessel had set off from the Dao-Seeking Sect, then traveled to the Great Xia Dynasty’s capital, journeying for tens and thousands of li. Considering the distance they had covered, Quhe Commandery was insignificant in comparison and barely marked out with a name on the map.

The flying vessel wouldn’t stop at small places like Quhe Commandery. If it were to stop at every single place, its speed would drastically reduce, and its effectiveness wouldn’t be much better than a horse carriage. As such, it would only stop at major transportation hubs like the Dao-Seeking Sect, Qingyun City, Sky-Reaching Valley, Crouching Dragon Mountain, and the capital.

Lu Yang had heard from Yun Zhi that they could directly jump off the boat should they wish to alight. That got his eyes twitching non-stop.

The flying vessel was similar to airplanes from his past life, possessing high speeds and prioritizing efficiency. The greatest difference was that in his past life, passengers simply had to wait for the plane to touch down before disembarking. On the contrary, passengers in the cultivation world could leap off whenever they wanted—the epitome of freedom and openness.

Updated from freewёbnoνel.com.

It was Lu Yang’s first time jumping off, and he was overwhelmed with emotions—evident from his trembling legs.

We are ten thousand meters in the air.

“Senior Brother Lu, do you know how to disembark?”

“Of course.” Lu Yang puffed out his chest, slightly proud.

At this altitude, if one doesn’t use proper techniques and falls straight down, even Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivators would turn into a pile of minced meat.

Lu Yang had asked Yun Zhi how exactly he could disembark, but the latter had avoided his question, telling him that he should check the books or ask other people; he should figure out a way by himself and develop the good habit of independent thinking.

After that, Lu Yang had successfully come up with a way to disembark, and he was prepared to do so. However, they weren’t the only ones disembarking. There were around seven to eight other strangers.

The pair stood at the edge of the deck with the other strangers in a line.

The other strangers took out standard paper umbrellas.

Tao Yaoye took out a meticulously crafted red paper umbrella.

Lu Yang took out a parachute[2].

“Hmm?” Lu Yang felt that he didn’t seem to fit in. Why is everyone else taking out something different from me?”

While Lu Yang was puzzled as to what they planned to do, an impatient middle-aged person in black leaped out of the flying vessel. The middle-aged person in black fell like a cannonball and didn’t stop accelerating. He unhurriedly injected spirit energy into the paper umbrella. The light, thread-like spirit energy was like a nimble green snake that climbed up the handle of the umbrella and wrapped itself around the rib.

It seemed as if the paper umbrella had come to life, awakening from its winter hibernation and stretching its body. The middle-aged person’s descent slowed down, swaying gently as he landed safely.

Letting go, the paper umbrella closed and turned into a ray of light. It darted through the sea of clouds before returning to the flying vessel. The paper umbrella didn’t belong to the man. It was meant to be loaned to passengers of the flying vessel.

The remaining strangers and Tao Yaoye turned to look at Lu Yang in succession, their eyes filled with bewilderment. We are all holding umbrellas to prepare for jumping off the boat. But why are you carrying a bag?

Lu Yang appeared unflustered. Despite the confused gazes, he returned a brilliant smile, as if he wasn’t the one out of place.

In reality, it was a scene of violent storms and raging seas in his heart. He didn’t even know where to start cursing.

All his words condensed into one sentence: "Big Senior Sister, you misled me!”

Chapter 18: Demon Bird

Lu Yang’s understanding of the cultivation world was not holistic. Before entering the Dao-Seeking Sect, his main sources of information were from the storyteller. A year had passed since he joined the sect, and his knowledge of cultivation had improved at an astonishing rate, but none of the books he read stated how one could disembark from a flying vessel.

Who would write such things in a book? When it came to daily life in the cultivation world, he was still far behind people like Tao Yaoye who had grown up in an ancestral cultivation clan. As for the flying vessel, the only thing he knew was that it was a property of the Luodi Merchant Guild. The method of disembarkment was jumping off, but he wasn’t sure exactly how.

Every year, the flying vessel could bring in enormous amounts of wealth, but this was an inconsequential business considering the entire merchant guild’s scale. They were the biggest merchant guild on the Central Continent, with a mysterious force behind them. Rare and precious treasures were countless as long as one had sufficient spirit stones. Even the Buddhist relics from the Buddhist Kingdom, holy bones from the Demon Region, and immortal fruits, which only existed in the legends, could be bought.

If anyone dared to owe the Luodi Merchant Guild or thought that they could be lucky enough to not get caught for stealing from the merchant guild, they should think twice as numerous formidable cultivators had vanished without a trace before.

Legend had it that there was a formidable cultivator called “Thief King” who was well-versed in the Dao of space. Stealing other people’s storage space was as effortless as taking something out from his own pocket. Distance was just a string of meaningless numbers to him. A single stride of his could pass mountains and rivers, traveling from the extreme west to the extreme north of the Central Continent. Even the belongings of Transcendent Tribulation experts were not spared from the Thief King.

However, there was an unspoken rule within the stealing community—never steal from the Luodi Merchant Guild.

Initially, the Thief King adhered to the ancestral rules for stealing and didn’t engage in any interactions with the Luodi Merchant Guild. As his reputation grew, countless successful experts joined hands to hunt him down, but they couldn't locate him at all. This got to his head, and he began to feel that there wasn’t much substance to the cultivation experts. Thinking that he himself had already surpassed the ancestors of thieves, he felt that there was no need for him to follow those rigid ancestral rules anymore.

He arrogantly announced that he would be robbing the Luodi Merchant Guild’s treasure tonight.

Everyone thought that there were two possible outcomes—either the Thief King stealthily stole the treasure with his mysterious Dao of Space or a conflict within the merchant guild broke out and the Thief King would have to battle the personage behind the merchant guild.

Out of everyone’s expectations, nothing happened that night. The Thief King never appeared again.

Lu Yang only had to awkwardly hold on for a bit. When it was time to jump off the boat, the others didn’t have spare time to continue staring at him.

Everyone opened their umbrellas and leaped off one by one. Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye followed.

This chapter is updated by freēwēbnovel.com.

High up in the sky, several people held on to their open umbrellas, appearing like small sesame seeds from a distance. Unlike the others, Lu Yang pulled the rope on his back. With a loud sound, the parachute opened, making Lu Yang stand out against the backdrop of the sky.

Normally, Lu Yang would be very nervous at such high altitudes, but he didn’t have the chance to think about it.

It was too embarrassing.

Fortunately, everyone was headed for different destinations. Only Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye were going to Taiping Village.

As soon as they arrived, they were warmly welcomed by the village chief, as if he had known about their arrival. “Master immortals, you’re finally here. The way you jumped off from the flying vessel was truly extraordinary.”

Lu Yang had his mouth open, but he ended up not asking why the village chief knew when they would arrive.

“I’m Lu Yang, and she’s Tao Yaoye. Both of us are disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. The description of the demon bird was not very detailed. Please provide us with more information.”

The village chief had originally prepared a welcoming banquet to have some drinks and give them some local specialties before going into details about the demon bird. This was the usual protocol when requesting someone up there to help. He didn’t expect Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye to be so swift and decisive and was pleasantly surprised, inwardly praising them. As expected of immortal sect disciples.

Tao Yaoye sized up the village chief. Advanced Qi Training cultivation. He didn’t set his foundation well in his early years, so there are many impurities in his spirit power with no chance to reach the Foundation Establishment Stage. He can be considered an ordinary cultivator.

Speaking of the demon bird, the village chief became depressed. There were not many outsiders in Taiping Village in the first place. Now that word of the demon bird had spread through the nearby areas, even traveling merchants weren’t willing to come near. He had reported the situation to Quhe Commandery, but they lacked manpower. Since the demon bird didn’t harm anyone, they simply said to wait until they had the capacity to dispatch someone to Taiping Village.

Twenty days had passed since.

“It began around twenty days ago. The tailor surnamed Feng ran out onto the streets shouting that a big, powerful man-eating demon had invaded his house. The villagers were frightened. A man-eating demon was not a small matter. We only have roughly thirty cultivators here in Taiping Village. Among them, my cultivation is the highest, and I am also the village chief, so Feng brought the villagers to look for me together.

“Before dealing with the demon, I had asked Feng, ‘You said that the big demon eats people. Who has it eaten?’”

Demons that had eaten people were far more dangerous than those that had not. Humans were beings born intelligent, and demons who had consumed them were addicted to this taste. They would then eat a second human, a third one...becoming a scourge.

“Feng said he doesn’t know who the big demon has eaten, but that demon can speak. It’s definitely because it has eaten humans before.”

There were indeed rumors among the people that demons could speak human words and transform into human form after eating people. However, they were just unfounded tales. How could it be so easy for demons to cultivate? For a demon to speak human words, it must refine the bone in its throat, and that would take at least the Advanced Qi Training Stage.

“Feng said that the demon was colorful. He initially thought that it was a bird that had gotten lost in the mountain forest. The demon bird had sat behind him and watched him sew clothes without moving. All of a sudden, it began speaking and gave Feng a scare, and he quickly ran out of the store.

“Feng couldn’t provide any more useful information, so I asked them to wait from a distance while I secretly approached the place. That was when I saw the demon bird.

“The demon bird’s feathers were brightly colored and lustrous, and around its eyes was a distinct red color. It was obvious at a glance that it wasn’t an ordinary bird. How could an ordinary bird dare to look so ostentatious?

“The demon bird opened its mouth and asked me, ‘Who are you? Where is Zhang Guanjia?’ Its tone was quite urgent.

“I didn’t understand. Zhang Guanjia is a cultivator in our village. He is at the Level Three Qi Training Stage and has an ordinary cultivation. Why would he have anything to do with a demonic beast?

“Back then, I tried my best to let myself relax and look like I was not a threat. Then, I politely asked, ‘Demon King, may I know why you are looking for Zhang Guanjia?’

“The demon bird didn’t answer. It flapped its wings and left the tailor shop.

“Ever since then, the demon bird has been flying around Taiping Village, eating grains from the fields and speaking human words. Although it doesn’t eat people, how could normal humans not be scared? That is why everyone has been living in fear during this period of time. They are afraid that the demon bird will suddenly unleash its ferocious side and devour them all.”

Lu Yang asked, “Have you fought the demon bird? How strong is it?”

The village chief shook his head. “The demon bird is always in the sky, elusive and hard to track. Moreover, I can’t see through the demon bird’s cultivation, which means that its cultivation is at least my level, Level Seven Qi Training. Since the demon bird doesn’t have intentions of harming people now, I’m worried that I may accidentally make things worse and provoke it by fighting it.”

Lu Yang nodded. That’s reasonable.

Chapter 19: The True Form of The Demon Bird!

Tao Yaoye asked, “Since the demon bird is looking for Zhang Guanjia, have you tried letting them meet?”

The village chief let out a long sigh. “We don’t need to let them meet. A few days ago, the demon bird went directly to Zhang Guanjia’s house and shouted ‘Monster! Monster!’ at him. Then, it flew out of the window and we don’t know where it went afterward.

“Just when we were at a loss of what to do, master immortals, you both came.”

Tao Yaoye was pensive for a moment before guessing, “Is Zhang Guanjia a demon? Perhaps the demon bird was warning you to be careful of Zhang Guanjia?”

There were also demons that were benevolent. They would sometimes transform into human form or reveal their true form to warn humans of calamities. The Great Demon King Zhu Yan was one example. In folklore, wherever Zhu Yan went, it would signify serious turmoil. As such, Zhu Yan was seen as an ominous demon beast.

After learning of the matter, the immortal sects had a completely different take. It was not Zhu Yan that had brought upon disaster. Instead, Zhu Yan had foreseen the chaos and specially traveled to the Central Continent from the Demon Region to inform the humans purely out of goodwill.

Of course, Zhu Yan was partly to blame for the people’s misunderstanding toward him—he had a phobia of people and dared not speak. His ferocious facial features also didn’t help his cause. It was hard for people to believe that he was a benevolent demon beast.

Maybe this demon bird is the same. It is here to inform the people of Taiping Village that Zhang Guanjia is a shapeshifting great demon.

The village chief was put on the spot. I don’t want to refute this beautiful fairy-like immortal, but I also can’t ignore the facts and say that Zhang Guanjia is a demon.

“Zhang Guanjia grew up in Taiping Village. All the old people can attest to that. He also has two younger brothers, Zhang Guanyi and Zhang Guanbing.[1] The three brothers are very close. He now runs a private school and teaches children Confucianism and cultivation. He’s one of the few teachers here in Taiping Village.

“To say that he is a demon...”

Tao Yaoye disagreed with the village chief. “Demons have long lives. Many long-lived types will stay in a certain place for decades and let themselves age, blending in with humans. One day, when they’ve seen enough of the scenery, they’ll feign their death and leave their graves. Then, they’ll go to a new place and start anew.”

The village chief opened his mouth, but no words came out as he felt that he wasn’t as knowledgeable as Tao Yaoye.

Lu Yang shook his head, pointing out the loopholes in Tao Yaoye’s speculation. “If Zhang Guanjia were a demon, that would mean that he is a shapeshifting great demon. How could a demon like that tolerate a little demon bird running its mouth off? It would have been killed by Zhang Guanjia before it even had a chance to speak.”

Tao Yaoye didn’t object. What Lu Yang said was indeed true.

Lu Yang stood up. “That said, we still have to meet with Zhang Guanjia.”

The village chief quickly led the way. “This way, please, master immortals.”

On the way, Lu Yang corrected the village chief’s way of address. “All of us are cultivators with the goal of becoming an immortal. Although we are currently only at the Foundation Establishment Stage, even venerable ones that are at the Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation stages and are closest to becoming immortals are not qualified to be addressed as master immortals.

“You may address us as Daoists.”

The village chief smiled obsequiously. He didn’t dare to treat Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye as ordinary Foundation Establishment cultivators. Not even one in ten could ascend to the Golden Core Stage, but that was for ordinary cultivators. The disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect were sure to advance to the Golden Core Stage. Their achievements in the future would be beyond his imagination.

“Isn’t that because no one has ascended to an immortal? There are only legends.”

Lu Yang merely smiled and said nothing more.

Soon, the three arrived at Zhang Guanjia’s house.

“Old Zhang, you have visitors. Open the door.”

The door creaked slightly open, revealing the expressionless Zhang Guanjia standing behind.

“Let me introduce, these two are disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. They have come to help us eliminate the demon bird.”

Hearing the name “Dao-Seeking Sect,” there was finally a change in Zhang Guanjia’s expression. He protested helplessly, “I’m really not a demon. You can’t simply believe whatever the demon bird says. It even shouted ‘patron, come and play.’[2] Why don’t you find a few patrons to play with the bird?”

The village chief smiled awkwardly. “We’re just touring around and happened to come by here.” The village chief was recognized for being diligent in his work. He had already spoken this much, so Zhang Guanjia could only open the door and invite them in.

Zhang Guanjia’s house consisted of the standard rooms along with a gatehouse and courtyard. As he was the only one living inside, it appeared empty. He was past forty and unmarried.

Their conversation still revolved around the demon bird, so Zhang Guanjia was not in a good mood. “I have never seen that demon bird before. Who the hell knows why it called my name? I’ve never left Taiping Village my whole life. The furthest place I’ve ever been to is Quhe Commandery. Where would I meet a demon bird?

“Every day, there will be students asking me, ‘Teacher, teacher, are you a demon?’ There are even students afraid that I will eat them up, and they will finish their homework on time every day!

“Even a neighbor came looking for me, saying that he has an enemy at the Foundation Establishment Stage in Quhe Commandery. He asked whether I could secretly kill the other party and that the price could be negotiated!” Zhang Guanjia shared his story through clenched teeth. He wished he could have a fight to the death with the demon bird just so that he could clear his name.

I’m just an ordinary person, but just because the demon bird said so, I’m now suddenly a demon? That’s totally unreasonable!

After the discussion, the three still didn’t obtain any useful information. They merely listened to Zhang Guanjia complain for four hours about how the demon bird had disrupted his life.

Fortunately, Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye hurriedly expressed that they must exterminate the demon bird and return justice to Zhang Guanjia. Only then was he satisfied and stopped grumbling.

“The demon bird is here again!” someone outside the house yelled as they fled for their lives.

Hearing the commotion, Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye immediately cast away their leisurely attitudes. Carrying their magical treasures, they left the house to confront the demon bird.

“Daoists, you must be careful!” The village chief got the villagers to stay quiet and move to a place further away from where the demon bird was sighted.

Lu Yang gripped the hilt of his sword. As soon as the demon bird had even the tiniest bit of intention to attack the people, it would be faced with a sudden cold glimmer and be sliced into half.

Tao Yaoye took out her red paper umbrella. This was her life-bound magical treasure—the Thousand Illusion Umbrella.

Lu Yang cautiously gestured that he would scout ahead, and Tao Yaoye nodded. The demon bird was currently in a villager’s house. Like a cat, Lu Yang made no noise as he moved up on his prey. He was on full alert, his muscles tensed as he prepared to pull out his sword for a battle any moment.

The most optimistic outcome is that the demon bird is only at the Level Seven Qi Training Stage. The worst case scenario is that it turns out to be an advanced Foundation Establishment demon. Fighting it wouldn’t be easy.

Finally, he saw the demon bird that had plagued Taiping Village for twenty days.

Its dark green feathers were vibrant and lustrous. Spanning from the corner of its eyes to its neck were large patches of red. The combination of red and green made it especially striking. Lu Yang could tell the demon bird’s origin at one glance.

It had come from the depths of the woods.

It fed on figs and berries.

It was adept at mimicking human speech.

This was a parrot.

Chapter 20: The Shang Family

Reality had proven that speaking human words didn’t necessarily mean they were demon beasts; they might just be parrots.

“How is this a demon bird?!” Lu Yang was furious. A suction power appeared in his palm, pulling the parrot over. It didn’t even have time to react until it was caught.

The village chief could also do the same, but he hadn’t dared to because he thought that it was some kind of demon beast at the Qi Training or Foundation Establishment stage.

“Demon beast! There’s a demon beast!” The parrot screeched non-stop.

Hearing the commotion inside the room, Tao Yaoye hurriedly rushed over. Upon witnessing the actual situation, her mood wasn’t that much different from Lu Yang’s.

Completing the mission is a good thing. Not having to fight is also a good thing. But the problem is that we came all the way from the Dao-Seeking Sect and rode the flying vessel for three days just to capture a parrot?

How are we going to write the mission report? We’ll only be laughing stock if word gets out.

The people in Taiping Village were not knowledgeable enough to recognize birds from the rainforest, but it was basic knowledge for everyone in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“As expected of you, Daoists! You captured the demon bird so effortlessly!” the village chief and other villagers praised Lu Yang one after another, lauding his high cultivation.

The two of them had no choice but to patiently explain to the people that the bird was actually very ordinary. It was simply not common in the northern region of the continent.

“This parrot, also what all of you call a demon bird, is most proficient in mimicking human speech.”

“Mimicking human speech, mimicking human speech.” The parrot kept screeching until Lu Yang had to pinch its beak close before continuing to explain, “It shouted that Zhang Guanjia is a demon not because it itself wanted to. Tailor Feng had shouted ‘demon,’ and it learned from him. When it bumped into Zhang Guanjia, it simply repeated the term.”

Zhang Guanjia heaved a sigh of relief. As expected of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s disciples. My grievances are cleared right after they arrived.

“By the same logic, when it shouted, ‘Who are you? Where is Zhang Guanjia?’ it also didn’t understand the meaning of the sentence. It had simply learned it from somewhere else and repeated it meaninglessly.”

“This damned bird! Let me kill it.” Zhang Guanjia couldn’t contain his anger.

Lu Yang raised his hand and stopped Zhang Guanjia. “This place is half a continent away from the rainforest. This parrot definitely didn’t fly here by itself but was instead brought here by someone. Unless someone was bored enough to cross half a continent just to bring this rare yet non-useful parrot, only the Luodi Merchant Guild would do such a thing. Is there a Luodi Merchant Guild in this area?”

The village chief shook his head. “A merchant guild wouldn’t set up a branch in a poor, remote, and small place like ours, but there is one in Quhe Commandery. It is located in the most bustling region with an endless flow of traffic. Maybe after someone bought the parrot from the merchant guild, it accidentally escaped.”

It is naturally impossible for the parrot to have directly escaped from the Luodi Merchant Guild.

Lu Yang pressed on, “This bird has been circling around Taiping Village for the past twenty days instead of heading somewhere else. Perhaps its owner is right here. What do you think, Village Chief?”

It took the village chief quite a while before replying, “The villagers all know about the demon bird. If there is really anyone who doesn’t know, it would be the Shang Family to the east. The Shang Family rarely goes out and is reluctant to interact with others. I heard that it’s because the family head is also a cultivator. When he was young, he experienced some setbacks and his cultivation regressed tremendously. Since then, he has lost his will to cultivate and lives here reclusively.

“The Shang Family is also quite wealthy. They are the richest in this place. It is possible for them to have bought the demon bird from the Luodi Merchant Guild.”

“If that’s the case, let’s go and ask the Shang Family.”

Updated from freewёbnoνel.com.

Taiping Village wasn’t huge, so the trio and one bird soon arrived at the Shang Family’s entrance. After knocking on the door, someone quickly came to open it for them. It was a middle-aged man with a mustache that stuck out on both ends, and he was dressed in scholarly robes.

“Oh, it’s you, Village Chief. May I know who these two are so that I can report to the patriarch?” the mustached man asked.

Still pinching the parrot’s wings, Lu Yang looked like he was preparing to slaughter a rooster while doing house visits during the New Year. “We found this parrot by chance. After asking around, we thought that it may belong to the Shang Family, so we have specially come to ask.”

The mustached man noticed Tao Yaoye first and was surprised. He had never seen a woman as beautiful as Tao Yaoye.

Then, he turned to the green parrot, showing an elated smile. “I see, many thanks to you two young heroes. This should be our young miss’ parrot. Ever since she lost her parrot, she has been in low spirits, which makes things difficult for us servants. She would be overjoyed if she learns that the parrot has been found.”

The village chief leaned in and whispered, “He’s the Shang Family’s steward and his surname is Zhang. He’s always the one opening the door when I come to the Shang Family.”

Steward Zhang hastily went inside to report, and he soon came back with a response. “The patriarch invites you three inside.”

They entered through the screen door[1], passed through the outer courtyard and walked from the secondary door to the corridor then finally the main room. Only then did they see the Shang Family’s head.

The Shang Family’s head had a plump physique, though his gloomy expression kept others at a distance. However, they could still tell that he was rather happy to see the village chief. “Old Brother Huang, long time no see.” The village chief’s surname was Huang.

The two cupped their fists and greeted each other.

Family Head Shang examined the parrot for a bit and nodded. “Mmm, this is indeed the parrot my daughter bought from the Luodi Merchant Guild in the commandery. At that time, I thought that this bird wouldn’t be worth much, yet the merchant guild demanded an exorbitant price. My daughter insisted on buying it, so I could only follow her wishes.”

“Steward Zhang, take these two young heroes to see Xiaoyuan.”

“Yes, Patriarch.”

Steward Zhang gestured for them to proceed and called a maidservant to serve tea to Family Head Shang and Village Chief Huang.

On the way, Tao Yaoye casually asked, “Steward Zhang, how long have you been with the Shang Family?”

Steward Zhang replied in a respectful tone, “The patriarch saved me when he was on his way to seclusion. Ever since then, I have been serving him. Let me think, it has been twenty years now. Young Miss wasn’t even born then.”

“That means that Young Miss Shang has a rather good relationship with you.”

“To be honest, I watched Young Miss grow up. I have no children, so I treated her as my own daughter. It pains me to see her so dejected every day.”

Lu Yang suddenly asked, “Were you around when the parrot went missing?”

Steward Zhang sighed, his voice laced with reproach. “At the time, I got distracted for a bit and didn’t notice the parrot flying away. If only I had paid more attention then, Young Miss wouldn’t be so sad now. It was a dereliction of duty on my part.”

Lu Yang simply replied, “Oh.”

Steward Zhang knocked three times and calmly said, “Young Miss, your missing parrot has been found by two young heroes wandering the jianghu. They have brought the parrot here.”

A voice answered from within the room. “Let them in then.”

“Understood.”

Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye opened the door. Young Miss Shang was leaning against the window while reading a book quietly. The evening sunlight fell on her hair, painting a picturesque scene where time seemed to have come to a stop.

Countless young men in Taiping Village were infatuated with Young Miss Shang.

Lu Yang reminded kindly, “Reading under the sunlight, especially at sunset, is bad for your eyes. You should light a candle. It’s not like your father is short of money.”

Chapter 21: Staying Overnight
