The corners of Young Miss Shang’s eyes twitched. She closed the book and stood up to receive the two, speaking in an icy voice. “Thank you for bringing Little Green back. I’m Shang Yuan.”

As if Shang Yuan was its savior, the parrot flapped its wings to escape from Lu Yang. Lu Yang let go, allowing the parrot to fly freely in the room.

“Do be careful next time. Fortunately, this parrot kept flying around Taiping Village. Had it flown somewhere else, it would have been nigh impossible to find it.”

Shang Yuan noticed that Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye were dressed in refined attire. It was obvious to her at one glance that the two were experienced young heroes upholding justice in the jianghu.

Their attire had actually been recommended to them by the Great Mission Hall. They claimed that the two could pass off as young heroes who had wandered the jianghu for a long time.

Shang Yuan’s attitude was somewhat distant. It was unclear if it was due to her personality or other reasons. “Now that Little Green is back, you two may leave.”

Tao Yaoye frowned slightly, displeased with the young miss's attitude.

Lu Yang pretended to not have heard her attempt at chasing them away. He cheerfully said, “Come on, let’s chat. The Shang Family is quite welcoming to us. Maybe they would even ask us to stay overnight.”

Shang Yuan sneered. “Just because the Shang Family welcomes you, it doesn’t mean that I welcome you. You should leave quickly. Best is if you leave Taiping Village.”

“It’s not like there are monsters here in Taiping Village. Why should we leave? Besides, you also haven’t left the Shang Estate for a long time. Don’t you want to hear us share stories about the outside world?”

Shang Yuan was taken aback by Lu Yang’s words, and her tone softened. “Where are you two from? I haven’t left the house for the past month. Can you tell me about your experiences in the jianghu?”

Lu Yang began unhurriedly, “We are from the Dao-Seeking Sect, one of the Great Five Immortal Sects. Both of our cultivation are at the Foundation Establishment Stage. We came to Taiping Village because we heard that there was a demon bird causing a disturbance...” His voice was gentle, making him a good storyteller.

Upon hearing that the two were at the Foundation Establishment Stage, a trace of joy flashed past Shang Yuan’s eyes.

The three chatted for a while. Shang Yuan was attracted to the life of cultivators traveling by land as described by Lu Yang. She was inspired to also venture outside to carve out her own path while witnessing the vast world.

“I want to cultivate, but my dad doesn’t allow me to. He says that cultivation is too dangerous. Had he not gotten lucky when exploring an ancient tomb, he would have long died. I’ve asked him about his experience many times, but he refuses to tell me,” Shang Yuan said angrily. She enjoyed hearing about interesting and strange stories, yet her own father wasn’t willing to tell her despite having first-hand experience.

Lu Yang sighed inwardly. Looks like Family Head Shang is also someone with a story.

“What’s Family Head Shang’s cultivation?”

Reminded of her father’s boastful expression, Shang Yuan rolled her eyes. “Listening to him blow his trumpet, he used to be Level Nine Qi Training. However, he encountered a disaster and was lucky to survive. Despite that, his cultivation regressed drastically to Level Four or Level Five Qi Training.”

Tao Yaoye comforted her, “That’s still not too bad. There aren’t many cultivators in Taiping Village. The village chief who is the strongest is only at the Level Seven Qi Training Stage. Level Four or Five Qi Training is good enough for a comfortable life, and that’s not even mentioning that Family Head Shang still has some foundation here.”

Shang Yuan lamented, “But I don’t want to be confined to just Quhe Commandery. I want to travel the jianghu and see this magnificent and intriguing world. We are of similar age, yet you are already a Foundation Establishment cultivator while I’m not even at the Qi Training Stage.”

Tao Yaoye was about to advise her when Steward Zhang knocked on the door. “Young Miss, it’s time for dinner. Young heroes, the patriarch specifically instructed that since it’s late, you may have a meal and stay for the night before leaving. The patriarch, matriarch, and Village Chief Huang are already waiting for you all.”

“Got it, we’ll be right there,” Lu Yang replied.

Tao Yaoye originally wanted to decline, but Lu Yang stopped her. “Look, I’ve already told you that the Shang Family is hospitable and will let us stay overnight. How can you not accept their kindness?”

~~~

At the dining table, Family Head Shang was seated in the main seat. He was engrossed in a conversation with Village Chief Huang. The others were enjoying their meal. Although it couldn’t compare to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s food, it was still considered delicious. Throughout the meal, Steward Zhang and the maidservants stood at the side respectfully and attended to them.

After the satisfactory meal, Village Chief Huang went back while Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye stayed for the night in the east wing, with only a wall separating their rooms. Tao Yaoye didn’t want to sleep there because she was picky about her bed. Apart from her bed in the Dao-Seeking Sect where she could fall asleep as soon as she lay down, she took a very long time to fall asleep in other places. She knew that it wasn’t a good habit since it was common for cultivators to sleep in the open, but her attempts at changing this habit hadn’t succeeded yet.

“Senior Brother Lu, you can really fall asleep anywhere,” Tao Yaoye mumbled to herself. For some reason, she chuckled softly before yawning. “I’m going to bed early tonight. Looks like I can get a good sleep...”

Tao Yaoye suddenly realized, “Something’s wrong! Someone poisoned us!” She turned to grab her Thousand Illusion Umbrella to open a barrier but discovered that the flow of spirit energy in her body was sluggish and hard to mobilize.

She was shocked. Someone actually poisoned us without me noticing! Who is it? This is a poison targeted at cultivators. Since the other party still dared to act despite knowing that we are cultivators, they must also be one. There are only a few people in the Shang Family. Other than Family Head Shang, I didn’t sense anyone else being a cultivator.

Is it Family Head Shang?

Or is there a higher-level cultivator that I’m not able to detect?

How’s Senior Brother Lu doing?

A string of questions overcame Tao Yaoye’s mind in an instant. Before she even had time to think, she heard light footsteps from outside the room.

The door opened.

Steward Zhang slowly marched in, smiling excitedly and cruelly.

“It’s you!” Tao Yaoye widened her eyes, not expecting his revelation. Her heart sank. I couldn’t tell that Steward Zhang is a cultivator, which means that his cultivation is higher than mine.

In Steward Zhang’s hand was a skinning knife. Even from five steps away, Tao Yaoye could feel the thick grudge emanating from it. I wonder how many people died under this knife to have such heavy resentment overflowing from it.

Moonlight shone on the blade, making it gleam brightly.

Steward Zhang licked his lips as he watched Tao Yaoye struggle yet to no avail, like a predator eyeing a ferocious prey that had fallen into a trap. “What beautiful skin. I have never seen such fair and fine skin.

“I know you’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect, and their influence extends far and wide, so killing you will be very troublesome. How could a minor character like me dare to provoke them?” Saliva was drooling from the corners of Steward Zhang’s mouth, and he wiped them off as he continued, “But your skin is simply too beautiful that I couldn’t resist taking the risk. Furthermore, you willingly stayed behind to eat at the Shang Family. With such a perfect opportunity to poison you, I couldn’t pass it up.”

There was poison in the dinner!

Seeing that Tao Yaoye had not given up, Steward Zhang exhorted her thoughtfully, “Don’t struggle anymore. Even if you hadn’t been poisoned, you’re still not my match. You’ve just reached Foundation Establishment while I’m at Advanced Foundation Establishment.”

That said, Steward Zhang didn’t let his guard down. I can’t treat a Foundation Establishment cultivator from the Dao-Seeking Sect as just an ordinary one!

He had said those words just to discourage Tao Yaoye from resisting. The more she resisted, the tighter the skin would be, and the harder it would be to peel the skin. This was based on his experience.

“Relax, it’ll just hurt for a moment. You’ll stop being scared soon.” Steward Zhang licked his skinning knife as he approached Tao Yaoye.

Suddenly, Tao Yaoye sprang up, her spirit energy flowing without obstruction. She smashed the Thousand Illusion Umbrella into Steward Zhang’s face. Just when Steward Zhang thought that victory was in his grasp, he was caught off guard.

“Why aren’t you poisoned?!”

Chapter 22: Who Said There’s No Poison Targeted At Skin?

After getting smashed in the face, Steward Zhang used the momentum to spin and reduce the impact. He still couldn’t register what had just happened. The poison he used on Tao Yaoye was supposed to be his proud masterpiece. He had lost count of how many cultivators died with grievances because of it.

How could it possibly fail?

Tao Yaoye didn’t answer. After confirming that the parrot did belong to Young Miss Shang, she had become more vigilant. Everyone in the village knew about the talking demon bird flying around. Had the Shang Family dispatched someone to look for it, they would have found the parrot easily, and none of these events afterward would have happened.

Since the Shang Family’s actions defied common logic, something was definitely amiss!

In addition, Young Miss Shang’s aloof attitude didn’t seem like she was chasing them away but rather warning them that there was danger in the Shang Family—she was urging them to quickly escape.

A lazy voice came from behind, answering in Tao Yaoye’s stead, “A compulsory introductory lesson in the Dao-Seeking Sect is One Thousand Eight Hundred Common Poisons and Cures. Do you want to take a look?”

Steward Zhang’s supposed proud masterpiece was just a joke in front of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Regardless of how skilled he was at crafting poisons, could they be stronger than the ones at the Pill Cauldron Peak?

Steward Zhang abruptly turned back and saw Lu Yang leaning against the door frame, hugging his ancient sword and smiling at him.

It dawned upon Steward Zhang. Tao Yaoye is not the prey.

I am.

He asked in a deep voice, “How did you find me out?” He didn’t think that he had given himself away. The entire Shang Family is under my control. No one leaked any secrets.

When Shang Yuan and Lu Yang were chatting inside the room, he was worried that he would be discovered if he extended his spiritual consciousness, so he chose to eavesdrop instead. That was how he learned that Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye were disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Shang Yuan didn’t reveal my identity then either.

Steward Zhang had excellent hearing. Even if they had written or drawn something, it wouldn’t have escaped his ears.

Lu Yang smiled. “Do you know what the parrot said in the village?”

“What did it say?”

“It said, ‘Who are you? Where is Zhang Guanjia?’

“Initially, we thought that the parrot was looking for Zhang Guanjia. However, we realized afterward that it was simply repeating what it had heard. That got me wondering. Zhang Guanjia didn’t wander the jianghu, so how did the parrot hear this sentence?

“Could there be a possibility that the parrot wasn’t saying ‘Who are you? Where is Zhang Guanjia?’ but instead ‘Who are you? Where is Steward Zhang[1]?’”

Lu Yang came up with a plausible scenario.

Twenty days ago, Young Miss Shang had accidentally discovered that Steward Zhang had been replaced by someone else, and she fearfully shouted, ‘Who are you? Where is Steward Zhang?’ Afterward, she knocked the bird rack and startled the parrot, causing it to fly away. This was the last sentence the parrot heard, so be it in the tailor shop or with Village Chief Huang, the parrot repeated this sentence.

Perhaps the parrot’s pronunciation was unclear, or perhaps it was Village Chief Huang's first reaction to associate it with Zhang Guanjia, someone he interacted with a lot, in any case, the parrot’s sentence became “Who are you? Where is Zhang Guanjia?”

Steward Zhang was burning with rage inside. I didn’t expect that silly bird that could only mimic others to be the one ruining my plan. If I had known, I would’ve slaughtered it from the start!

However, it wasn’t Steward Zhang’s first day in the jianghu. Despite being surrounded by the two, he laughed heartily. “I’m at Advanced Foundation Establishment. If I want to escape, do you think you can stop me?”

Tao Yaoye was a little anxious. If Steward Zhang escapes, we can only report to the sect and get our senior brothers and sisters to handle it. But whether they’re able to track him down is another story.

This made Tao Yaoye slightly ashamed. She had only completed two missions, and she was already encountering trouble with the third.

On the other hand, Lu Yang was as composed as usual, making Steward Zhang uneasy. “Did it not cross your mind that since you can poison us, we can also poison you?”

Steward Zhang relaxed and scoffed, “I thought it was something serious. Poison? What use would that be against me?”

Right as he said that, his skin suddenly became loose, as if he was molting. The skin separated from the flesh, and the shedded skin formed a complete human figure. It stood in the middle of the room, its organs hollow, and it stared right at Tao Yaoye eerily. The body with the skin detached fell to the ground with a thud.

Painted Skin[2] Ghost.

Tao Yaoye’s expression grew grave. She now understood why Steward Zhang mentioned that poison was no use against him. Poison had always been targeted at the body, specifically the organs, muscles, and meridians. However Steward Zhang was a Painted Skin Ghost, his true form just a skin. Who would poison the skin?

Besides, why would there be poison specifically for the skin? At the very least, Steward Zhang had not heard of it before.

But Lu Yang knew.

Just as Steward Zhang was about to flaunt his own body, to his horror, he saw blisters the size of mung beans forming on his legs as layers and layers of skin peeled off. The blisters swelled and were itchy, bursting at the slightest scratch. All Steward Zhang did was rub against the floor a few times, and yellow pus was already oozing out.

“What...what is this?!” Fear began to creep into Steward Zhang’s voice. He had never encountered something like this before. After all, when was he ever poisoned?

“Athlete’s foot.”

“What?” Steward Zhang thought he had heard wrong.

“You thought I was just making small talk with you all this while? No! I was waiting for your disease to act up.

I knew you would come looking for Tao Yaoye, so for that, I specially left poison that could trigger athlete’s foot in this room!”

Steward Zhang’s face was white.

Tao Yaoye’s face was black.

Lu Yang grinned menacingly as he approached Steward Zhang step by step, causing the latter to retreat until he fell to the ground on his bottom.

“You...how did you know that I’m a Painted Skin Ghost?!”

If he hadn’t known that I’m a Painted Skin Ghost, then how could he have had such a specific poison?!

Most importantly, I’ve never heard of any Painted Skin Ghost getting athlete’s foot!

Both his feet were itching so badly that it almost drove him mad. He even considered chopping his feet off. He was forced to expend the majority of his energy and power to suppress the poison, making escape impossible.

Suddenly, Steward Zhang’s vision blurred for a bit, and Lu Yang had vanished into thin air.

“How is that possible?!” Steward Zhang’s eyes widened. Lu Yang just reached Foundation Establishment. No matter how skilled he is with his movement techniques, he can’t possibly escape my eyes.

“It’s an illusion!” Steward Zhang suddenly realized and quickly tried to roll away.

However, it was too late. A cold light appeared as swift as lightning, and a fine line started from Steward Zhang’s forehead and ended at his groin. Lu Yang sheathed his sword.

Steward Zhang had been sliced into half, the cut as smooth as a mirror.

“Not bad.” Lu Yang gave Tao Yaoye a thumbs up.

Earlier on, Tao Yaoye had used the Thousand Illusion Umbrella to trap Steward Zhang in an illusion. The illusion wasn’t impeccable; based on Steward Zhang’s many years of experience in the jianghu, he would only be dazed for a moment before seeing through it.

However, what Lu Yang needed was exactly this moment of confusion. He drew his sword, slashed it vertically and sheathed it in one fluid motion.

Painted Skin Ghosts were known for their trickery and queerness, not defense, while sword cultivators were known to be the strongest in offense. Just getting caught off guard for a moment prevented him from having the time to counter, so the result of the battle was naturally decided in one move with no uncertainty!

As soon as Lu Yang had seen through the Painted Skin Ghost’s identity, its advantage was completely gone.

The Painted Skin Ghost stared at Lu Yang in disbelief, mouthing words that seemed to ask, “How did you recognize my true form?”

Tao Yaoye looked toward Lu Yang; she also wanted to know the answer.

Lu Yang didn’t reply to him, simply swinging his sword again and slicing the Painted Skin Ghost into four pieces. He poured some spirit wine and set them on fire. The pained howls of the Painted Skin Ghost were eventually reduced to ashes.

Who knows if this ghost has any tricks left up its sleeve? Better to kill it first then slowly explain.

Chapter 23: Family Head Shang’s Past

“How did you figure out that he was a Painted Skin Ghost?” Tao Yaoye asked the burning question Steward Zhang never found the answer to even until he died.

Lu Yang cleaned up the aftermath and used a broom to sweep the Painted Skin Ghost’s ashes into a small clump. Taking the hint, Tao Yaoye also took out a bamboo winnowing dustpan [1] to collect them.

“It’s simple. Think back to what the parrot said. ‘Who are you? Where is Steward Zhang?’ After we met Shang Yuan, she deliberately chased us away because she wanted us to stay away from the Shang Family. This implied that the current Steward Zhang was no longer the one Young Miss Shang knew and was also extremely dangerous.

“Thus, there are three possible reasons Steward Zhang was replaced.

“First, Steward Zhang was possessed. But why would an old monster possessing others stay in the Shang Family for so long? If it were me, the first thing I’d do after possessing the person would be to leave Taiping Village and find a favorable place with good feng shui to continue cultivating. Besides, Steward Zhang’s cultivation isn’t worth much mention. Possessing Family Head Shang instead would be more beneficial.” Lu Yang tried to put himself in another’s shoes.

“Second, someone was disguised as Steward Zhang. But this doesn’t make sense either. There is nothing valuable in the Shang Family. Why pretend to be Steward Zhang? It can’t be that he has a fetish for serving others, right? Even if there is something valuable in the Shang Family, couldn’t he have just snatched it? With his Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivation, no one would care even if he crawls through Taiping Village.

“The third possibility is that he was a Painted Skin Ghost. Painted Skin Ghosts love collecting human skin and disguising as humans, assuming their identities and continuing to live among humans.”

Painted Skin Ghosts were humans when they were alive and ghosts when they were dead. They could be considered as a type of ghost cultivators. Most ghost cultivators faced some psychological issues. For example, Painted Skin Ghosts hate having their identities exposed. They would try their best to convince themselves that they were human, speaking and acting like humans. When they got bored of it, they would switch to another skin and begin a new life under another identity, repeating this cycle.

Lu Yang’s reasoning was logical and well-supported, making Tao Yaoye look at him with admiration. I can’t see any traces of the timid Senior Brother Lu on the flying vessel. Despite us possessing the same amount of knowledge, I couldn’t come up with as many ideas so quickly. This is a difference in our mental agility.

“Keep the ashes well. They’re proof that we’ve completed the mission.” Lu Yang took out two white porcelain bottles that were as tall as his palm and stored the ashes in them.

The Painted Skin Ghost is an extension of the mission, so it can be considered as a part of the mission. The rewards for killing a Painted Skin Ghost will definitely be more than finding a parrot.

There were sounds of running footsteps from outside the room, and they stopped outside the door, as if several people had been jolted awake by a nightmare and come to the east wing to check on the situation but dared not enter.

It was not hard to guess the identity of the person behind the door. Lu Yang laughed resoundingly, “Family Head Shang, come in. I have already slain the Painted Skin Ghost. It’s very safe here.”

Bang! Family Head Shang pushed open the wooden door with the matriarch, young miss, and servants standing behind him. All twelve of them wore a relieved expression as if they had just cheated death.

“Master immortals, thank you for slaying the Painted Skin Ghost and saving all twelve lives of the Shang Family!” Family Head Shang knelt with a thud, followed by everyone else behind him.

As the Painted Skin Ghost ghost was temperamental, after it got tired of a steward’s identity, it would very likely slaughter everyone in the Shang Family!

“Family Head Shang, you exaggerate. Exterminating demons and devils and upholding justice have always been what we, disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect, are supposed to do.” Lu Yang had never seen such a grand gesture before, and he was startled. He hurriedly helped each of them up.

Family Head Shang explained, “Please forgive us, master immortals. The Painted Skin Ghost was unpredictable, appearing in one moment and disappearing in another. I also don’t know where he came from. Ever since this Painted Skin Ghost pretended to be Steward Zhang, he forbid us from leaving the estate. If someone visited, he didn’t allow us to mention his existence, otherwise, only death would await us!”

Shang Yuan was also embarrassed. She was originally a gentle girl from a wealthy family, but she had to act like she was cold in her boudoir so that she could get Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye away from danger.

Family Head Shang continued, “It’s a pity that I have retired and been living reclusively in the countryside. All my valuables from when I was a cultivator have already been exchanged for gold, silver, and jewelry, which are useless to you, so I’m afraid I can’t repay you with that. Please let me know what you need. I’ll fulfill your request even if it means selling off whatever I have.” He wasn’t being polite but genuinely wanted to repay the favor for saving their lives. However, his current wealth was no different from scrap metal to disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

It turned out that Lu Yang did need something.

“I heard that you encountered a life-threatening great horror while raiding tombs, and that was what made you decide to quit once and for all and exit the cultivation world. May I know what happened then?”

Tao Yaoye also looked at Family Head Shang, her curiosity piqued. Tomb raiding, life-threatening, great horror, quit once and for all—these words definitely sound like a very enticing story. Maybe there’s even a great fortuitous opportunity. She liked exploring mysterious places and the unknown best.

As for Lu Yang, he wasn’t as interested as Tao Yaoye in exploring the unknown, but he did like listening to strange tales.

Family Head Shang’s eyes twitched. If he could be honest, he wished from the bottom of his heart that he didn’t have to recall that frightening past. However, since it was a question from his life-saver, he couldn’t decline.

He dismissed everyone else, especially Shang Yuan, who tried to secretly stay behind, leaving behind only Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye. “What I’m about to say must not be shared with anyone else.”

Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye nodded.

Only after receiving their assurance did Family Head Shang recounting the events from twenty years ago. “Back then, I, Shang Zhongtian, was at the Qi Training Stage, I was also somewhat famous in the world of tomb raiding. Though not infamous, it was still to the extent where many people disliked me as soon as they saw me.” Family Head Shang said, arms akimbo, as he reminisced his golden years.

On the contrary, Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye didn’t understand why Family Head Shang was so proud of it. What they didn’t know was that people in the same trade were enemies, and competition existed between tomb raiders. The fact that Shang Zhongtian could have such a reputation indicated that his skills were superlative.

Family Head Shang continued with his story. “I had always been cautious when raiding tombs. I never touched those large tombs and ancient tombs. ‘There are ghosts in large tombs and immortals in ancient tombs.’ All of us in this trade knew this saying.”

The “ghosts” he mentioned weren't small ghosts at the Foundation Establishment Stage like the Painted Skin Ghost. They were powerful entities that ruled dominion among ghosts.

“Qi Training cultivators are poor, and any valuable items they have are passed on to their descendants. How would they have burial goods worth mentioning? I didn’t touch Qi Training cultivators’ tombs because there was no profit to be gained.

“Foundation Establishment and Golden Core cultivators have a bit of wealth, and they would usually leave most of their assets to their descendants, leaving a small portion for their burial. It was precisely this small portion that was enough for me to make a gold bucket.

When I got to the end, I realized that it was a tomb within a tomb. The Golden Core cultivator’s tomb was just an accompanying burial—the main tomb belonged to a Nascent Soul cultivator!

Chapter 24: Great Horror

Shang Zhongtian lowered his voice, “I tiptoed through the cold, dry tunnel. On both sides were fist-sized luminous pearls that had been glowing for who knows how many years. With their faint blue glow, it was only enough to illuminate my silhouette but not my features. I kept feeling like someone was watching me, which made my hair stand on end, but in the end, there was nothing when I turned back. At the time, I thought it was just a figment of my imagination.

“I followed the light through the winding passageway and arrived at the core main tomb. Its scale could leave one’s mouth agape. For a moment, I forgot that I was in a dark and terrifying tomb chamber.”

Shang Zhongtian closed his eyes and paused, seemingly recalling every detail he had seen then. Only after he was done with his recollection did he slowly speak, “I had never seen such a gigantic tomb chamber. The ceiling of the cave was as high as the sky, and below it, terracotta soldiers wielding sharp bronze spears guarded their master faithfully. The lineup of burial items was dazzling, and they were all arranged in a bagua array, subtly reflecting the order of the heavenly law.

“The ancient corpse had been dead for hundreds of years, yet the terrifying aura emanating from the coffin caused my heart to palpitate. It felt as if that old Nascent Soul being hadn’t died but was merely asleep, and it could wake up from its slumber any moment.

“It wasn’t my nature to be hesitant. I made a swift decision and took away half of the burial items. Just as I was about to leave, I heard footsteps not far away. The sound ricocheted in the empty tomb chamber, making me shudder in fear.

“What happened next was a terrifying situation I had never encountered in all my years in this line of work.”

Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye involuntarily leaned forward, eager to hear more.

Shang Zhongtian showed an extremely pained expression, his voice quivering, “I met the descendants of that Nascent Soul cultivator! They had come to pay respects to their old ancestor!”

“What?” Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye had heard him clearly but the meaning of his words clearly didn’t register.

“Those people brought offerings and magical treasures to pay respects to their old ancestors. They prayed for their family’s longevity and to have many geniuses in their family gaining honor in the imperial examination. On their way, they noticed me stealing from the tomb, so they swarmed up to me and captured me. It was so scary then. Even when I think back on it now, my forehead breaks out in cold sweat.”

"...I think their reaction was pretty normal," Lu Yang said truthfully. They were cultured enough to not kill you on the spot.

"This is the great horror you mentioned?" Tao Yaoye asked.

Shang Zhongtian scratched his head, not understanding their reaction. "That’s right, encountering the descendants of the tomb owner while tomb raiding. Is there anything more terrifying?"

"And then?"

Most importantly, this junior brother constantly carried with him poison that causes athlete's foot. At the thought of that, the senior male disciple quietly moved a bit further away.

Tao Yaoye had no objections. Lu Yang had played a pivotal role in this mission while she was just bait.

Chapter 25: The Bizarre Rewards Board

Contribution points was the currency circulating within the Dao-Seeking Sect. Purchasing items, eating at the dining hall, trading with fellow disciples—all of this needed contribution points. Apart from that, obtaining special prizes in the Great Mission Hall also required contribution points.

One example was the most popular but unaffordable prize—the “Dao-Seeking Sect Leader One-Day Experience.” As the name suggested, redeeming this award allowed one to become the sect leader for a day, holding meetings with the elders and handling the affairs of the sect while being addressed as “sect leader” by others. They would be omnipotent and enjoy the privileges of the top leader among the Five Great Immortal Sects.

There were numerous benefits, but the downside was that it required too many contribution points. No one was able to redeem it even until now. It was said that several senior disciples wanted to pool their points and redeem it once for the thrills, but they got into an argument over who would become the sect leader. Nobody conceded, leading to an all-out brawl. In the end, all of them were carried to the Pill Cauldron Peak for treatment, attracting a crowd of onlookers.

Now, these senior disciples were executing long-term missions outside and hadn’t returned to the sect for a long time.

Another example was the Herb King Spirit Elixir. It was described as a precious liquid specially concocted by the higher-ups in the Dao-Seeking Sect and one of its own kind. It could be ingested or applied externally. The effects included strengthening one’s physique, enhancing one’s strength, solidifying one’s soul, and stabilizing one’s cultivation. Although its price in contribution points was exorbitant, it remained a top-seller among the senior disciples.

When one was in combat, a sip of it could allow one’s energy and powers to be replenished and their wounds to heal faster. Everyone who had used it sang high praises for it.

Yet another example was the “Flying Vessel Accident Insurance,” which could be bought for just one contribution point.

“Wait, why is there an accident insurance for flying vessels?” Lu Yang felt that the term didn’t bode well.

The senior male disciple explained it in a matter-of-fact way, “That’s very normal. How can there be a transportation vehicle that is hundred percent safe? Even the flying vessel operated by the Luodi Merchant Guild can encounter accidents like bumping into some formidable cultivator, experiencing mechanical failures, having emergency landings going wrong, and the vessel’s captain demanding a pay raise...these are all very common accidents. The good thing is that there haven't been any fatalities, so there’s nothing to be surprised about.

“After the president of the Luodi Merchant Guild realized that the flying vessel would often get into accidents, he felt that it was a risk, so he proposed to have passengers pay a small amount of money into an insurance pool. As soon as an accident with the flying vessel occurs, the merchant guild would take out a large sum to compensate the passengers.

Updated from freewēbnovel.com.

“That way, if nothing happens to the flying vessel, the passengers would simply have forked out an insignificant amount of money, but if something really happens to the flying vessel and causes delays, the passengers can get the corresponding compensation. The merchant guildmaster called this ‘insurance against risk’ and ‘insurance’ for short. This was then widely promoted to other industries.

“Not to worry though, us Dao-Seeking Sect won’t disappoint the disciples. We have always been generous in terms of insurance. When you joined the sect, all kinds of insurance had already been purchased for you, including the flying vessel accident insurance. The one shown on the rewards column is just for increasing the compensation amount.”

The senior male disciple had an expression that said “We are a proper sect from the righteous path, different from those of the diabolic path that seek death, so all necessary insurance will be provided.”

Lu Yang’s mouth twitched. “The advancements in our cultivation world are really rapid. We even have something like insurance.” In his memory from his previous life, insurance was born from maritime transport. He didn’t expect that in the cultivation world, it would be born from flying vessel transport.

This is too inauspicious. I’d rather buy something else. One should still be somewhat superstitious in the world of cultivation.

It was as if the senior male disciple had heard Lu Yang’s thoughts. “However, an expert studying karma posed the question as to whether there is a causal relationship between buying insurance and actual risk. In other words, he wondered if purchasing insurance would actually increase the likelihood of incidents.

“The merchant guild denied this possibility. Even after debating for a long time, they still haven’t come to an official conclusion. This topic has much room for research in the cultivation world. If your study concludes that there is indeed a causal relationship, that expert will take a liking to you. If your study concludes that there is no causal relationship, the Luodi Merchant Guild will take a liking to you. Regardless, it’s a win-win situation.”

Lu Yang thought to himself, If the result of my study suggests that there is a causal relationship, I’m afraid the merchant guild will come after my life.

“One contribution point can be exchanged for a hundred low-grade spirit stones. One hundred and twenty low-grade spirit stones can be exchanged for one contribution point.

“Blood-Drinking Flying Sword: Two thousand contribution points. The longer it is bathed in blood, the more powerful it becomes. Looking at the description, it doesn’t seem like it is a weapon of the righteous path.”

A senior male disciple next to him clarified, “It’s not a must for it to be soaked in human blood. Pig blood, cow blood, and duck blood all work. I heard that the shopkeeper selling Sichuan hotpot[1] in the sect went to the various mountain peaks to lodge a complaint, asking which bastard had secretly left the Blood-Drinking Flying Sword inside their duck blood.

“After a series of investigations, the culprit was found, and the hotpot shopkeeper punished him by making him drink a pot of chili oil soup base. That scene was really...tsk, I bet he wouldn’t want to eat hotpot ever again.” The senior male disciple clicked his tongue a few times. His expression turned peculiar, as if he had witnessed something unusual then.

Lu Yang continued to browse. “One bottle of fasting pills in any flavor: One contribution point.

“Ancestral barbeque secret recipe: One hundred contribution points.

“Sword Hovering Array: Twenty-five contribution points. This array can be inscribed onto a weapon, allowing it to hover behind one’s back. Without the constraint of a scabbard, one can use their sword anytime. It also comes with a protective array that can guard one’s sword from the elements.”

Lu Yang contemplated for a bit and thought that the array would be quite useful, so he happily bought it. This was a half-concealed array that congealed mid-air. When placed on the ancient sword, it evaporated like water droplets. The sword quietly hovered behind Lu Yang, making him look very cool. Whenever Lu Yang turned, the ancient sword would move together with him without the slightest delay.

“Good stuff.”

“Ten-Buffalo Strength Pills? One hundred contribution points, one thousand contribution points, ten thousand contribution points? The classic work of the pill-concocting master, Wu Ming. After consuming the pills, one can obtain the strength of ten buffaloes and sweep through armies of thousands. It is suitable for cultivators from the Foundation Establishment to the Nascent Soul stage.”

If it weren’t made by that Senior Brother Wu Ming who concocts half pills and half poison, the price would probably have been higher. Nonetheless, from the description, this pill really seems like good stuff and has wondrous use during a fight. I can buy one to test its effects.

“Junior Sister Tao Yaoye, I’m sorry, are you planning to use your contribution points to buy something? I was hoping to borrow five contribution points. I’ll pay you back the next time I complete my mission.”

Contribution points could be transferred between individuals. The thing Tao Yaoye wanted to buy required many contribution points, so five contribution points didn’t matter much to her.

“Sure.”

Lu Yang swiftly bought a Ten-Buffalo Strength Pill. The senior male disciple who had issued the mission gave Lu Yang a small porcelain bottle. Inside was a golden pill that would radiate under sunlight. It clearly didn’t look like an ordinary item.

“Didn’t I previously say that we should celebrate you reaching Foundation Establishment? Come on, let’s go eat. I’ve reserved a table at Hundred Fragrance Restaurant. I assure you that they are all what you like to eat.” Meng Jingzhou laughed heartily and extended the invitation to Tao Yaoye, “Junior Sister Tao, would you like to come with us?”

Ranked second during the entrance trials, Meng Jingzhou was considered Tao Yaoye’s senior brother.

Although Tao Yaoye knew that Lu Yang had a fear of heights, had a mouth full of lies, and even placed poison in her room without telling her, they did after all complete a mission together.

We should count as friends.

“Sure.”

Chapter 26: The Origin of The Meng Family

There were numerous businesses within the Dao-Seeking Sect, offering food, drinks, and entertainment. Cultivation was not just about going into seclusion; dull and monotonous cultivation wouldn’t lead to one becoming an immortal. The necessary forms of entertainment should also be available.

One example was the Sichuan hotpot they mentioned earlier, and another was the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant they were heading to.

However, Lu Yang heard that this was not the case for the Dao-Seeking Sect in the past. Back then, cultivation meant purely cultivation and didn’t include these miscellaneous activities that would affect one’s heart to seek the Dao.

Later, the old sect leader and former elders retired, and the new sect leader and eight elders assumed their positions, bringing a transformative change to the Dao-Seeking Sect. They encouraged everyone to cultivate hard and play hard. In their words, if even such distractions could affect one’s heart to seek the Dao, then one should forget about seeking to become an immortal.

Lu Yang felt that the current culture in the Dao-Seeking Sect was unhealthy. Once I become a higher-up in the sect, I must organize a reform.

The Hundred Fragrance Restaurant was bustling with people. Many Dao-Seeking disciples who had completed their missions or finished an arduous session of cultivation liked to gather here for a meal and share their insights regarding cultivation and their missions.

Just the taste of the food alone was already better than the dining hall.

“Waiter, we previously reserved table nine. Serve the three sets of utensils and dishes as I’ve ordered earlier.”

“Got it, please wait a moment.”

Upon reaching the second floor, the aroma of the dishes from other tables wafted into their noses, greatly boosting their appetite.

Lu Yang had been staring at the waiter for a long while, only retracting his gaze after the waiter disappeared at the entrance of the stairway. He realized that he couldn’t tell the waiter’s cultivation.

Lu Yang and Tao Yaoye looked around, both curious about this place. The former had meals at Heaven’s Gate Peak while the latter could cook, so they didn’t have a need to come here.

On the other hand, Meng Jingzhou was fairly familiar with such places. “You’ve never come here before, right? Let me tell you, there are loads of delicious food here. There’s only food you’ve never imagined before and no food you can’t find. Check out the menu.”

Lu Yang looked at the menu and flipped open to the first page, quickly drawn to its contents.

There were no dishes on the first page but only a prominent notice: “This establishment only sells prepared dishes and not raw ingredients. We seek your understanding.”

The second page was the main part, listing dishes with two types of prices—contribution points and spirit stones.

"Steamed Lightning Tribulation Liquid: Essence left behind during a cultivator's lightning tribulation; greatly beneficial for becoming enlightened with the Dao of Thunder and Lightning."

"Braised Ice Abyss Giant Elephant in Soy Sauce. The Ice Abyss Giant Elephant lives in the frigid far north. They are the dominant species in the Extreme North. An adult can crush glaciers with a single foot and remain standing upright against avalanches."

"Tomato and Egg Stir-Fry: Our shop offers various types of eggs including ordinary chicken eggs, eight treasure chicken eggs, and golden great peng bird eggs."

Noticing the prices, Lu Yang couldn't help but click his tongue. These items were clearly not meant for Foundation Establishment cultivators like them. Besides, they also couldn't afford them. However, there were things he could afford, such as stir-fried Fasting Pills.

Tao Yaoye saw Lu Yang’s furrowed brow and thought he was shocked by the prices. She couldn't help but ask with a smile, "What's wrong? Did you come across some problem?"

"Look, the meaning of fasting is to consume the spirit qi of heaven and earth instead of eating meals. Taking Fasting Pills allows one to fast."

"That's right." Tao Yaoye nodded.

"Then do you think that eating stir-fried Fasting Pills counts as eating or fasting?"

Tao Yaoye and Meng Jingzhou were both stunned. At first, they thought that the question was nonsensical, but upon further contemplation, they found it oddly profound.

The three called the waiter over and asked if he knew the answer. The waiter was also stumped. Despite working here for such a long period of time, it was his first time encountering a customer asking such a question.

Is it because I took too long to serve them?

"The prices here aren't low. Do you have enough contribution points?" Lu Yang didn't dwell on the question about the Fasting Pills. Instead, he was worried whether they had sufficient money for the food.

Meng Jingzhou had only completed three missions, so he couldn’t have earned that many contribution points. It also feels like it’s in Meng Jingzhou’s character to invite me and Tao Yaoye to a big meal only to end up washing dishes to make up for the bill.

"What contribution points? Of course, we’re using spirit stones," Meng Jingzhou said in the tone of a wealthy person.

Tao Yaoye gave Lu Yang a slightly surprised look, wondering why he would worry about the Meng Family lacking money. "Haven't you heard of the Meng family?"

Lu Yang was baffled. "Is Meng Jingzhou’s Meng Family very famous?"

The Central Continent is so vast that cultivators can spend all their lives exploring it and still not be done. There are multiple families and clans with the surname Meng. How would I know which one Meng Jingzhou is from? He had known Meng Jingzhou for a while now, but he had never heard him talk about his family.

When Meng Jingzhou came to the Dao-Seeking Sect for the entrance trials, not even a single senior member from his family accompanied him. Lu Yang had thought that Meng Jingzhou’s family had waned and needed Meng Jingzhou who had a Single Spirit Root to restore the family.

"The most famous one."

Lu Yang's pupils contracted. He now knew which Meng family Meng Jingzhou belonged to. There were many Meng families, but the most famous one was the Meng Family of the capital city. "The Meng family of the imperial city that once fought alongside the ancestor of Emperor Xia and established the Great Xia Dynasty?!"

Lu Yang was truly shocked. The Meng Family of the imperial city had a significant background. A hundred thousand years ago, when the world was in turmoil, it was often said that heroes emerged in turbulent times. The ancestors of the Meng Family and Emperor Xia led an uprising, fighting across the land for dominion, giving birth to a legendary story that was widely praised.

Even until now, the story was still popular among storytellers in teahouses and on opera stages.

A hundred thousand years ago, the previous dynasty was beset by internal strife and external threats, culminating in its fall and the start of a turbulent era. Demons and sea beasts left their territories, desiring to obtain a slice of the prime land that was the Central Continent.

The ancestor of the Meng Family rose from their ancestral land in the east, waging wars across countless li. The demon beasts fleeing from slaughter escaped back to the Demon Region, the sea beasts went back to hiding in the eastern sea, and traitorous officials and bandit heroes bowed their heads to them.

The Meng Family’s ancestor led the army for a thousand years, conquering half of the Central Continent, becoming one of the two hegemons of the land.

The other hegemon was the ancestor of Emperor Xia, who had conquered the other half of the territory. Emperor Xia’s ancestor had also driven away barbaric tribes and demon beasts, playing a part in ending the turbulent era. Each of them governed half the land, and they both made similar meritorious achievements.

At the time, people thought that the two hegemons would either rule each half of the Central Continent or start an all-out war for dominance. Thus, various strategists began to calculate which side had a bigger advantage and how the other weaker party could overcome the difference in strength.

What the people didn't expect was that both the Meng Family’s and Emperor Xia's ancestors felt that the continent had already suffered a thousand years of chaos. People were in a miserable plight, and blood flowed like rivers—it was a living hell. If the war continued, who knew how many more years of turmoil there would be and how many more would die?

They fought not for the imperial throne but to return peace to the world.

As such, the Meng Family’s and Emperor Xia's ancestors abandoned their armies and fought a decisive battle as cultivators in the expansive starry sky. During that battle, the heavens and earth almost collapsed, the sun and the moon lost their brilliance, and massive stars fell. In the end, Emperor Xia's ancestor gained a slight edge and became the final victor.

The Meng Family’s ancestor accepted the defeat and conceded. At that time, Emperor Xia's ancestor publicly declared that as long as Great Xia existed, the Meng Family would never perish.

And so it was. After the Great Xia Dynasty was established, the Meng Family settled in the capital city and was never oppressed.

Chapter 27: Cultivation Breakthrough in Hundred Fragrance Restaurant

The imperial family and the Meng Family had a close relationship and were often related through marriage. There was no lack of geniuses from the Meng Family. Every time people thought that the Meng Family had depleted their assets and foundation with their descendants unable to support the clan, a genius would emerge from nowhere and take on the mantle of continuing the Meng Family’s legendary story.

Therefore, there were rumors that the Meng Family had linked its destiny with the Great Xia Dynasty. As long as the Great Xia Dynasty remained standing, the Meng Family would never perish.

“You exaggerate,” Meng Jingzhou laughed. He humbly added, “I didn’t expect you to have guessed that I am precisely the genius from the Meng Family that emerged out of nowhere.”

“...No, we don’t think that you’re a genius,” Lu Yang spoke the truth. If the improper Meng Jingzhou were to take over the reins of the Meng Family, that would mark the end of their legendary story.

Speaking of genius, it’s more like it for me, Lu Yang, the genius, to bear the duty of leading the Dao-Seeking Sect in the future.

The two tooted their own horns while playing down the other party, completely forgetting that Tao Yaoye was right next to them. With her Metamorphic Celestial Physique, she was more of a genius than a Single’s Spirit Root and a Sword Spirit Root.

Fortunately, the two didn’t dwell on this topic for too long. An imposing and wild aura fanned out downstairs, sweeping through the entire Hundred Fragrance Restaurant. If the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant wasn’t this sturdy, one whole section of it could have collapsed!

The trio felt as if they had been struck on the head with a heavy hammer. Their minds went blank, and they could feel a large hand gripping their internal organs and squeezing the life out of them. No words could describe the immense pain they were experiencing.

The people nearby had cultivation that was minimally at the Golden Core Stage, so they were in a better state than the trio, though not by much.

“This...someone broke through to the Nascent Soul Stage?!” a Nascent Soul senior female disciple exclaimed. She hadn’t been affected. Upon further rumination, she could sense the wild intent from the aura waves.

The dishes in the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant were not just delicious. One dish could let one’s cultivation increase or let a cultivation technique circulate longer. If the dishes were combined well, they could stimulate one another’s effects, resulting in an overall better efficacy.

“I’ve long heard that just a meal at the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant can let one break through to the next major cultivation stage. I thought it was just a rumor, but I’ve now seen it in action! I wonder which junior brother or sister is so lucky to have broken through here.”

When most people broke through, they would be in seclusion and protected, desiring silence and tranquility. However, the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant was the total opposite. It was noisy and bustling with people, and that could meddle with one’s frame of mind, so it was not conducive to a breakthrough.

If someone could break through even in such an environment, it only showed how beneficial the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant was for increasing one’s cultivation!

The waiter snapped his fingers, and the oppressive pressure instantly disappeared. Everyone caught their breaths and looked at the waiter in astonishment. To them, the waiter appeared to be at the Golden Core Stage, but the casual move he displayed clearly exceeded that of a Golden Core cultivator.

The waiter had feigned his cultivation stage.

Someone whispered to their companion, “I heard the elders mention that he was already the waiter here at the Hundred Fragrance Restaurant when it first opened a thousand years ago. Even after a thousand years have passed, he is still a waiter here and his appearance hasn’t changed the slightest bit.”

Although it was fairly normal for cultivators to maintain their looks, it was still rare for someone to not change their appearance for a thousand years.

The waiter didn’t seem to have heard them whispering, and his expression was apologetic. “I’m sorry, perhaps a customer got too excited when breaking through and forgot to restrain their aura. We seek your kind understanding.”

A senior male disciple who had just reached the Golden Core Stage mused over the breakthrough aura waves from just now, his eyes lighting up. “This aura wave contains a trace of wildness like the Ancient Dragon Tribe has just appeared. It should be a physique cultivator who has broken through. Let us quickly comprehend this aura wave. Maybe it’ll be useful for improving our physiques!”

“Absolutely! This is a fortuitous opportunity for us. We should seize it.” His companions concurred and began sitting in a meditative position.

The five of them slightly levitated into the air. Their eyes were closed, and they kept silent. As a cool breeze blew in from all directions, they felt extremely comfortable. Even if one wasn’t a physique cultivator, they still valued the strength of their physique. If their power was sufficient but their body couldn’t keep up, they could easily be ambushed by others and killed in one move. If the other party insisted on engaging in close combat, they would die as soon as the enemy got close.

Hence, the Dao-Seeking Sect placed much importance on their disciples’ physique.

The Ancient Dragon Tribe was one of the supreme clans in the Demon Region, renowned for their abilities to summon the wind and rain and their invincible body. If one could comprehend even a tinge of the Ancient Dragon’s aura, it would be highly beneficial for the physical body. If they went a step further and comprehended even just half a move of the Dragon Tribe’s remarkable powers, it would be a tremendous fortuitous opportunity!

It was uncommon to see five Golden Core cultivators seated around piping hot dishes without eating them but instead sitting in a meditative position.

Lu Yang found such sensitivity to fortuitous opportunities very admirable.

Tao Yaoye proposed, “Why don’t we also take the chance to comprehend?”

Lu Yang was surprised. “You can feel the Ancient Dragon aura the senior brothers mentioned?”

“There’s no harm in trying.”

Just as the trio was considering whether they should also meditate and try to comprehend the wild aura of the Ancient Dragon Tribe, the sound of hurried footsteps came from the stairway.

A wild boar with a green face and tusks appeared, its eyes filled with panic and anger. The crowd felt a strong sense of danger.

They found the demon to be ferocious and terrifying, and its cultivation surpassed most of the people present! Furthermore, the wild boar’s aura waves were unsteady, as if it had just broken through!

The waiter knitted his brow, a small vortex rising in his palm. Just as he contemplated whether he should intervene, there was the flash of a blade, its sharp saber qi carrying a fiery aura. With one slash, the wild boar’s head and body were separated, its head rolling far away until it stopped at Lu Yang’s feet.

The wild boar stared right at Lu Yang, its eyes full of unresolved grievances.

What should have been a bloody scene ended up with not a single drop of blood lost. The burning saber qi had roasted the wild boar at its severed neck, and the aroma of roasted meat assailed the nostrils.

The owner of the saber finally appeared. He was an ordinary-looking chef wearing a tall hat. He even wore a specially made work apron, and one of his hands held a butcher knife. His face was fierce-looking; when he smiled, he resembled a bandit who intended to kill a hostage.

“Sorry, sorry, I’m sorry for startling everyone. I was just about to butcher this wild boar that is a descendant of dragons. Maybe my killing intent was too fierce, causing this beast to feel the threat to his life. He made use of this life-and-death opportunity to activate the trace of Ancient Dragon blood, breaking through to the Nascent Soul Stage.

“It is our restaurant’s fault. It won’t happen again. Please forgive us!” The chef was still carrying the butcher knife and wearing a ferocious smile, though his tone was fairly sincere.

Even if the crowd didn’t want to forgive him, they had to.

The chef picked up the boar’s head from Lu Yang’s feet and dragged it back. Only then did the pressure vanish.

The five Golden Core senior male disciples were a little embarrassed. It didn’t seem right to either continue comprehending or stop comprehending.

One person slapped the table. “Damn it, bring us a plate of slaughtered pig dish[1] made from that wild boar!”

The price of Nascent Soul pork meat was outrageously expensive, let alone a wild boar with Ancient Dragon blood. Eating this plate of slaughtered pig dish would be enough to make them slap themselves when they wake up. Even if they would slap themselves, they were determined to eat the dish today. If they didn’t eat this wild boar, their Dao hearts wouldn’t be stable, and their bottled-up resentment could likely result in internal injuries.

The waiter placed the towel on his shoulder, beaming as he shouted, “Alright, one more slaughtered pig dish for the five esteemed guests!”

Chapter 28: I Heard That There Was a Time You Ate Tofu Everyday?

Lu Yang and the other two silently retracted their gaze, hoping to make themselves invisible. Judging by the five senior male disciples’ ferocious expressions, it didn’t seem like a stretch for them to silence the witnesses on impulse.

“Speaking of which, do you want to guess what I’ve ordered for you? They’re definitely what you like to eat,” Meng Jingzhou whispered, afraid of attracting the attention of the five senior male disciples eating their slaughtered pig dish.

Lu Yang was bewildered. How does Meng Jingzhou know what I like to eat?

Tao Yaoye asked in an even softer voice, “How do you know what Senior Brother Lu likes to eat?”

Meng Jingzhou gave himself a thumbs-up, flashing his teeth as he smiled brightly. “I specially asked Big Senior Sister.”

Lu Yang instantly had a bad feeling about it.

“Fermented tofu is here!

“Freshly made tofu pudding!

“Tofu with shallots.

“Mapo Tofu.”[1]

The waiter called out the names of the dishes as he served them. A feast of fragrant tofu dishes appeared before Lu Yang. Even someone like Tao Yaoye who wasn’t interested in tofu was tempted to dig into it.

Every time a dish was announced, Lu Yang’s face would turn a bit paler.

Meng Jingzhou was proud of himself. “Big Senior Sister said that there was a time you ate nothing but tofu every day and for every single meal. You even mentioned some ‘Tofu Heavenly Sovereign’ in your dream, so I figured that you probably like tofu very much.

“You don’t have to be too touched. My family members told me that if I am to treat someone to a meal, I should find out about their preferences to show my sincerity. Although I often don’t agree with my family members, this is one point I agree with.

“I specifically came to Hundred Fragrance Restaurant to order a tofu feast. Don’t underestimate these dishes. They may look ordinary, but they’re all actually made from the finest spirit beans and spirit herbs. Even the water used is pure water obtained by melting the ice from the Extreme North...”

Lu Yang’s face instantly turned whiter than the tofu.

So this is what you found out?!

~~~

After the diners had a satisfactory meal, they patted their bellies as they left Hundred Fragrance Restaurant. The waiter swiftly wiped the tables and chairs and cleared the dishes. As soon as he took a break, he thought about Lu Yang’s question again: did taking a Fasting Pill count as eating or fasting?

Although the question seemed ordinary, there was more than met the eye. The more he thought about it, the more he thought it was philosophical. Looks like this cohort of newly recruited disciples includes a highly perceptive person. He’ll surely achieve great things in the future!

“Hey, Chef, I have a question for you.” The waiter came to the kitchen and threw the question to the chef who had slaughtered the pig.

The kitchen was scorching hot, its heat waves almost visible. If a Qi Training cultivator touched them in the slightest, even a lucky one would leave behind a lasting side effect of fire poison and be tormented for life. The unlucky ones could have their internal organs burned directly, leaving behind only a charred skeleton.

To cook heavenly and earthly treasures and rare celestial treasures, mundane fire from the mortal world wouldn’t be enough. To even burn the hair of a Nascent Soul wild boar, it was minimally required for the flame to be from the Advanced Golden Core Stage.

Ignoring the terrifyingly high temperature in the kitchen, the waiter casually fanned with the towel on his shoulder. The high temperature suddenly vanished without a single trace and was replaced by a cooling feeling.

“What’s going on? Learning how to butcher pigs from me?”

The waiter rolled his eyes. “Why would I learn this kind of thing? I just thought of a philosophical question related to culinary arts, so I came to test you.”

The chef, who was washing the stove, was intrigued and stopped washing. He cast the brush to one side and propped up his leg, “Ask away.”

“You mentioned that you’ve eaten Fasting Pills. Does that count as eating or fasting?”

The chef let out a chuckle. He thought he didn’t have to think to come up with an answer, but as soon as he wanted to say it out loud, he became mute.

Exactly, so does it count as eating or fasting?

The chef eyed the waiter suspiciously. “Hold on, everyone knows about your intelligence. How could you have thought of this question with your intelligence?”

The waiter furiously refuted, “Hey pig slaughterer! Don’t look down on others!”

“So, were you the one who thought of this question?

“No.”

The two discussed for a bit, but eventually felt that it was still too early for their brains to be pondering about such a matter. Thus, they decided to take the question to the restaurant owner.

The fragrance of tea wafted about, coming together to form ancient characters that were cryptic and mysterious. As the restaurant owner heated up the teapot, placed the tea leaves, warmed the cups, and tasted the tea, every movement was fluid as water and pleasant to the eyes.

The restaurant owner was a beautiful woman with an elegant demeanor. She was as fair as jade, and a faint star mark was imprinted on her forehead. She looked at the waiter and chef helplessly. Do they have too little work to do? That’s why they have the time to think about such a boring question?

“Don’t be misled by the name of Fasting Pills. The purpose of Fasting Pills is not for fasting. Instead, it is concocted from food such that it can slowly break down in the stomach, achieving the effect of not having to eat for a long time.

“Fasting pills are essentially food. Do you get it now?”

The chef mused over it. “I get it. So, pill-concocting masters who concoct Fasting Pills are in the same trade as me.”

The waiter laughed out loud and mocked, “Don’t flatter yourself. At best, you’re in the same trade as the pill-concocting assistant.”

The chef flew into a rage, raising his butcher knife at the waiter. The waiter was also not a pushover. He swung the towel on his shoulder, emitting a slight sound of metals clashing. The towel had instantly turned into a large white metal rod. Both got into a brawl with one person wielding a knife and the other holding a sword. They were like thugs, constantly dishing out all sorts of dirty tricks.

The restaurant owner could only sigh. If not for their cheap wages, I would never have hired them.

Gently blowing on the tea, the dense fragrance encircled the two people. With the lingering scent, they lost their bearing for a moment. By the time they regained their senses, they had already arrived downstairs.

The restaurant owner’s slightly annoyed and cold voice rang in their ears, “Go downstairs to fight. If you damage anything, it’ll be deducted from your wages.”

~~~

Lu Yang wasn’t aware of what happened in Hundred Fragrance Restaurant after they left. Finished with his celebration feast, he returned to Heaven’s Gate Peak, his face pale as if he had just died for three days.

Yun Zhi donned an indigo long skirt and wore a plain Daoist hairpin. She was seated cross-legged and three feet above the ground. Currently in a meditative position, she was cultivating and resembled an otherworldly fairy.

She slowly opened her eyes. They seemed to contain a thousand worlds in them and were as resplendent as the night sky. Right after the illusion flashed by, Lu Yang rubbed his eyes and saw Yun Zhi staring at him calmly with no sign of what he had just witnessed.

An illusion?

“Why is your face so pale?”

Lu Yang complained, “You’re purposely asking the obvious. Meng Jingzhou heard from you that there was a time I ate tofu for every meal, so he treated me to a table of tofu to congratulate me for reaching Foundation Establishment.” Lu Yang highly suspected that his dear big senior sister had a hand in this.

“Meng Jingzhou asked me what you eat most. My impression was that you ate a few vats of tofu when you were training with tofu. I simply told him the truth. What’s the problem with that?”

“Then what about the Tofu Heavenly Sovereign...”

Yun Zhi cut him off in a flat tone, “You were yelling in your sleep that you had inherited a legacy, and you shouted out the name ‘Tofu Heavenly Sovereign.’ I merely passed on what you said.”

Lu Yang stared at Yun Zhi’s innocent eyes that were free of desires.

I give up.

I keep suspecting that Big Senior Sister is playing with me, but I have no evidence.
