Chapter 29: The Story Of The Ancient Great Era

“I have already seen your mission report. You made use of your wisdom to eliminate a Painted Skin Ghost. You did pretty well.”

Lu Yang was elated. Receiving praise from Big Senior Sister is not easy. It’s worth me making the trip to Taiping Village.

The source of this content is freēwēbηovel.c૦m.

After her appraisal, Yun Zhi thought of the implication behind the Painted Skin Ghost, and her brow furrowed. “For a hundred years, following the arrival of the Great Era, various hidden factions are getting restless, and monsters are starting to roam freely. Although the Great Xia Dynasty may seem peaceful, it is unknown how many calamities lie hidden within. However, the Great Xia Dynasty insists on preserving its face, too proud to seek the Five Great Immortal Sects for help.” Yun Zhi sighed softly, her words clearly not directed at Lu Yang.

Lu Yang paid particular attention to a term Yun Zhi mentioned. “The arrival of the Great Era?” He had not heard of it before, and neither had he seen it in books.

Yun Zhi’s voice became ethereal, as if it didn’t belong to this world. “A hundred years ago, after the Grand Elder of the Heaven Strategy Sect narrowly avoided death, with his blood polluting the clear rivers, he used his life to ask the heavens, but it was unknown what he had divined.”

It was said that the Heaven Strategy Sect could divine all things. They paid attention to Heaven’s law and the natural order and believed in karma. They were the ones who questioned the Luodi Merchant Guild’s insurance.

Yun Zhi continued, “The Grand Elder announced to the world that the Great Era has already arrived and that the glory of the ancient cultivation world would reappear.

“According to past cases, accepting one Single Spirit Root from one cohort of disciples was already considered a decent outcome. However, for your batch, we have someone from the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, three Single Spirit Roots, and a Metamorphic Celestial Physique which is even more rare than a Single Spirit Root. I heard from others that the other sects have also recruited a number of Single Spirit Root geniuses in the past hundred years. From these signs, we can get a glimpse of one corner of the Ancient Great Era.”

A rare, almost indiscernible smile appeared at the corner of Yun Zhi’s mouth, seemingly mocking. “Although the Ancient Great Era is said to be a period of glory, it was in fact in extreme chaos. Various factions were intertwined; the demons, devils and monsters schemed against one another, and human hearts were unfathomable with their life and death left up to fate. Countless innocent people died before any formidable cultivator appeared. The peace and stability then definitely can’t be compared to now.”

Lu Yang found Yun Zhi’s smile to be very cold.

He had come across descriptions of the Ancient Great Era in books. It was a survival of the strongest. The victors would reign supreme, and there was no distinction between good and evil. Humans were also only one of the many powerful forces then, a far cry from their current hegemon status on the continent today.

Demons and devils emerged, intense battles clashed ceaselessly, and prodigies roamed the world, using their blood and bone to forge their fame. They were swift and decisive in slaughter, and countless cultivation experts became legends admired by millions in the process. This was a goal unattainable for many cultivators in their lifetime. Such depictions stirred cultivators’ hearts, and they wished they could transmigrate to that era to showcase their talents.

It was only in such turbulent times that various heroes had the chance to stand out. However, judging by Yun Zhi’s expression, Lu Yang realized that the Ancient Great Era might have been a good thing for prodigies, but it was hell for ordinary people. Their lives were fleeting, alive in one moment and dead in another. Just a normal conflict between those from the upper echelons, and one’s own clan members might be enslaved and imprisoned. There was no stability to speak of.

The books painted a magnificent Ancient Great Era because the author was a high-level cultivator, so he yearned for those times. If it were from an ordinary person’s perspective, it would have been an entirely different picture.

It dawned upon Lu Yang that ever since becoming a cultivator, he had seemed to forget that he was once a mortal.

This is not the way.

Yun Zhi didn’t discuss this topic further, finding it too early for Lu Yang. “What else did you want to ask?”

“Well, Big Senior Sister, do you have spells for traveling quickly?”

“Of course, I do. But what do you need this kind of spell for?” The Dao-Seeking Sect and the Luodi Merchant Guild have an agreement: when our disciples travel out, the Luodi Merchant Guild will cover all their travel and accommodation expenses and record it under our sect. Lu Yang doesn’t even need to fork out spirit stones for riding the flying vessel. What use is there for him to learn a spell for traveling quickly?

Lu Yang scratched his head, revealing an embarrassed expression. “Nothing much, I just want to learn and help our sect save money.”

Yun Zhi didn’t suspect anything. “Since you have this kind intention, as your senior sister, I shouldn’t turn you down. You’ve just reached Foundation Establishment, so there aren’t many spells you can use.”

Lu Yang sheepishly rubbed his hands. “Anything that works will do.”

“I’ve witnessed your journey in cultivation for the past year, and you live up to the name of a Sword Spirit Root. I have a Flying Sword Technique here. It can let you step on a flying sword and travel across the world.

“I also have a repositioning technique. It trains your spiritual consciousness, making it powerful enough to shift your body. You can fly as you wish, but it’s not as fast as the Flying Sword Technique. Its advantage is that it conserves our energy, and honing your spiritual consciousness can be beneficial for your battles in the future.

“Transformation techniques are also an option. After you get the grasp of it, you can transform into a bird and soar in the skies freely.

“Little Junior Brother, which one would you like?” Yun Zhi listed out a few spells for Lu Yang to choose.

“...Umm, are there spells that don’t involve flying?”

Yun Zhi looked at Lu Yang’s reddened face with an amused look. “Oh? Why do you want to learn a traveling acceleration spell that doesn’t require flying?”

Lu Yang stammered but couldn’t form a proper word.

Yun Zhi didn’t press further. “There is also a spell that doesn’t require flying. However, this spell requires immense comprehension of the Dao and has a high requirements for one’s magic power. It’s a bit too early for you to learn it now.”

“No worries, I can give it a try first. It’s fine if it doesn’t work out.”

“The name of this spell is Shrinking Earth To Inches. This is an inner cultivation method and mantra. Once you’ve memorized it, I’ll teach it to you officially.”

Yun Zhi raised her hand, casually tearing open a space. She took out a golden piece of paper that had delicate and pretty characters written neatly on it.

Lu Yang gingerly took the golden paper. This thing looks incredibly expensive. I mustn’t accidentally tear it.

After Lu Yang left, Yun Zhi closed her eyes and continued cultivating. A gust of frigid wind blew by, and an old grudgeful voice streamed into her ears. It was capable of sending chills down one’s spine and making them feel as if they had fallen into an ice cellar.

“My dear disciple, how much longer do you plan to imprison your shifu?” The voice sounded like it had come from the depths of hell, causing one’s hair to stand on ends.

“I haven’t taught you much, but it’s not easy for you to have obtained such achievements in your cultivation. Your shifu is proud of you. The saying goes that ‘a teacher for a day is a father for life.’ You can’t disregard the gratitude for your shifu’s teachings and imprison me here.

“The Dao-Seeking Sect has been without a sect leader for ten years. By acting on my behalf as the sect leader, aren’t you afraid of rumors and that it would ruin your illustrious image as Big Senior Sister?

“You even accepted a disciple in my stead. Since he’s a sword Dao genius, I’ll leave it be. But at the very least, you should let me out so that I can meet that disciple of mine. You have the real person here, yet you only let him bow at my portrait. Wouldn’t that be laughable if word gets out?” The voice contained a kind of magical power that seemed to enchant one’s heart, making one subconsciously want to believe the voice and do as it said.

Yun Zhi continued concentrating on her cultivation, turning a deaf ear to the voice.

Seeing that Yun Zhi was unmoved, the old voice turned into a long sigh. It completely vanished, as if it had never appeared.

Nothing changed for Yun Zhi as she continued sitting in a meditative position.

Chapter 30: Shrinking Earth To Inches

Three days later, Lu Yang was clad in a fit outfit. He stood ramrod straight with a jubilant smile on his face from finally memorizing the contents of the golden paper.

“Recite it once for me.”

“An existence from a thousand li instantly appears right before one’s eyes, it can be returned to normal...“[1] Lu Yang recited it fluently from memory.

Yun Zhi nodded. The mantra was awkward to chant, and every seemingly subtle word held profound underlying meaning. Reciting it would deplete a tremendous amount of mental energy. The fact that Lu Yang could recite so much was evidence enough that he had worked hard.

“This mantra is a preamble. In the initial phases, when you’re still not used to the spell, you can recite it inside your mind, and it can help you execute the spell successfully. When you become familiar with Shrinking Earth To Inches, this mantra will no longer be needed.

“Shrinking Earth To Inches is categorized as a spatial spell. You’re still early in your cultivation, but you’re Shifu’s disciple after all. When Shifu was at your cultivation, he learned this spell. Perhaps you can do it too.

“The most important thing about cultivating spatial spells is safety. As soon as there is a wrong distortion and shift in space, you may end up with your head and body separate or be severed at the waist. As such, the cultivation world has an unspoken rule—when one cultivates spatial spells, there must be a senior well-versed in spatial cultivation to guide them by the side.”

Yun Zhi was rarely solemn, so Lu Yang followed suit and listened intently to her.

“The principle of the spell Shrinking Earth To Inches is to shrink the earth until it is as small as one square inch. With that, the spell caster can easily step over it, traveling across limitless distances and arriving at a totally different place. The more familiar one becomes with the spell, the area of landmass that can be shrunk becomes bigger, and the distance they can cross also becomes farther. When you master it, nothing can stop your footsteps no matter how huge the Central Continent is.

“What you need to pay attention to is that cultivating spells requires comprehension. You’ve never been exposed to spatial spells. You should be mentally prepared that the outcome can go both ways. A cultivator should remain calm in all situations and avoid extreme joy and sorrow.” Yun Zhi imparted her cultivation experiences to Lu Yang.

Lu Yang nodded. Big Senior Sister is indeed the most qualified to say this. I've never seen her lose control of her emotions.

This is one of my flaws.

At the start, when Lu Yang saw that Yun Zhi had always maintained the same expression, he thought that it was because she had no emotions. However, after spending time with her, he realized that she did have varying emotions. It was just that the fluctuations were too subtle. Lu Yang could now roughly guess Yun Zhi’s mood based on the minute changes in her expression.

For example, now...umm, I can’t tell.

“I’ll demonstrate it for you once.”

Yun Zhi didn’t know what Lu Yang was thinking about. She threw a red flag to the summit of the mountain opposite them. Before Lu Yang could see clearly, she had already taken a step gracefully, suddenly disappearing and suddenly appearing back again, this time with the red flag in her hand.

“Just like this. After you succeed, practice a few more times and you’ll become as proficient as I am.”

Lu Yang stood rooted to the spot. He blinked his eyes.

And blinked his eyes again.

What just happened?

In Lu Yang’s eyes, Yun Zhi seemed to have thrown the red flag and taken it back directly. He couldn’t even see if the red flag had landed on the opposite mountaintop. There were no traces of a spell being used.

Yun Zhi frowned, which was a rare sight. Back when Shifu taught me, he also demonstrated it like this. I learned it in one go.

Worried that Lu Yang might not have understood, she demonstrated it once more.

She threw the flag, stepped forward, and came back. It was as fluid as the water muddling Lu Yang’s brain.

Lu Yang, “...”

As expected, there are also times when Big Senior Sister isn’t reliable. I still have to rely on myself to learn things like this.

Lu Yang met Yun Zhi’s eyes. This time, he could discern her mood.

This content is taken from fгeewebnovёl.com.

She hopes to see me succeed.

But Big Senior Sister, you have to know that no one can learn anything based on your teaching methods. Lu Yang sighed. I can’t count on Big Senior Sister anymore. I should cast the spell based on my understanding of Shrinking Earth To Inches.

“An existence from a thousand li, instantly appears right before one’s eyes, returning to normal when left alone...” Lu Yang's eyes were tightly shut. He chanted and made finger gestures as he performed the spell.

“Shrinking Earth To Inches!” Lu Yang yelled. Instantly, his body vanished, and his surroundings changed. It became pitch black, as if he had landed in an alternate space.

Lu Yang was elated. I actually succeeded on the first try.

I’m indeed a genius!

Lu Yang had heard from Yun Zhi that the principles of Shrinking Earth To Inches were distorting space. The spell caster walked in an alternate space which was a straight line. Through this alternate space, one could reach their destination in the shortest possible time.

Just as Lu Yang wanted to smile, he realized that the surrounding black matter began pouring into his mouth. He also got trapped by the black matter, unable to move his hands and legs. Furthermore, there seemed to be no air inside this alternate space, making his breathing laborious.

After a short moment of composed rumination, he realized one thing—he had shrunk into the earth.

Lu Yang now had good news and bad news.

The good news was that he had learned half of Shrinking Earth To Inches: Shrinking Earth.

The bad news was that he had only learned half of it.

Still standing on the ground surface, Yun Zhi didn’t know what to say. She witnessed the whole process of Lu Yang casting the spell and then shrinking into the earth, learning the Earth Escape Technique.

How did a spatial spell change to an elemental spell?

As the Big Senior Sister of the Dao-Seeking Sect and the most senior disciple of the sect leader, her cultivation and talent were the best among all disciples. She could casually scribe cultivation techniques and learn spells by just observing. Her comprehension was also extraordinary and rare even throughout history. Any genius before her would probably lose their radiance and might even find her terrifying.

However, even she could not understand Lu Yang’s spellcasting principle. These are clearly two unrelated spell types.

With a muffled pop, Lu Yang performed Shrinking Earth To Inches again. His head popped out of the ground like a mole, giving people the urge to hit him with a hammer or step on him.

He coughed, trying to resolve the awkwardness. However, no matter how thick-skinned Lu Yang was, he still couldn’t withstand such an awkward situation.

Yun Zhi pulled Lu Yang out from the earth without any expression, shaking off a pile of mud and dirt along with it.

It was just like pulling up a radish.

“That was just an accident. I’ll try again.” Lu Yang felt like he was close to finding the key trick.

“An existence from a thousand li, instantly appears right before one’s eyes, returning to normal when left alone...” Lu Yang made finger gestures as he chanted faster than before.

“Shrinking Earth to Inches!” Lu Yang hollered.

Something took effect again.

Although Yun Zhi was tall, she was still half a head shorter than Lu Yang. Usually, Lu Yang could see the top of Yun Zhi’s head, but it was different now.

Yun Zhi’s body gradually became taller. Starting from looking down at her, Lu Yang looked straight at her, then looked up at her, and finally ended up straining his neck to look up. With his current angle, he couldn’t even see the whole of Yun Zhi’s face.

Yun Zhi looked like a titan holding up the sky, her head touching the heavens and her feet stepping on the earth.

“Wait, it’s me who got smaller!” Lu Yang shrieked. When he saw the stone that was half a person’s height, he realized the source of the problem.

The three-inch Lu Yang jumped around on the ground, his voice much softer than normal.

He had learned a new spell: To Inches.

Lu Yang’s talent in spells could also be described as terrifying. The genius, Yun Zhi, had only learned one spell—Shrinking Earth To Inches—when she was learning the spell. However, Lu Yang learned two spells instead—Shrinking Earth and To Inches!

Yun Zhi squatted down to observe Lu Yang. Her brow was knitted, seemingly because she still couldn’t figure out which step had gone wrong.

1. This is taken from the poet Li Bai. The “Shrinking Earth” technique is also a well-known immortal technique. It originated from the book Deities and Immortals or Shenxian Zhuan by Ge Hong of the Jin Dynasty ☜

Chapter 31: Learning For Practical Application

Yun Zhi grabbed Lu Yang’s collar with two fingers and shook him. However, she still couldn’t understand the underlying reason, so she put him back.

Lu Yang was similarly bewildered. “This doesn’t make sense.”

I followed Big Senior Sister’s mantra and method, but why did it become two completely different spells when I cast it?

“I’ll demonstrate it to you again.” Yun Zhi was a responsible teacher. Although her teaching skills were average, her patience made up for it.

She took out an hourglass and put it on the ground. Then she touched Lu Yang’s shoulder, and the both of them leaped through space and time.

Lu Yang’s vision blurred for a moment before he found himself in a strange space with colorful rays of light flowing like a stream on both sides. He subconsciously reached out to touch the flowing light, but Yun Zhi stopped him. “That’s a phenomenon from time distortion. Even Divine Transfiguration cultivators would be shredded into smithereens and have their soul disintegrated if they touch this light, let alone you.”

Her words frightened Lu Yang so much that he instantly retracted his hand.

The two stepped out of the space and saw a giant white snake coiling around a mountain. It was devouring the sun and the moon, cultivating with the essence of heaven and earth. Something flickered in its eyes, and the two of them happened to land inside the giant snake’s mouth and enter its stomach.

Before the gastric acid was about to drip onto them, Yun Zhi took another step and they arrived at another strange space. Following Yun Zhi, Lu Yang witnessed all kinds of bizarre and gaudy scenes—oceans of lava, cultivators going through lightning tribulations, and silent swordsmen carrying their wide sabers... He had never seen or heard of such places, so it was hard to imagine that such wondrous people and sights still existed in the world.

Finally, the two were back at their starting point. Lu Yang was panting and still hadn’t recovered from his shock.

“All the places I took you to just now are within the Dao-Seeking Sect. You can head there by yourself when you have the chance in the future.”

The Dao-Seeking Sect was too expansive; anywhere apart from the nine core mountain peaks were still unknown to Lu Yang.

“Why don’t you try casting the spell again?” Yun Zhi felt that things might be different this time.

Under Yun Zhi’s earnest gaze, Lu Yang braced himself as he cast the spell again.

After a day of training, Lu Yang finally learned how to sense the underground environment and how he could avoid getting stepped on after shrinking himself.

He didn’t succeed a single time for Shrinking Earth to Inches, but he succeeded every single time for both Shrinking Earth and To Inches. In fact, he became more proficient with every attempt.

In the end, he didn’t even need the mantra. As if he had immersed himself in this Dao for years, he could now cast the spell with just a thought.

Lu Yang’s original intention in learning Shrinking Earth To Inches was for traveling quickly. However, he had instead mastered “Shrinking Earth” to travel faster, so it could somewhat be considered to be in line with his initial goal. The only issue was that he didn’t know what to make of his method, and its speed was also slower.

Watching Lu Yang having plenty of fun changing his size at will and darting in and out of the earth, Yun Zhi casually asked, “Little Junior Brother, I heard that you had a hard time finding missions in the Great Mission Hall?”

“That’s right, many missions can only be completed with the Golden Core Stage and above, so there are very few missions suitable for me.” Lu Yang was considering going and camping in the Great Mission Hall for a few days to see if he could find a suitable mission.

“It just so happens that a few days ago, I had a meeting with the elders, and someone mentioned that there was a slight problem at the herb garden. They posted the mission in the Great Mission Hall, but no one accepted it. You seem like a suitable candidate. Why don’t you go to the herb garden and take a look?”

Lu Yang knew that ever since his master went into seclusion, it was Yun Zhi who presided at the meetings on his behalf. “What mission is it?” Lu Yang was puzzled. I don’t have any particularly outstanding strength. What kind of mission could be suitable for me? Besides, I know nothing about the herb garden. I haven’t even finished learning how to distinguish herbs.

“You’ll know when you’re there.” Yun Zhi didn’t give an answer to his question.

~~~

From Lu Yang’s current observations, the Dao-Seeking Sect was like a miniature version of the cultivation world. Without leaving the sect, one could find people to concoct pills, craft artifacts, and set up arrays... They were self-sufficient most of the time.

Concocting pills required spirit herbs. The Dao-Seeking Sect had an extremely high demand for pill concoction, but they couldn’t keep relying on external procurement. To mitigate this issue of spirit herb supply, the sect opened up a massive patch of land for a herb garden, meant for planting medicinal herbs. The Great Mission Hall also posted missions about helping with growing the herbs in the herb garden.

Growing herbs required professional knowledge, something Lu Yang completely lacked. Up until now, he was still ignorant of the herbs and spirit meat he ate every day, much less knowledge on cultivating herbs.

From a distance, Lu Yang could already smell the fragrance from the herb garden. Unlike the fragrance from the Pill Cauldron Peak which had a probability of being poisonous, the smell here was the purest medicinal fragrance. Inhaling it for prolonged periods of time could let one live longer and remain healthy.

An old man lay at the entrance of the herb garden. He was leisurely napping on the rocking chair with a cattail-leaf fan[1] covering his face.

“Mister, is this the herb garden?”

The old grandpa glanced at Lu Yang with half-hooded eyes. “Who are you?”

“Lu Yang.”

“I didn’t ask for your name. I was asking for your identity.”

“Fourth disciple of the sect leader and Big Senior Sister Yun Zhi’s little junior brother.”

The old grandpa didn’t give much of a reaction when he heard the first part. The sect leader? That old fellow has already disappeared for ten years. Who cares about him? He should retire and stop occupying the position. How can he make Yun Zhi do all the work for him?

However, he immediately came to a realization when he heard the latter part. The sect leader’s disciple means that he is Yun Zhi’s little junior brother!

The old grandpa immediately sprung up, even more agile than Lu Yang. This was normal in the cultivation world; one couldn’t judge the other party’s skills and age just by their outer appearance. When an old man and a child stood together, you could never be sure who the grandfather was and who the grandson was. No one advocated for respecting the elderly and doting on the young, for the elderly and child could actually be more of a fighter than you were.

“So it was Yun Zhi who recommended you. You should’ve said that earlier.” The grandpa hooked his arm around Lu Yang’s shoulder as if they were brothers. “We are all part of the Dao-Seeking Sect. You can just call me Old Ba. I call the shots for this herb garden.”

Lu Yang suspected that Grandpa Ba was taking advantage of him, but he had no evidence.

“What did Yun Zhi ask you to do? Pick herbs? How many years old do you need the herbs to be, one thousand or two thousand?”

Seeing Grandpa Ba like this, Lu Yang couldn’t help but be reminded of the meal Yun Zhi made for him. Don’t tell me they’re all one- or two-thousand-year-old herbs picked from the herb garden? One-thousand-year-old herbs are not like common vegetables. They’re precious to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

No way, no way. Big Senior Sister is a fairly frugal person, she couldn’t possibly waste these medicinal ingredients on me.

Lu Yang replied politely, “Big Senior Sister said that the herb garden posted a mission a few days ago, but no one accepted it. What mission is it?”

Grandpa Ba immediately knew what he was referring to. “Do you know how to cultivate herbs?”

“Not at all,” Lu Yang answered honestly.

“I’ll explain it to you simply then. Cultivating herbs comprises rather complicated steps. One of them is loosening the soil. This is so that the roots of the herbs can better absorb the spirit energy from the soil and exchange it with the spirit energy in the air.

“This task of loosening the soil has always been done by a Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm husband and wife. However, they recently have some family issues, and there’s no one doing the work, so I posted a mission to have the herb garden’s soil loosened. This requires one of the elemental spells—Earth Escape Technique. Although there are many who know this technique, they all find it too troublesome and are unwilling to accept the task. Fortunately, Yun Zhi sent you here.”

“So what I need to do is...”

“Mimic an earthworm and burrow into the soil to loosen the soil for the herb garden.”

Lu Yang, “...”

I suspect that Big Senior Sister is playing with me, but I still have no evidence.

Chapter 32: Ginseng Doll

Objectively speaking, burrowing into the earth in the herb garden was a good idea. While practicing the technique of Shrinking Earth, he could also put his herbal knowledge to practical use and make up for his lack of knowledge, essentially killing two birds with one stone.

Big Senior Sister is doing this for my sake.

Big Senior Sister is doing this for my sake.

Big Senior Sister is doing this for my sake.

Lu Yang hypnotized himself into thinking that Yun Zhi had his best interests at heart, so he should sincerely accept this mission of burrowing into the ground as a replacement for the earthworms. Suddenly, he remembered something.

Earthworms are supposed to be hermaphrodites.

“Why would earthworms have husband and wife?”

Grandpa Ba explained, “The earthworms in the mortal world are indeed hermaphrodites, but that’s a trait of low-level beings. Oh, I don’t mean that in a derogatory way. Earthworms that are sentient can transform to have genders, especially the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworms. They are the king among earthworms and can exert bloodline suppression on all other earthworms.”

“I understand. Please continue.”

Grandpa Ba continued, “Originally, with the Silver-Ringed Monarch Earthworm couple around, there was no problem with loosening the soil. It’s my fault for shooting my mouth off that day. I asked the wife, ‘I heard that earthworms can still live after splitting into two. If you also split into two, wouldn’t you be able to work for one day and rest the next day by alternating with your new self?’

“She was tempted by what I said, and she split herself up on the spot, turning into two individuals. They were as identical as twin sisters, no, it was like a clone splitting technique. I watched right as one person turned into two people, and I couldn’t identify the original. Fortunately, they themselves could tell.

“When the husband returned, he was stumped to see two wives. The two of them asked the husband who he liked. The husband was a straightforward person, so he directly said that he liked the two beautiful sisters.

Lu Yang, “...”

Dang, that’s crazy.

“What exactly should I do?” Lu Yang quickly regained his composure and gradually adapted his mindset to that of a cultivator.

They’re all small matters.

Grandpa Ba stroked his white beard and smiled. “You can go in first, someone will guide you. But let me remind you, you’re entering the herb garden to loosen the soil. If you dare to secretly pick herbs, the Law Enforcement Peak will definitely hold you responsible!”

The Law Enforcement Peak, managed by First Elder, was strict and impartial.

Lu Yang thanked Grandpa Ba and walked into the herb garden. Upon entering, the medicinal fragrance was ten times stronger than before.

The smell can’t possibly differ so much in just a few steps. Lu Yang immediately realized that although it seemed that Grandpa Ba was the only one guarding the herb garden, there was actually an entire array protecting the herb garden and preventing outsiders from entering. This array kept the herb garden’s aura waves locked in, but the medicinal fragrance was so intense that even the large array couldn’t contain all of it, and a bit of it had leaked out.

Just this slight bit was already sufficient to extend the lifespan of mortals. One could only imagine what other miraculous effects the medicinal fragrance inside the herb garden could provide!

Apart from the medicinal scent, the most striking aspect was the spirit energy. It was too thick. Lu Yang suspected that it was not dew but water droplets condensed from spirit energy on the leaves. Every drop would be roughly worth one low-grade spirit stone!

Wherever Lu Yang’s eyes went, it would be verdant and lush greenery. Manifold types of herbs that he had never heard of or smelt spread out before him. They were neatly arranged into rows and categorized into different regions based on their breeds.

Lu Yang didn’t even know where to look. He didn’t dare to walk as he wished, afraid that he might accidentally step on some rare breed.

Squatting down, he looked at several herbs before finally finding one he recognized. The herb had three leaves and clear veins. It appeared as if it had been formed from ice, emitting a faint coldness.

“Ice Soul Grass. I remember that this kind of flower can help those cultivating ice-element techniques and increase their absorption of spirit energy.”

Every Ice Soul Flower was spaced apart from one another to prevent the coldness they emanated from combining together and freezing themselves.

Lu Yang’s memories of his battles with the puppet were still vivid. When he was beaten into a sorry state by the puppet, the puppet would use Ice Soul Grass afterward to apply on his wound. However, he really didn’t recognize the other herbs.

“Hey, who are you?” a not so courteous voice called out.

Lu Yang turned around but saw no one. “Who’s speaking?”

“Hey, look down,” the voice told him.

Lu Yang lowered his head and saw a three-inch tall ginseng doll hopping around at his feet. It seemed to be displeased with Lu Yang for being so slow and needing it to hint to him.

“You’re so stupid. Why didn’t you know to look down? You even needed me to remind you!”

The ginseng doll’s legs were chubby and sturdy. It ran around Lu Yang, its two roots acting as its arms and waving up and down. Its facial features from its body line patterns were as expressive as a human.

“Youngster, who are you?” the ginseng doll asked in an old-fashioned manner.

A ginseng that could become sentient had to be quite old. Lu Yang didn’t dare to be disrespectful, so he bowed. “I am Lu Yang. I accepted the mission to loosen the soil for the herb garden.”

“So you’re just someone loosening the soil.” The ginseng doll heaved a sigh of relief. I thought it was those vile humans coming here to pick the herbs again. The herbs in the herb garden are all cultivated by me.

“Since you could come in, you must have gotten Little Ba’s approval. Other than Little Ba and that she-devil, I haven’t seen outsiders for a while now.”

The old Grandpa Ba was simply considered a junior to the ginseng doll. To them, high cultivation was not as important. What mattered to herbs was who lived the longest. There was no one that caught the ginseng doll’s eyes in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Lu Yang had heard about the herb garden’s rules. The herbs were precious. If one wanted to get the herbs for treatment purposes, they had to ask the person guarding the garden to pick it for them. Apart from the person guarding the herb garden, no one else could enter.

If not for Lu Yang’s mission, he also wouldn’t have been able to enter the herb garden. The ginseng doll mentioned a she-devil. Is she the other person guarding the herb garden?

The ginseng doll placed its hand-like roots on its hips and complained, “Why are you humans all so tall?”

Lu Yang felt that keeping his head lowered while talking was tiring, so he made use of the To Inches technique to shrink himself into three inches, the same size as the ginseng doll.

“Oh? Youngster, you’re much better than Little Ba.” The ginseng doll was initially shocked, but the surprise quickly turned into joy instead.

It was rare for a human to be the same height as it. It was irking for it to always have to look up at humans; the ginseng doll’s head and body were one entity with no neck.

“From now on, in this herb garden, you can just follow my lead!” the ginseng doll declared in a bold and grand manner. It used its ginseng roots to pat Lu Yang’s shoulder as a form of approval.

“I still have some things to attend to. You can follow me. After I’m done, I’ll take you to see the other herb kings.”

When herbs became sentient, they would become herb kings and the most precious of herbs. Even other powerful sects might not have one. If they did obtain one, they would likely worship it as their ancestor.

However, based on what the ginseng doll implied, it seemed that herb kings like it were not a rarity in the herb garden.

Lu Yang clicked his tongue softly. The Dao-Seeking Sect’s foundation is really scary.

Chapter 33: Herb Garden

Lu Yang followed the ginseng doll closely, taking in the scenery of herbs from a novel perspective. The sunlight shone through the gaps between the leaves, casting spots of light on Lu Yang.

After turning small, the herbs had become trees in Lu Yang’s eyes. They could shield him from the sunlight and were much taller than he currently was.

Soon, one human and one ginseng came across a rapid stream. As it was imbued with spirit attributes bred from nature, it was used to irrigate the herbs, and some of the water would be purified and flow back to the stream, achieving a win-win situation.

”This is the river guarded by the River Spirit,” the ginseng doll introduced.

The surrounding of the Dao-Seeking Sect was a stream that would sometimes be fast and sometimes slow. Its source was an endless spring.

This spring carried a long history. Before the Dao-Seeking Sect was established, the spring received blessings from heaven and earth, developing spirit light. To non-living beings, their greatest fortuitous opportunity was to gain spiritual intelligence. This spark of spirit light was instrumental.

If the spirit light came to them and they became sentient beings, it would be akin to suddenly being elevated to nature’s favored child. If the spirit light dissipated into nature, it was unclear how many more years would be needed to produce that bit of spirit light again.

These non-living beings drifted with the tide of the world, and one day, they might be caught up in a battle among cultivators and disintegrate, losing all hope of ever gaining spiritual intelligence. The probability of the spirit light disappearing was greater than the probability of it becoming theirs.

Fortunately, a predecessor from the Dao-Seeking Sect passed by. They discovered this situation and cast a spell to trap this spirit light within the spring. Only then did the spring truly gain spiritual intelligence.

Grateful to the Dao-Seeking Sect predecessor, the spring willingly guarded the Dao-Seeking Sect. This stream flowed throughout the whole sect, protecting the sect at its periphery and becoming one of the sources of life from within the sect. The spirit of this spring was also known as the River Spirit.

From an ordinary person’s perspective, the river was no more than two zha[1] long, and the flow was also slow. It would be complimenting it to even call it a stream.

After turning small, this stream appeared even more exciting. A wooden plank lay across the stream as a bridge. The herb kings had likely built it here in advance.

When Lu Yang crossed the stream, he didn’t know whether it was an illusion, but the stream seemed to flow more rapidly.

As if it’s...excited to see me?

Lu Yang wasn’t very sure.

Not far away, he saw a majestic city wall constructed with limestone, each larger than his present self. Only when they got closer did he realize that it was the wall of the herb garden.

The ginseng doll dug at the base of the wall a few times, revealing transparent stones that seemed to have their insides sucked away, leaving only an empty transparent glass. The ginseng doll stretched its roots which were as nimble as tentacles, stringing the transparent stones together.

Lu Yang raised his eyebrow. “This is...” He kept feeling that these things looked familiar.

“I remember that you humans call these things spirit stones.”

Realization hit Lu Yang. No wonder it looked so familiar! Aren’t these spirit stones that have their spirit qi drained? But I haven’t seen such high-quality ones.

“You like these things? Little Ba often buries these stones at the base of the wall. When the stones become empty, he’ll ask me to collect them so that he can take them all away at once.”

Lu Yang now understood how it worked. Planting herbs requires vast amounts of spirit qi, but the spirit qi in the herb garden wasn’t infinite. Thus, the Dao-Seeking Sect buried spirit stones in the herb garden to provide pure, concentrated spirit qi.

No wonder I felt that the spirit qi in the air was absurdly rich right as I stepped inside the herb garden. It’s because they’re fed by spirit stones. Spirit stones used in the herb garden won’t be of a low grade. It’s quite possible that they’re rare high-grade spirit stones.

After the ginseng doll was done with stringing the spirit stones together, it walked ahead with Lu Yang following behind. As they walked, it chatted with Lu Yang, “There’s a great array covering the whole herb garden underneath our feet. I think it’s called the Eternal Evergreen Array, and it helps our herbs grow healthily. These transparent stones are part of the array.”

Lu Yang had heard of the Eternal Evergreen Array. It was a top-notch array used for cultivating spirit herb, but it required an enormous amount of spirit stones yearly.

“By the way, I heard Little Ba mention that our sect is rather poor, struggling to keep their stomachs full just to keep us. They’re like playing some cuju[2] match where a group of people fight to the point of bleeding just to snatch a ball. Is that true?”

Lu Yang didn’t dare to answer. This Grandpa Ba appears to be kind on the outside, but he has no qualms about lying to the herb kings.

“This is called Illusion Shattering Immortal Wood, also known as the bane of the unreal. It has the ability to shatter illusions and let one see the truth. If you’re caught in an illusion technique, quickly grasp this wood and you’ll be able to dispel the illusion.”

Lu Yang followed the ginseng doll’s gaze.

He saw a cactus.

“Those are Sun-Exploding Flowers, one of the essential ingredients for cultivating the Searing Sun Dharma Body. Other than its capabilities for cultivating dharma bodies, adding it to any fire-element pills can add a bit of searing sun true essence, greatly benefiting cultivators with a Fire Spirit Root.

“The best-quality Sun-Exploding Flowers are Nine-Turns. Nine-Turns Sun-Exploding Flowers are useful even for Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. This area consists of Six-, Seven-, and Eight-Turns Sun-Exploding Flowers.

“That's the Dao Enlightenment Forest over there. When its leaves are soaked in water, it has the ability to help with Dao enlightenment, and its wood is a raw material for crafting high-grade magical treasures. I heard that the price in the outer world has shot up to the sky. Every autumn, Little Ba would pick a large batch of Dao Enlightenment leaves for all of you to consume.”

Lu Yang had seen many descriptions of the Dao Enlightenment Tree. They comprised all kinds of flowery words, praising the tree to be an immortal species and divine tree and even claiming that the reason for the rise of humans in ancient times was partly attributed to the Dao-Enlightenment Tree.

Read latest chapters at freewebnovel.com Only.

However, it was his first time seeing a real Dao Enlightenment Tree in person. The Dao Enlightenment Tree was a few dozen meters tall, but to the three-inch Lu Yang, it looked like the Sacred Jianmu Tree that could reach the sky in the legends. He had to raise his head so much that dizziness seized him, and his ears rang as if the Dao of the world was rumbling in his ears.

“I heard Little Ba say that it’s best for low-rank cultivators to not consume Dao-Enlightenment leaves because their Dao heart and foundation are lacking. Giving it to them too early would be like pulling at a seedling to help it grow, ruining it due to excessive zealousness. It wouldn’t be favorable for their cultivation and comprehension of the Dao in the future.

“This is the same concept as not using too much fertilizer when the herbs are young.

“As the tree ages, the Dao Enlightenment in its leaves would become better. The oldest in the Dao Enlightenment tree is even older than I am and also an herb king. You’ll see it later.

“This is called Lovesick Grass, one of the key ingredients for concocting the Lovesick Moon Pills. When the bright moon is in the sky, if two people separated by distance ingest these Lovesick Moon Pills at the same time, they’ll be able to cross the boundaries of time and space to speak with each other.

“It is said that there was a pair of lovers in ancient times. The man was born from an eminent clan and was the clan leader’s son, while the woman was of a humble origin and the descendant of slaves. One day, when the man was hunting outside, he met a woman. The two fell in love at first sight and promised themselves to each other for life.

“Unfortunately, as the son of an eminent clan’s leader, he had no freedom to choose his partner, much less marry a slave as his wife. The clan forced him to marry the daughter of another eminent clan’s leader so that the relationship between both well-matched clans could get closer.

“However, the man refused to comply. He sneaked out on the day of his wedding and eloped with the woman. When the elders of the clan found out, they dispatched experts to kill the woman, and she died in the man’s arms. Overwhelmed with grief, the man took his own life, and their blood converged to form a wild grass which had even the roots stained red. It then became known as Lovesick Grass.”

The story piqued Lu Yang’s interest, and he subconsciously asked, “That’s so touching. Did it really happen?”

“It’s fake. Someone made up this story just so that they could sell the Lovesick Grass for a high price. I was right there when the story was fabricated.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Chapter 34: Little Herb Kings

“Back when I traveled across the Central Continent, I made quite the reputation for myself. If not for someone spreading the word about my yang-boosting efficacy, I wouldn’t have been forced to come to the Dao-Seeking Sect to seek refuge. I would still be traveling around.

“The person traveling with me was also a big name among humans, called Devotee Guyue. When he sent me to the Dao-Seeking Sect, he said he would include me in his book so that people can remember me.”

Devotee Guyue was a famous traveler from the Central Continent. He liked adventures and wandering across places. He left his mark on the Central Continent, Demon Region, and Buddhist Kingdom, with legends of him circulating around various regions.

Legends said that he once served as a scribe in the Great Xia Dynasty, meticulously chronicling the Xia Emperor’s romantic encounters and his many illegitimate children.

In the Demon Region, Devotee Guyue was abducted by the princess of the Dragon Tribe and forced into marriage. He managed to escape, but they pursued him all the way to the Buddhist Kingdom for his head.

In the Buddhist Kingdom, he pretended to be a monk and became a con artist. Every time someone found a loophole in his logic or met a problem they couldn’t solve, he would say “Buddha says it can’t be told.” Later, this phrase would become widespread in the Buddhist Kingdom.

Devotee Guyue also compiled his own experiences into a book, which became fairly popular in the cultivation world.

Although there were no ancient records that explicitly documented Devotee Guyue’s cultivation, Lu Yang surmised that it shouldn’t be low. If his cultivation were just a bit lower, he would probably have gotten beaten to death a long time ago.

The ginseng doll was a superb teacher. It shared stories from its personal experiences, and even revealed that it had discovered the numerous herb species in the herb garden alongside Devotee Guyue. Lu Yang was engrossed the more he listened to it.

The duo of human and ginseng arrived at a small hut built from flowers and grass. The closer they got to the small hut, the more the almost tangible vital energy emanating from within caused Lu Yang’s heart to race.

“Something’s wrong!” Lu Yang clutched his chest, his body trembling involuntarily.

Thump, thump, thump... Lu Yang’s heartbeat became increasingly faster. He felt as if there were countless tiny bugs flying around his ear and buzzing incessantly.

Paying closer attention to the sound, his heart sank into coldness, and a chill ran down his spine. That’s not the sound of tiny bugs. They’re the voices of countless people speaking inside my body!

Those voices are telling me that they’re trapped within my body and that they want to leave...

The ginseng doll was the first to notice that something was amiss with Lu Yang and hollered, “Hey hey hey, an outsider is here. All of you, quickly withdraw your vital energy!”

Lu Yang manipulated his cultivation technique and quelled his boiling blood. Only then did the voices gradually vanish. He fell to the ground on his knees, gasping for air. Everything that had just happened was not an illusion. There was really something inside me. What was it?!

The ginseng doll placed down the empty spirit stones and ran to Lu Yang while bobbing up and down. Its tone was apologetic, “Sorry about that, I didn’t expect you to not have reached the Nascent Soul Stage.”

Different from humans, herb kings didn’t measure their cultivation stage but by their age instead. The ginseng doll couldn’t tell Lu Yang’s cultivation, only finding him pleasing to the eye.

“What...was that?” Lu Yang still hadn’t fully recovered from his shock. He felt as if he had just returned from a tour around hell.

“Little Ba’s and the she-devil’s cultivation are considered too high among you humans, so I forgot about how our vital energy might affect you. It is so abundant that it can make you feel like every organ in your body has developed its own consciousness and become a separate entity. When you’ve reached the Nascent Soul Stage with perfect meridians and orifices and no vulnerable interstices in your body, you will no longer be affected by our vital energy.”

Hearing the commotion from the ginseng doll’s side, numerous three-inch tall herbs hopped over to Lu Yang.

“Ginseng King, who is this person? Why is he so tiny?”

“You call this tiny? He’s clearly the same height as us! Are you calling yourself tiny too?!”

“It must be magic. Humans’ spells are very mystical. There’s nothing surprising about turning big or small. I’ve even seen males becoming females and humans becoming demons.”

“This person’s cultivation doesn’t look like it’s very high? Has he not reached the Pregnant Stage?”

“What Pregnant Stage? Qilin King, your memory is failing. It’s called the Nascent Soul[1] Stage.”

“He doesn’t look like he’s steady on his feet. Let’s carry him inside the hut.”

The little herb kings softly discussed among themselves for a while, their buzzing noises uncomfortable for Lu Yang’s ears. They first raised Lu Yang over their heads, then carried him into the small hut.

The Dao Enlightenment Tree stood outside, scratching its trunk, causing the leaves to rustle. Its head was too huge, so it couldn’t enter the small hut.

Only when Lu Yang got inside did he realize that the small hut wasn’t built from flowers and grass but ancient wood. Under the vital energy of the herb kings, the ancient wood appeared to be perpetually in spring, sprouting new leaves and fresh flowers and covering its original appearance.

Lu Yang was feeling much better. He slowly got up and tried to distinguish the herb kings.

Guess what? I don’t know a single one.

“Human, what’s your name?” a small grass with three tender leaves asked. Its entire body was silver, and there were specks of starlight on its leaves, as if they were the microcosm of space.

“I am Lu Yang. Senior, may I know who you are...?” Lu Yang asked politely. According to their ages, the little herb kings were not only his seniors but also the seniors of everyone in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“It's called Three-Leaf Starry Herb. We all call it Star King,” another little herb king answered quickly. It was a multi-colored flower, each of its leaves corresponding to the five elements. The center of the petals was divided into black and white, with a bit of white in the black part and a bit of black in the white part, forming a Taiji design. It looked like a mesmerizing ink painting that could suck one’s soul inside.

“I’m the Time Terminus Flower. You can just call me Terminus King. Everyone says that I’m the most beautiful flower. I think it’s because someone is jealous of my charm and is trying to bring me down by showering me with excessive compliments. As a modest herb king, I think that I’m just the world’s second most beautiful flower...” the Time Terminus Flower chatted endlessly.

Lu Yang stared at the Time Terminus Flower for two seconds, his pupils widening with incredulity. Although he didn’t know how a Time Terminus Flower looked, its reputation preceded it.

“Time Terminus Flower...is that the flower that is claimed to bloom so beautifully that time would come to a standstill, but that’s only when the world is about to end and living beings are plunged into devastation?!”

Lu Yang couldn’t be blamed for being so astonished. The ancient records documented that the blooming of the Time Terminus Flower signaled the end of the world, meaning that the world would be completely reset.

But from what I’ve read in the ancient books, a catastrophe of such scale has never happened before!

The Time Terminus Flower scratched its nectar. “Someone did say that, but I remember that I bloomed during very peaceful times. Everyone was joyful and in harmony, and I didn’t see any disasters. Perhaps the story of my blooming is just a rumor.”

Lu Yang was about to ask more when he heard another little herb king speak. “Lu Yang, why did you come to the herb garden? Did Little Ba ask you to pick some herbs?” a small jade-green Qilin asked. It appeared as if it was an exquisite piece of work carved from fine jade, looking like it didn’t belong to this world.

Lu Yang was taken aback again. “Qilin?!”

A qilin is one of the most mysterious demon beasts. It’s a miracle to even find one or two. They’re much rarer than Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. Their traces can only be found through fragmented information in ancient records. But you’re telling me that there’s actually one in the Dao-Seeking Sect?!

The depth of Dao-Seeking Sect’s foundation was so terrifying that it was completely beyond Lu Yang’s wildest imagination.

The ginseng doll explained, “It’s the Qilin Immortality Herb. Its current form is its dharma body. Your cultivation is inadequate. When you’ve reached the Divine Transfiguration Stage and cultivated a heavenly eye, you would be able to see its true form clearly then.”

Chapter 35: She-Devil

The moment Lu Yang heard the words “Qilin Immortality Herb,” he felt a shiver run down his spine. Qilin have gone extinct, which means that the Qilin Immortality Herb is also almost extinct.

Only a handful had ever existed since time immemorial. Looking back in time, there were hardly any records of this herb. Some even said that there was only one such herb in the world and that the Qilin Immortality Herb was going through cycles of reincarnation.

An ancient sage once speculated that there was in fact no qilin in the world at all. They were merely figments of people’s imagination. The records of qilin were actually only sightings of Qilin Immortality Herb. Before people opened their heavenly eye, it was easy for them to mistake the Qilin Immortality Herb as qilin, just like how Lu Yang did.

“Grandpa Ba told me to come and loosen the soil.”

“Oh, so you’re here to loosen the soil. You know elemental spells?” The little herb kings appeared very excited. There’s finally someone here to do the work.

Lu Yang had a complicated expression. “I can’t really say that I’m proficient with it. I learned it by accident, so I’m not sure if it’s considered an elemental spell. But I can definitely burrow into the ground.” Lu Yang felt that he was performing a spatial spell, just that it had traits similar to that of an elemental spell.

“It doesn’t matter whether it’s counted as an elemental spell. It’s fine as long as you can burrow into the ground,” the Time Terminus Flower said offhandedly. After the earthworm couple went on leave, it would often hear the various complaints from the herbs. They would grumble about the soil being too hard which made it uncomfortable for growing and the soil being unbreathable, making them want to pull their roots out for fresh air and to bathe in the sunlight. This put the distressed little herb kings on the spot.

But now, the problem could be solved.

Extremely few people knew about the existence of herb kings. Lu Yang was one of them before coming; he didn’t recognize a single one of them. The little herb kings’ medicinal properties were out of this world. If they appeared in the outer world, it would be sufficient to drive the formidable cultivators crazy.

Wait, I actually do recognize one of them.

Lu Yang recognized the sunflower in the Time Terminus Flower’s hand. The petals opened and closed, its black skin shedding off and revealing the jade-white pulp that was the herb king’s nutrients.

The herb king was eating sunflower seeds.

And the seeds were strewn across the ground.

I wonder if this is counted as cannibalism.

“Oh, this is called Sunflower.” The Time Terminus Flower noticed Lu Yang’s gaze and introduced.

Lu Yang answered in his heart, I know that.

The herb kings weren’t big, so rather than saying that they were eating sunflower seeds, it looked more like they were hugging the seeds and gnawing on them. He could see that the Time Terminus Flower was enjoying its meal.

“Terminus King, you’re littering again. How many times have I said that we are plants and that we shouldn’t follow how humans eat seeds? The seed coat is also edible!” The Qilin Immortality Herb was enraged, berating the Time Terminus Flower for foolishly imitating humans.

The Time Terminus Flower continued doing things its own way. “I was the one who planted sunflowers. I can eat it however I like. What can you do with me? Hmph!”

His words pushed the Qilin Immortality Herb over the edge. The latter pounced toward the Time Terminus Flower, and the two little herb kings began to tussle, rolling over each other but completely not posing any threat.

The ginseng doll and Three-Leaf Starry Grass were already used to such sights. They were focused on clamoring for Lu Yang to demonstrate how to burrow into the ground. “Ignore them. They’ll stop fighting when they get tired.”

Outside the wooden hut, Lu Yang noticed a towering tree. Its roots were as thick as two thighs, and it was in high spirits, its dense foliage of leaves rustling persistently.

“Dao Enlightenment Tree?” Lu Yang was surprised. Even if he returned to his normal size, the Dao Enlightenment Tree could still be considered as blocking out the sky. Even a dozen people wouldn’t be enough to completely hug it.

There was a flow of charming energy circulating it, its rustling leaves sounding like Daoist sounds. It was as if all Dao had converged into one, shaping the Dao Enlightenment Tree to be mysterious, solemn, and inviolable.

“This is the Dao Enlightenment Tree I told you about. We all call it Tree King. It's not a stretch to say that its talent in Daoist arts is unparalleled.”

The leaves of the Dao Enlightenment Tree can help one be enlightened by the Dao. If the tree itself becomes a demon spirit, their talent in cultivation must be ridiculous. Lu Yang couldn’t imagine.

The little herb kings might appear weak, but they each had their own unique magical abilities and were not to be looked down upon. If they didn’t have life-saving skills, they couldn’t have survived up until now just based on the compassion of humans alone.

The big tree laughed and cursed, “Ginseng King, you bastard, overpraising me to my death again. If I’m unparalleled, then what kind of talent does that she-devil have?”

“Who is the she-devil?” Lu Yang was curious. Judging by the little herb kings’ tone, she didn’t seem like a good person.

“Other than Little Ba, only the she-devil can come into the herb garden. The she-devil is incredibly powerful. None of us can defeat her. She takes whatever she wants, and no herb can stop her!”

“A few of my old ginseng roots were broken off by her. It was so painful that I had to lie in bed for several days,” the ginseng doll chided the she-devil for her outrageous behavior.

“She also plucked a few stars off my leaves. Look, aren’t these few stars dimmer than the rest? I don’t know how long it’ll take for it to grow back!”

According to the herb kings’ descriptions, the she-devil was laden with innumerable evil deeds and was the common enemy of all herbs.

“What’s even more infuriating is that she said she would take these things back for bathing. Can you imagine? She actually bathed together with our body parts. How perverted!

“By the way, I heard Little Ba say that the she-devil has a fairly high position in your Dao-Seeking Sect. Her name is Yun Zhi.”

Lu Yang, “...”

He realized that he was not surprised by the answer. Is it Big Senior Sister’s problem or my problem?

Lu Yang laughed awkwardly, unsure what to say. “About that, the person all of you mentioned, I think I know her. She’s my Big Senior Sister.”

The Dao Enlightenment Tree laughed heartily, dismissing it. “That’s nothing. Who doesn’t know that all you Dao-Seeking Sect disciples call her Big Senior Sister. Did you think that we’d take our anger out on you just because you said that you’re her junior brother? You underestimate us herb kings. We have lived for so many years. How could we possibly care about a mere human?”

Upon seeing how reasonable the Dao Enlightenment Tree was, Lu Yang heaved a sigh of relief. “That’s great. It seems like it doesn’t matter even if I share the same shifu as her.”

The Dao Enlightenment Tree’s laughter abruptly stopped. Even the gentle breeze halted in its steps, and the rustling of the leaves ceased.

The ginseng doll waved its ginseng roots, its composed expression cracking to show a trace of a sinister smile.

The Three-Leaf Starry Grass had the stars on its leaves swirling like a volcano about to erupt and exact its revenge.

Killing intent had suffused the air in an instant.

Lu Yang calmly explained, “Don’t resort to violence first. Did you really think that I’m on the she-devil’s side just because I’m her junior brother?”

The ginseng doll stared at Lu Yang suspiciously, waving its roots more slowly. “Is that not the case?”

The Dao Enlightenment Tree and the Three-Leaf Starry Grass also temporarily refrained from attacking.

“Absolutely not!” Lu Yang firmly declared. His hands were tightly clenched into fists as he revealed a pained expression of him recounting unbearable memories. “That she-devil’s behavior is so egregious that it makes my blood boil and my hair stand on end! You are not the only victims of her bullying; even I have received immeasurable suffering! I may seem to be leading an illustrious life with a bright future on the surface, but who can I confide in about the torment I’ve endured?!”

Chapter 36: Not A Single Reassuring One

“Big Senior Sister may appear to be placid, but she’s actually temperamental. It’s just that she never shows it on her face. As the saying goes, accompanying a monarch is like accompanying a tiger. Staying by her side is no different from being with a tiger!

“She’s indeed a rare beauty or even the most beautiful woman I’ve ever seen, but you can’t judge a book by its cover. Can you imagine? Every meal, she would make me gnaw on lots of broken limbs of wild beasts and remains of plants. When it was late at night, she would even make me completely soak myself in water filled with the corpses of spirit medicinal herbs, claiming that this could help with strengthening my body!

“Another time, I wanted to learn spatial spells for more convenient travel in the future, but she taught me how to turn small instead, gripping me with her hand and literally having me toyed within her palm!”

Lu Yang denounced all of Yun Zhi’s “atrocities,” quickly resonating with the little herb kings and gaining their sympathy.

The ginseng doll couldn’t help but propose, “In that case, let’s coordinate to act from both inside and outside. You’ll be our inside agent while we’ll be your external support. Let’s rebel against that she-devil right now!”

Lu Yang was taken aback and hurriedly dissuaded, “Absolutely not! We still need to consider this at length. As the number one disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect, Big Senior Sister’s cultivation is unfathomably high. I’m afraid that just the few of us won’t be a match for her.” He calmly analyzed, “For our safety, we could wait until my cultivation has reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Our chances will be better that way. Then everyone can act together and retaliate against Big Senior Sister, taking her down in one move! At that time, everyone can exact their revenge and settle their scores. Wouldn’t that be better?”

The little herb kings were impressed. As expected of humans, they’re very thorough. “We initially thought that your intelligence was inferior to ours, but to think that you came up with such a meticulous plan! It looks like your intelligence is comparable to ours!”

With a common enemy, Lu Yang and the little herb kings soon became good buddies. It was a cacophony of noises as they shouted out their intentions to attack the she-devil.

With Lu Yang joining us little herb kings, we’ve become even stronger like tigers that have grown wings. Victory is already within our reach, just like us reaching into our pockets!

At the entrance of the herb garden, Grandpa Ba watched how Lu Yang inspired the others with his plan through a water mirror. He slowly let out a sigh. Yun Zhi had instructed him to keep an eye on Lu Yang so that nothing happens to him. However, if an accident did occur, he should inform her right away.

Is this current situation considered an accident? If I really tell Yun Zhi, it may become an accident even if it wasn’t one.

“The youngsters nowadays...why is there not a single reassuring one?”

“After all that talk, I realized that I haven’t demonstrated my spell to you.” Lu Yang stretched himself and prepared to cast the Shrinking Earth spell. Getting into a diving pose, he directly jumped into the earth.

The Dao Enlightenment Tree had a similar reaction to Yun Zhi, marveling at the sight. Despite having lived so long, it hadn’t seen any spell like it before. On the surface, it seems to be a spatial spell like Shrinking Earth To Inches. But when it’s actually applied, it resembles an elemental spell.

He can already cast an unprecedented spell at such a young age. He’s truly a spell genius.

Now that Lu Yang was entirely in his element with Shrinking Earth, he could also pull off diving, breaststroke, butterfly stroke, and even freestyle. Watching how he burrowed in and out of the soil smoothly could easily mislead one into hallucinating that the soil was actually water.

After the Qilin Immortality Herb and Time Terminus Flower were done fighting, the ginseng doll and Three-Leaf Starry Grass described their tragic experiences under the claws of the she-devil.

“Us herb kings finally have an undercover agent planted among the humans!” The four little herb kings sat on the branch of the Dao Enlightenment Tree and applauded, finding Lu Yang very powerful.

A strange cry emitted from Lu Yang. Pushing off with his legs, he jumped high up. He extended his arms, forming a cross shape and spinning 360 degrees in the air. However, with a grunt, he landed face-first on the ground; he had gotten dizzy from spinning mid-air.

Attempt to act cool failed.

The little herb kings hastily carried Lu Yang up in a frenzy. Such injuries were just superficial external wounds to Foundation Establishment cultivators; it wouldn’t take long for them to heal.

Seeing that Lu Yang really knew how to loosen the soil, the little herb kings took out a map of the herb garden, asking Lu Yang to follow the sequence when burrowing into the ground.

“This area of herbs have roots that run very deep—they can reach up to the third layer of soil. You have to be careful not to touch their roots and cause a misunderstanding. My suggestion is to burrow into the soil and loosen it around three to five meters underground. This is the safe zone. Herbs in other regions have roots reaching from half a meter to two meters.”

Lu Yang was curious. “What happens if we touch the root?”

The ginseng doll replied solemnly, “We would think that you have a foot fetish.”

Question marks were almost popping out of Lu Yang’s head.

The Time Terminus Flower intervened, “There are so many perverts among you humans. They like to eat our plant foot skin with beer, saying that it tastes good. For that, they even grow large quantities of it.”

”What's the plant you’re talking about?”

“Peanuts.”

Lu Yang couldn’t really keep up with the little herb kings’ train of thoughts. Fortunately, he didn’t dwell on his topic longer and started to follow the digging route provided by the ginseng doll.

The ginseng doll was tired from watching the earthworm couple, but it found it entertaining to watch humans burrowing into the ground. It ran behind Lu Yang and followed him closely.

The little herb kings were also capable of traversing underground, but their method was different from Lu Yang’s—they merged with the earth instead of pushing apart the soil like Lu Yang.

The soil in areas Lu Yang passed by became soft, just right for the little herb kings.

The Dao Enlightenment Tree watched them having fun and sighed. Sadly, trees can't burrow into the ground. It then looked up at the sun and found it scorching hot, sighing again. “Why am I so tall? I can't even find shade to sit in.”

The Dao Enlightenment Tree felt that the world was full of malice toward it.

The little herb kings followed right behind Lu Yang’s buttocks and played for the whole day. On the way back, they were still frolicking around and giggling, “Boil some water for a bath!”

The Dao Enlightenment Tree had already prepared a wooden bucket filled to the brim with water, drawn from the stream that irrigated the herbs.

A bright light appeared from the Qilin Immortality Herb’s stomach and slowly moved upward. It finally ended at the mouth, causing it to spew out Qilin True Fire.

The Qilin Immortality Herb was just like the real qilin. It was no wonder that the ancient people claimed that they had seen a qilin.

The Qilin True Fire had an extremely high temperature. In a split second, the water was already bubbling. The little herb kings jumped in one after another, closing their eyes as they floated about on the water surface.

Lu Yang found this sight very familiar, as if he had seen something similar in the kitchen before.

Oh, I remember now. This is called medicinal cuisine.[1]

But it's still my first time seeing the ingredients jumping into the pot so enthusiastically.

Soon, medicinal fragrance wafted through the air. Lu Yang inhaled a deep breath and instantly became invigorated, even finding that his cultivation seemed to be on the verge of improving.

“As expected of herb kings. Their medicinal power is really terrifying.”

Lu Yang watched the little herb kings playing in the water and couldn't help but smile helplessly.

I recall Big Senior Sister mentioning that longevity is a poison, a kind of pain and suffering that no ordinary person can endure. Only those with characters beyond a normal person can bear the misery of immortality.

The little herb kings lived through countless ages, witnessing an unimaginable number of major historical events. Those people and matters might have long passed, but only the little herb kings still live.

I'm afraid it's precisely because of their child-like personalities that they can live so long without breaking down.

It's just that...they're too gullible.

1. ”Yaoshan” or medicinal cuisine and medicated food among many other translated names, is part of a branch of the TCM culture of combining medicine and food with medicinal properties, bringing out a delicious yet beneficial meal. Chapter 37: Herb King Spirit Elixir

Under the resplendent night sky, the Dao Enlightenment Tree’s imposing figure blocked out the moonlight. The little herb kings were still playing gleefully in the water, and even Lu Yang joined in the fun. Time seemed to have come to a standstill in front of this harmonious sight.

After the little herb kings were comfortable with their bath, they sprawled out on the ground and ceiling of the wooden hut, snoring loudly as they slept. The Dao Enlightenment Tree didn’t let this time go to waste; it put away the wooden bucket and water, something Lu Yang found puzzling.

“What are you doing?” Lu Yang asked.

The Dao Enlightenment King casually replied, “Oh, this is for Little Ba. He said that their bathwater is worth a lot of money. The Dao-Seeking Sect disciples love to use it.” It shook its branches like someone shrugging, expressing its helplessness toward the behavior of humans.

As a plant, it was hard for it to understand some of humans’ strange actions. I know that humans like to use my hair or what they call leaves to brew tea. They also like to use my skin to prepare meals, claiming that it can improve the fragrance; I think they call it cinnamon or something.

“Oh, by the way, Little Ba even gave the bathwater a nice name. It’s called Herb King Spirit Elixir. I have to give it to you humans. You are much more cultured when it comes to names.”

“Herb King Spirit Elixir?” Lu Yang subconsciously repeated the name, finding it familiar. He soon remembered where he had seen the term before.

Isn’t this the extremely popular Herb King Spirit Elixir on the contribution points rewards board?! The list described the Herb King Spirit Elixir as a precious elixir specially concocted by the higher-ups of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

So this is what they mean by “specially concocted?!”

Lu Yang began to question the various bizarre items on the board. Although the description may seem to have no problems, it doesn’t mean that it really has no problems!

~~~

In the following days, Lu Yang worked diligently to burrow into the ground, all the while hearing the little herb kings chatter incessantly about medicinal knowledge. With that, his days were very fulfilling.

“I remember that there’s an area of Eight-Treasure Lotus Flowers ahead. They’re pink and tender, and they look amazing. Do you want to burrow there and take a look?” the ginseng doll asked from behind Lu Yang.

“... Lotus flowers grow in ponds, right?”

“That’s right.” The ginseng doll nodded matter-of-factly.

“Then if I burrow there, wouldn’t I be diving headfirst into a pond?”

The ginseng doll finally realized. “Oh, you’re right. That makes sense.”

Lu Yang gave up on communicating.

Following the ginseng doll’s directions, Lu Yang burrowed his way through and emerged from the earth. Not far away were the magnificent Eight-Treasure Lotus Flowers. Morning dew condensed on its petals, some dripping into the water and creating gentle ripples. Eight-Treasure Lotus Flowers could help dispel heat and dampness, and it had efficacies in detoxification and nourishing the heart, so it was often used in concocting pills.

“I just don’t know why Eight-Treasure Lotus Flowers have the term ‘Eight-Treasure,’” Lu Yang remarked, recalling the information he saw from the books.

This was an unsolved mystery among pill-concocting masters. Numerous pill-concocting masters wrote books, citing the classics and mentioning various viewpoints. For example, some mentioned that the reason was because Eight-Treasure Lotus Flowers had eight types of efficacies. Others mentioned that the name evolved from Daoist bagua, while there were even those who claimed that “Eight-Treasure” referred to the eight meridians in the human body and that eating more Eight-Treasure Lotus Flowers could open up the Eight Extra Meridians[1].

Lu Yang leaned more toward the first hypothesis that there were eight types of efficacies. I can’t say much about the rest, but at least the first reason sounds reliable.

The ginseng doll asked, “Are you referring to this? I know.”

“You know?”

The ginseng doll crossed its ginseng roots at its hip, smugly replying, “That’s right! Devotee Guyu was the one who discovered the Eight-Treasure Lotus Flowers. At that time, both of us happened to enter an undiscovered secret domain. Fortunately, both of our cultivation were high, so it wasn’t dangerous for us. The two of us played to our hearts’ content in the secret domain. When we got tired, we would rest, eat, and sleep on the spot for the atmosphere.

“When we were eating, Devotee Guyue found a patch of pink lotus flowers that he had never seen before. I asked him how he wanted to name them. He glanced at the Eight-Treasure Congee[2] in this hand and offhandedly suggested that we could just call it Eight-Treasure Lotus Flower.

”Afterward, he took away a few lotus flowers and made them multiply in the outside world, leading to the scale of propagation you see today.”

“Devotee Guyue originally didn’t go by this name. His surname was Hu, so he called himself Devotee Hu. However, his handwriting wasn’t very good. There was once he wrote his surname “Hu” with the components written too far apart, causing people to read it separately as Devotee Guyue.[3]

Little Li husband-and-wife the second were also very affectionate.

Chapter 38: The Farewell Scene Is Rather Moving

Lu Yang was at a loss for words. He simply didn’t know what to make of such a method that challenged morals, ethics, and social norms.

“All’s good as long as the matter is resolved.” He finally managed to force a sentence out.

Lu Yang did as he was told, and Grandpa Ba tapped his jade pendant. “The mission reward of three hundred contribution points is already inside your jade pendant.”

When one works hard, it will pay off. My efforts didn’t go to waste. Three hundred contribution points was considered a big sum for Lu Yang.

That said, although three hundred points may seem like a lot, I can’t seem to even afford the little herb kings’ foot-washing water.

It was clearly written on the rewards board that the Herb King Spirit Elixir was separated into regular and deluxe versions. Based on what Lu Yang had understood, the regular version was the little herb kings’ foot-washing water while the deluxe version was their bathwater.

What the Qilin Immortality Herb said was true. During the past month, the little herb kings had been suppressing the vital energy inside their bodies, fearing that they might knock Lu Yang out. The little herb kings quickly told Lu Yang to move, chasing him away.

The farewell scene was rather “moving.”[1]

One of the Meng Family’s teachings was to discuss matters over a meal. That way, if the conversation went well, the Meng Family would treat, and if things didn’t go well, everyone would split the bill.

“Dear guests, what would you like to drink? We have all kinds of tea here in our teahouse,” a tea waiter[2] was swift to approach them.

“Oh, I said it wrongly. Let’s have a basin of milk tea. I recall that it’s a specialty near the Extreme North.” Noticing the tea waiter’s darkened expression, he hurriedly gestured that he bore no ill intentions.

Soon, the tea waiter carried a hot metal brazier. In it were stir-fried millet, butter, beef jerky, and clotted cream. He then came back again with a pot of milk tea.

Lu Yang and Man Gu exchanged confused looks, so they could only leave it to Meng Jingzhou. The latter first stir-fried the ingredients inside the brazier until the millet turned yellow and gave off a crunchy texture. Then he lifted the pot of milk tea and poured all of it inside the basin. When the milk tea contacted the red-hot iron, it sizzled, and the fragrance of the milk tea wafted out, assaulting one’s nostrils.

Lu Yang took a sip and smacked his lips. It’s salty. The taste is wonderful and quite delicious.
