“Hmm?”

Lu Yang didn’t expect that his bathing in boiling water wasn’t the worst. Big Senior Sister was still too kind to me. It’s a pity that I didn’t get to meet Li Haoran; otherwise we could’ve exchanged our insights on bathing.

When Zhou Lulu arrived at the bustling dining hall, her fervor vanished without a trace. She secretly retreated two steps back, and she spoke as rapidly as a machine gun, “Junior Brother Lu, the food in the dining hall is of high quality and reasonably priced. Go ahead and buy it yourself.”

Before the last word left her mouth, she had already run off. Lu Yang didn’t even see how she disappeared.

He sighed. Looks like I can only count on myself.

“Braised fish bones in soy sauce, freshly made braised fish bones in soy sauce! The best choice for cutting down trees and humans. Everyone who has used them says that they’re great!”

“Shaobing, fresh meat shaobing fresh out of the oven. They won’t break even with punches and kicks!”

“Come and take a look! Noodles that are even harder than steel and bones, an essential for binding people. They can’t break free once bound. Purchase now and get a complimentary binding tutorial!”

The dining hall was like a food market in the mortal world where the vendors would hawk their own food. The only difference was that the dining hall was much noisier than a marketplace; the vendors were of high cultivation and had louder voices.

Lu Yang noticed a senior male disciple holding a braised fish bone that looked like a sharp blade. Just a light scrape would result in a deep wound, as if bitten by a ferocious shark.

The senior male disciple promoted enthusiastically, “Junior Brother, would you like a fish bone? This is from a fish demon in the Blue Wave Pool, and it was at the Apex Foundation Establishment Stage, so the fish bones it left behind are very sturdy. It took me a very long time before I finally crafted these few bones. This can be used as a weapon in combat and food when hungry.” Crunch. He bit down on a fish bone.

I have no idea how he trained his teeth.

Lu Yang checked out the very useful fish bone then glanced at the price.

Right, I can’t afford it.

Seeing Lu Yang’s apologetic smile, the male disciple didn’t force him and continued promoting to others.

Lu Yang saw another senior male disciple putting his hand directly into the pot of oil to take out the youtiao and drain the oil.

“Junior Brother, do you want one? There are ones suitable for Foundation Establishment and Golden Core respectively. The Foundation Establishment ones only cost one hundred and fifty contribution points.”

In terms of price, it was indeed cheaper than the Mountain Quaking Hammer on the redemption list. The latter cost two hundred and seventy contribution points while the youtiao only cost one hundred fifty contribution points, almost half of it.

“My youtiao’s strength isn’t only its sturdiness. It comprises three layers of covert force. A single strike combined with the three layers of hidden force could unleash tremendous power, delivering a surprise blow to the enemy.

“If you are hungry and want to eat it, that’s also fine. It has a long shelf life.” The senior male disciple even took a bite. The three layers of covert force blasted inside his mouth, but other than his mouth bulging for a moment, nothing else happened.

“Senior Brother, I’m new here, so there are some things I don’t understand. Why can our youtiao be both a weapon and food? Can you really bite through them?”

The senior male disciple discerned Lu Yang’s cultivation. Since this junior brother is at Foundation Establishment, he’s definitely from the newest batch. It’s normal for a newcomer to ask such a question.

“This is a way to train and verify the results of our training in refining the body. In body refinement, one must refine the internal organs, muscles and bones while also refining the outer skin and seven orifices. Only then can they be counted as a true physique cultivator. Apart from that, the teeth are also an indispensable part.

“I heard that some physique cultivators only refine their muscle, bones, and skin to the extreme. Just a brute collision from them would even lead to mountains shaking. They can be considered excellent. However, others are very troubled when they face these impenetrable physique cultivators, so they thought of a solution.”

“What solution?”

“They used body transformation spells like Size At Will to shrink their body and attack these physique cultivators from the inside. As these physique cultivators didn’t reinforce their organs, they are very susceptible to these kinds of attacks.

“These people are not considered as true physique cultivators, or they can be called unorthodox physique cultivators.” The senior male disciple clinked his teeth, producing the sound of metal clanging.

People like them who crafted artifacts were considered half a physique cultivator. Although their body’s strength couldn’t be compared to a true physique cultivator, their bodies had been refined internally and externally.

“Ordinary cultivators use magical treasures as weapons, while a physique cultivator’s strongest weapon is their body. Since it’s their strongest weapon, eating youtiao isn’t a hard thing.”

Lu Yang finally understood. The food in the dining hall has strong functionalities that were divided into two main purposes—selling them as weapons to cultivators like me who aren’t physique cultivators and selling them as food to physique cultivators.

“Meng Jingzhou became a disciple of Third Elder and is a bona fide physique cultivator, so he should be able to bite through it,” Lu Yang murmured to himself.

He bought a youtiao and swung it twice, finding it heavy and compact.

1. The original Chinese text stated that Li Haoran got used to it, but Zhou Lulu wondered if it’s not that he has gotten used to it but rather that he has been cooked. There’s a double meaning to the “cooked” here—it can also mean to be familiar with something. ☜

Chapter 41: Setting Off

Lu Yang went to the stall selling shaobing again. The seller was a senior female disciple. She leavened the dough, let it rest, kneaded it, and tossed it until a shape formed. It was unknown how long she had taken to achieve this level of proficiency.

The female disciple broke the dough into smaller balls. With her hands, wrists, arms, and body, she exerted all her strength to roll the dough into the shape of a shaobing. Her movements seemed to secretly follow some principle. Rather than simply kneading dough, it was also a method for training the body’s coordination.

Then the senior female disciple placed the shaobing dough on the forging table and struck it vigorously with a huge hammer, producing deafening bangs and sparks that burned small holes in the ground. The unfinished shaobing was quenched and tempered, the cold water instantly boiling and bubbling up. Soon, a shaobing was ready.

Lu Yang felt that he had broadened his horizons. The Hundred Refinements Peak is really full of ideas—they integrated food and weapon crafting so seamlessly.

“I’ll have one shaobing.”

Lu Yang came across many interesting and wondrous things in the dining hall. The stuff here is really cheap. If not for my limited contribution points, I’d really want to buy everything.

~~~

Early the next morning, Lu Yang met up with the two at the entrance of the Dao-Seeking Sect as they had agreed.

“You’re the only one left.” Meng Jingzhou waved to Lu Yang. Behind him was a horse carriage, the same one that had taken them to the Dao-Seeking Sect. The old horse was also still the same old horse.

The only difference was that the third passenger had changed from Yun Zhi to Man Gu.

Man Gu was diligent in his studies, studying even while waiting. His wide scholarly robes covered his muscles, making him look the part of a tall and burly scholar.

“We don’t have to take the flying vessel?” Lu Yang had already braced himself to ride the flying vessel.

Although his Shrinking Earth To Inches was convenient, it was not as fast as the flying vessel. Thus, he decided to temporarily give up on learning Shrinking Earth To Inches and instead focus on Shrinking Earth and To Inches respectively.

Meng Jingzhou patted the horse carriage, pleased with himself. “This horse carriage of mine is a rare magical treasure. It contains a spatial array, so even though it may feel slow to us when we sit inside, people on the outside will see that it is traveling as fast as a flying vessel.”

That did make sense. The Meng Family was far away in the capital city. Since Meng Jingzhou had relied on a horse carriage to travel all the way to the Dao-Seeking Sect, if the old horse had trudged through the journey, even a year wouldn’t be enough for it to reach the Dao-Seeking Sect.

On its way to the Dao-Seeking Sect, the carriage had activated an array to speed up until it could fly. Only when it got near to the sect did it turn off the array and slow down as a sign of respect to the Dao-Seeking Sect. By the time Lu Yang saw the carriage, it had already slowed down.

The three of them boarded the carriage, yet the interior of the carriage was as spacious as ever. Only now did Lu Yang understand the true value of this carriage.

“Speaking of which, where are we going? What’s the mission?”

“Oh, I didn’t tell you? We are going to a place called Qinghuai Commandery. I'll let Brother Man Gu tell you the specifics. After all, he was the one who found this mission.”

Man Gu inserted a bookmark and closed his book before proceeding to elaborate unhurriedly, “This was when I was out doing a mission. I heard it from a passenger on the flying vessel. He’s a traveling merchant leader and knows many things ordinary people don’t. He told me about a story circulating among them traveling merchants, and it has some credibility.

“Between Qinghuai Commandery and Yanjiang Commandery lies an enormous mountain range. If traveling merchants want to pass through this mountain range, they would need a local hunter as their guide. However, a terrifying entity has appeared in the mountain forests, forcing the hunters to leave the forest they rely on for survival...”

~~~

Night descended, and the wild-growing tree branches blocked out the moonlight. Thunder roared, and rain poured, turning the ground into a muddy swamp with no safe space for one’s feet. Seven to eight people were bound together through ropes tied around their waists, preventing someone from accidentally slipping down the mountain and getting lost.

The torrential rain drowned out the sounds of their surroundings. Even if someone fell and hollered at the top of their lungs, it would be hard to hear them. These people were clad in straw raincoats. They leaned on mountaineering sticks and carried wicker baskets, cautious with every step they took lest they tread into a deep pit. The bone-chilling rain had made them disheveled. Whenever they raised their head, the dense rain curtain would obstruct their view, so they could only follow the old hunter right in front.

“Watch your step, the mountain path is very slippery on rainy days!”

“Don’t stop even if you’re tired. Push through, we're almost there. If you stop now, it’ll be hard to get going again!”

“I... I really can’t...Save me! I’m falling!” Someone slipped, and without anything to hold onto for support, they slid toward the precipice beside the mountain path.

Sensing a tug from the other end of the rope, the traveling merchants realized that someone had fallen behind. They instantly halted and scrambled to pull the person back up.

“A’yue, hold on to the rope tightly. We’ll pull together!”

“I have no strength left.” A’yue dangled by the cliff, the coarse rope around his waist being the only thing preventing him from falling. He was tired and hungry, unable to muster any strength to even climb up the rope.

The old hunter was experienced, calmly directing the group while personally pulling A’yue up.

“You guys hug the big tree. Don’t let the seven of us also slide down.

“The rest of you, wind the rope around your wrist. On the count of three, everyone will pull together!”

“One, two, three, pull!”

“One, two, three, pull!”

After expending their strength, everyone finally pulled A’yue up. Everyone was originally exhausted, and now they couldn’t even stand firm.

The old hunter still hadn’t let down his guard. He nervously checked on A’yue’s condition. “A’yue, how did you slide down? Did you feel like someone pushed you?”

A’yue shook his head blankly, unsure why the old hunter had asked such a question. Of course, I had slipped on my own. Surely no one would try to harm me, right?

“Old Sun, what do you mean by that?” Qi Wu, the leader of the traveling merchants asked. He vaguely detected that something was amiss from the question.

The old hunter shook his head, pointing at the dilapidated temple ahead. “Let’s hurry along first. We’ll talk when we arrive at the Mountain God Temple.”

With the relentless downpour, it was indeed not the right environment for discussing matters. Qi Wu nodded and uttered a few words of encouragement, urging everyone to quickly seek shelter from the rain in the Mountain God Temple.

Once everyone arrived, they didn’t bother caring about appearances. Removing their straw raincoats, they plopped down on the ground panting. Then, they quickly checked their wicker baskets to see if anything had been damaged by the rain. If these baskets were ruined by the rain, their whole trip would have gone down the drain, and they would be totally unable to recover their losses.

“Phew, fortunately, we wrapped them with waterproof cloth beforehand. Big Brother Qi, I have to give it to you for having such foresight.”

The Mountain God Temple was not particularly grand, but it was spacious. Three old mountain god statues covered in dust stood in the center, their surroundings filled with dirt and feces. The memorial tablets written with the mountain gods’ names were missing, and the offerings had long been eaten by wild animals. Even the two main doors had disappeared, and the wrecked windows let the frigid wind in.

Everyone didn’t mind it much. For them, any shelter from the rain was a good place.

Qi Wu took out some goods from his wicker basket as offerings for the three mountain gods, thanking them for letting them use the temple for shelter. The three mountain gods were crudely sculpted from clay, but they could still be distinguished. The mountain god in the middle wielded a gentleman sword[1] with a righteous expression. The two mountain gods flanking him represented literature arts and martial arts. One donned a scholarly robe and held a book, demonstrating literature while the other exuded a pure upright aura, a symbol of the military. The statues were arranged according to their ranks.

“Mountain gods, please bless us to have a safe journey.” Qi Wu couldn’t shake off the feeling that the three mountain gods had much spirituality to them, almost as if they were alive.

Chapter 42: Legends Often Deviate From Reality

After offering tribute to the mountain gods, Qi Wu quickly joined the others who were gathered together. Drenched from head to toe, everyone shuddered as a cold breeze blew past.

“We’ll get sick at this rate.” The old hunter walked to a corner and carried a bundle of firewood, flashing his large teeth as he smiled. “Us hunters will occasionally seek shelter from the rain here, so we left some firewood here in case of unexpected weather like today.”

Qi Wu was elated. “That is much appreciated.”

The old hunter waved it off, “It’s nothing. Life in the mountains is about you helping me and me helping you. When the rain stops tomorrow, we just have to collect some firewood and put it back.”

Everyone swiftly piled up the firewood on the ground where traces of a fire remained. Qi Wu lit up a stick with a fire talisman and placed it within the dry firewood. He gently blew and fanned it until a fire slowly ignited.

Watching the flames dance and feeling its warmth, someone heaved out a sigh of relief. “We’re finally alive again.”

“Big Brother Qi, do you want a yellow rice biscuit or a white rice biscuit?”

“What about one of each?”

One person distributed the rations. After everyone received their portion, they placed it near the fire to roast. As the aroma wafted into the air, A’yue took out a can of soy sauce pickles so that everyone could spread it on their biscuits. One bite filled their mouths with a salty fragrance.

“A’yue, your skills in preparing soy sauce pickles are really decent. Why not set up a soy sauce pickles store? You don’t have to join us as traveling merchants then.”

A’yue simply smiled and didn’t make any comment.

Reminded of the incident earlier, Qi Wu asked, “Old Sun, why did you ask whether A’yue was pushed by someone?”

It was the first time for Qi Wu’s group to be entering the mountains. They wanted to cross the mountain range and reach Qinghuai Commandery on the other side to sell their goods. After searching for a long time, they finally found a local old hunter as their guide.

The old hunter’s expression turned grave. “Have you heard of tiger-henchman ghosts[1]?”

Qi Wu and the others similarly became solemn. Having traveled extensively, they naturally knew of some supernatural stories. Someone even exclaimed, “Are you referring to the tiger-henchman ghosts from the saying ‘acting as a henchman to a tiger’?” [2]

The old hunter nodded, lowering his voice, “This mountain is called Pine Mountain. Around ten years ago, a hunter came into the mountain to hunt but vanished subsequently, leaving only a shoe behind. At that time, some people claimed that a tiger demon had come to the mountain and eaten that hunter.

“Initially, the people were unwilling to believe that. They had been living here for generations, so how could it be possible for a tiger demon to appear? However, as time passed, someone mentioned that their hunter dog would bark in a certain direction when hunting. When he looked in the same direction, he was frightened until his body went stiff.

“There was a brightly colored fierce tiger, at least four meters long. The fierce tiger pounced toward the hunter dog, and he fled for his life right away. Fortunately, that fierce tiger didn’t chase him!

“Some people also noticed that people would go missing from time to time, so they reported the situation to Qinghuai Commandery. After the officials learned of the matter, they asked me to look for Yanjiang Commandery, saying that Pine Mountain was close to Yanjiang Commandery and that this should be under their jurisdiction since we would be sending our game to Yanjiang Commandery.

“However, upon arriving in Yanjiang Commandery, the officials there said that Pine Mountain was part of Qinghuai Commandery and should be under Qinghuai Commandery’s jurisdiction.

“After going back and forth multiple times, both parties sent two cultivators to search for traces of the tiger demon in Pine Mountain. However, they didn't even find a single tiger hair in ten days. Those two cultivators thought that we were playing with them and wasting their time, so we explained that the tiger demon could be purposely hiding from them and didn't dare to come out. They didn't listen to our explanations and left in a huff.

“We then went to look for the authorities again, but they no longer bothered with us. Left with no choice, most people left Pine Mountain to seek another way out. Only a few of us old folks who know nothing else but hunting stayed behind.

“Afterward, we realized that we would encounter those missing travelers when we went hunting. These travelers would suddenly disappear in one moment and appear in another, even pushing you. Sometimes, when I take people into the mountains, those travelers would pretend to bump into us by coincidence and ask whether they can tag along since we're all going in the same direction. How could I possibly dare? I quickly led my group away.

“The older generations mentioned that there was something called tiger-henchman ghosts. After a tiger demon kills a person, they would become a tiger-henchman ghost and help the tiger demon find their prey by tricking people to some place where they are turned into new tiger-henchman ghosts.

“However, dealing with tiger henchman ghosts is still manageable. As long as you reject their requests, they won't do anything to you.”

Realization dawned upon Qi Wu. With how big this mountain forest is, there should be many hunters, yet we only found a few after such a long time, and these hunters are even staying together.

So, it's because of the tiger demon.

Noticing A’yue’s hesitation, Qi Wu prompted him, “A’yue, just speak your mind.”

A’yue was originally embarrassed to ask, but since his boss had spoken, he decided not to hold back anymore. “I have a question. Are there female tiger-henchman ghosts? Are they beautiful? Can they seduce? Will they suck a man’s yang energy? Is it possible that she and I begin a forbidden romance and run away from the tiger demon’s murderous pursuit and roam the jianghu?”

With every question that left Ayue’s mouth, a question mark would pop up above everyone else’s heads.

A’yue scratched his head abashedly upon seeing everyone’s reactions. “This is how it’s always written in the novels I read and Chinese ghost stories[3], something about a beautiful female ghost and a human’s romantic entanglements and the likes.”

Qi Wu fell silent for a moment before patting A’yue’s shoulder. “You should read fewer books.” He then turned to the old hunter. “Old Sun, why didn’t you report this matter to the Five Great Immortal Sects? As upholders of the righteous path, they wouldn’t turn a blind eye.”

“Five Great Immortal Sects?” The old hunter was bemused. I have never heard of this term.

“They include righteous sects such as the Dao-Seeking Sect and the Hanging Monastery, and they are the five strongest sects on the continent.”

“I seem to have heard of this name before,” said the old hunter with uncertainty. I’m not sure where I’ve heard it before. It could’ve been in the teahouse below the mountains, the travelers who entered the mountains, when I was younger or after I got old.

I can’t remember clearly anymore.

In fact, the common folk barely knew anything about cultivators, only joining in for the gossip and fun. Moreover, it was too easy for a story to become warped after being passed on by word of mouth. By the time it reached the civilians’ ears, it would have become poles apart from the true story and no longer credible.

For example, Qi Wu once heard that the Dao-Seeking Sect’s name was an allusion to the boundless path to an immortal and asking the heavens for seeking the Dao. Cultivation was also about cultivating one’s heart and mind. It required one to constantly question themselves which path they were pursuing, whether it was the righteous or diabolic path, so that they do not forget their true self and original aspirations.

The source of this content is freёnovelkiss.com.

When Qi Wu encountered a Dao-Seeking Sect disciple who seemed to go by the name of Dai Bufan, he asked the latter how the Dao-Seeking Sect got its name. Qi Wu still remembered Dai Bufan’s answer even until now.

“Oh, this question? Well, I’ll have to start with our sect’s founding ancestor, Innate Daoist. In order to find an area with favorable feng shui, he spent a large sum to invite someone from the Heaven Strategy Sect to calculate the position. Finally, he located a prime land that accumulated feng shui in all eight directions. He even said that to ensure the sect’s longevity, it needed to be established at a specific place and time.

“However, our founder was someone with no sense of direction. Despite the clear markers, he still got lost, so he could only seek the way from an old farmer. Only then did he find the sect’s location in time.

“To thank the old farmer, our founder named the sect the ‘Dao-Seeking Sect.’”[4]

Chapter 43: Your Mountain God Grandfather

“That means that this Dao-Seekinger Sect is very powerful?” the old hunter asked.

“No, it’s the Dao-Seeking Sect,” Qi Wu corrected the old hunter’s pronunciation. “When we go to Qinghuai Commandery tomorrow, we will write a letter to the Five Great Immortal Sects to ask for help.” Qi Wu had asked about the procedure during his meeting with Dai Bufan.

Back then, he was still lamenting about how the local officials with hardly any cultivation were aloof, finding themselves to be above the rest. He didn’t expect that immortal sect disciples who were detached from the mortal world would be more affable. However, Qi Wu didn’t know about Dai Bufan’s position in the sect and thought that he was only an ordinary disciple. Had he known Dai Bufan’s true identity and cultivation, he probably wouldn’t just be lamenting like he was now.

The old hunter was overjoyed and hurriedly thanked Qi Wu and the others. He even offered to waive their travel expenses if they could really deal with the tiger demon once and for all, but Qi Wu was quick to decline. It wasn’t that they didn’t want to save money but rather because they weren’t sure if the old hunter was just being polite or actually sincere.

“I’m sorry, but I got caught in the rain. Could I stay here for the night?” A graceful figure emerged from the curtain of rain. She donned a cyan dress, and her brows carried a trace of sorrow, making people involuntarily agree to her request.

Everyone turned their heads to A’yue. Speak of the devil, a female ghost really came as soon as you said it! Did you jinx it?!

Updated from frёewebnoѵēl.com.

“No!” Qi Wu immediately refused the young woman’s request. We are in the middle of nowhere with not even a village or shops nearby. All of a sudden, a pretty woman appears in the mountain forest. Recalling the old hunter’s words, he couldn’t help but be suspicious.

Most importantly, this woman is dry! It’s like a deluge out there, so how could she be dry?

The girl in cyan was slightly annoyed. Although the group looked educated, she felt that their words lacked decorum. “You are so unreasonable. Let’s not mention that this mountain god temple has no owner and that all of you are simply seeking shelter here, it’s also pouring outside. Are you honestly going to let a girl like me keep maintaining a spell just to protect myself from the rain?”

“Spell? You’re a cultivator?” Qi Wu cautiously asked. Most cultivators were amiable toward mortals, but there was no telling what the other party might do if provoked.

He began to hesitate.

On the other hand, the old hunter’s attitude was firm. Based on his many years of living experience in the mountain forest, he felt that there was definitely something wrong with the girl, but his tone became much more tactful. “Esteemed cultivator, you’re a cultivator but also a girl. If you stay with eight men in a temple, it wouldn’t be good for your reputation.

“How about this? To the north is a mountain path, and halfway up there is a temporary wooden hut built by us hunters. This distance should be not more than a few steps for an expert like yourself.” The old hunter was telling the truth. There was in fact a wooden hut, but it couldn't accommodate so many of them, which was why he had brought the group to the Mountain God Temple to seek shelter instead.

The girl in green contemplated for a bit and felt that the old hunter's words made sense. As a woman, although I don't care about trivial details when I wander the jianghu, there's no reason to stay in this tattered temple when I have a better option.

After the girl left, everyone let out a long sigh of relief. They had been scared that the girl might transform into a ferocious tiger and devour them.

“Alright, let's go to sleep and recharge. We still have to wake up early tomorrow to continue on our way. I really don't want to come to this awful place a second time.” Qi Wu was yawning, his eyes still droopy.

He originally wanted to sleep with his head facing inward, but he would be facing the Mountain God statue. He couldn't shake off the feeling that something was amiss with the Mountain God statue. Not daring to get too close, he could only ask everyone to have their heads face the door while sleeping.

After arranging for pairs to take turns keeping watch for the night, the rest went to sleep. After they slipped into slumber, the Mountain God statue’s eyes rolled, turning downward to stare at everyone.

But no one noticed.

~~~

A’yue yawned, his eyes still blurry, as if he could fall back to sleep any moment. He was part of the first pair to be on night watch. “So tired, how I wish I could sleep.”

“Just hold on for a bit. They’ve already said that it isn't safe on this mountain ...”

“Right, I can't sleep. I'm still waiting for the female ghost to attack me in the night.”

“You look average. Haven’t you read in the books that female ghosts like the handsome ones? I should be the one getting ambushed instead.”

“The female ghosts like scholars. You've only studied for a few days. They like well-read people like me.”

The two people’s debate on the non-existent female ghost became increasingly intense, and they also became more awake.

Suddenly, a low roar rumbled. Even the curtain of rainfall and thunder couldn't drown out the roar. Both of them immediately shuddered.

Just when they wondered if they were hallucinating, another roar resounded in the air. And this time, it was closer!

“It's that tiger demon!” The two exchanged glances, seeing the fear in each other’s eyes.

“Everyone, get up! There's a demon!” A’yue hurriedly hollered.

The rest were jolted awake from their sleep. With their weapons tightly grasped, they stared fixedly outside the temple. Beads of cold sweat kept tumbling down from their foreheads, and their legs couldn't stop trembling.

The roar vanished, but it was replaced by heavy breathing. From the sound of it, it was easy to imagine how colossal its owner was.

A dark figure appeared in the rain, continuing to grow larger. Everyone was on tenterhooks and kept shivering.

The gigantic head of a tiger passed through the rain and extended toward the Mountain God Temple. Qi Wu could even count the individual strands of hair on the tiger’s head!

The tiger demon walked into the temple, and everyone's clothes were drenched in sweat. This is actually a four-meter-tall tiger! Pushing on its hind legs, the tiger demon could stand upright.

“Old Sun, what do we do now?” Qi Wu asked softly. We definitely can't beat this tiger demon with the wooden rods in our hands.

To everyone's surprise, the old hunter walked toward the tiger demon and bowed. “Lord Tiger, please enjoy your meal.”

“Mmm, good job,” the tiger demon spoke. It was unclear what cultivation it was at.

Qi Wu’s eyes widened in wrath, wishing he could tear the old hunter into smithereens. That girl in cyan wasn't a tiger-henchman ghost.

It was the old hunter beside us all along!

The tiger demon revealed a human-like smile and mocked, “I initially didn't want to eat you since there's too many of you. If all of you die, it'll attract the attention of the outside world. But you left me with no choice. To think you wanted to report me to the Five Great Immortal Sects. In that case, I can't leave you alive!”

The tiger demon pressed the old hunter down with a paw. “And you, you just can't stop talking, insisting on telling some story. Now, you even need me to turn up and clean up your mess. Do you want me to kill you again?

The old hunter begged for forgiveness, declaring that he wouldn't do it again.

The tiger demon harrumphed. “It’s considered a merit that you chased that female cultivator away. Since your merits cancel out your faults, I won't punish you this time.”

The tiger demon didn't have the habit of toying with its prey. It bent down to size Qi Wu up, making a sound as if there was phlegm in his throat. “You're the smartest one here. If you are willing to serve me, I can transform you into a tiger-henchman ghost where you will neither be dead nor alive.”

At this point, Qi Wu was no longer scared. He pointed at the old hunter and sneered, “If I had to go around harming people like him, I might as well die! Bah!”

“You don't know what's good for you! I gave you the easy way out, but you chose to do it the hard way!” Having never been insulted like this before, the tiger demon flew into a rage. The sound waves spread out, causing the roof of the temple to vibrate and threaten to collapse.

The tiger demon gave up on talking them into surrender. It opened its humongous bloody mouth and pounced toward everyone. Qi Wu shut his eyes, waiting for his demise.

Just then, a gentleman sword appeared between the tiger demon and Qi Wu. The sword rays were dazzling, radiating like the sun at dawn as it cut across the tiger demon's face.

“Who is it?!” the tiger demon bellowed in ire.

“Your Mountain God Grandfather!”

Chapter 44: Gentlemen Hide Weapons On Themselves

Qi Wu watched incredulously as the scene unfolded before his eyes. The clay Mountain God statue has come alive! And it’s wielding a sword to slay demons!

“The Mountain God has answered our prayers,” Ayue commented in a daze.

Qi Wu was the fastest to react. “That’s not right. Someone was hiding in the Mountain God statue!”

Consuming this pill could let one obtain the strength of ten buffaloes!

This pill definitely takes the throne among explosive-type pills!

With the combination of my cultivation as a sword cultivator and the strength of ten buffaloes, never mind if you're a tiger with a trace of the Qiongqi bloodline, I’ll even dare fight a pure-blood Qiongqi!

Chapter 47: Breaking Word Mantra

~Pill Cauldron Peak~

New novel chapters are published on novelbuddy.cσ๓.

“What is most important to us pill-concocting masters is learning how to think out of the box. Pills don’t necessarily have to boost the strength of the person who ingested it. One example is my version of the Ten-Bull Strength Pill,” Wu Ming spoke with confidence in the Pill Cauldron Learning Hall, giving a complicated yet accessible lecture on the principles of pill concoction.

The disciples below at their desks furiously took down notes, thinking to themselves, It’s hard to hear these precious pill concoction principles in the outside world. Pill-concocting masters in the outside world placed enormous emphasis on passing down a legacy. As the saying went, “Teach the disciple well and the shifu starves.” As such, learning the principles of pill concoction in the outside world was fraught with challenges.

It was, however, different for Pill Cauldron Peak. They wished they could impart all of their knowledge, teaching the new junior disciples their own ideas without any other regard.

The pill-concocting masters in the outside world were particular about tradition and posited that the ways of the ancestors should not be changed. Hence, there were many challenges to letting the outside world understand the principles of pill concoction on Pill Cauldron Peak.

Seeing his junior disciples listen to the lesson with rapt attention, Wu Ming was inwardly very delighted.

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s intake for this cohort didn't just include Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Man Gu, Tao Yaoye, and Li Haoran. It was simply because they had such remarkable talent and became the center of attention in the sect, causing others to subconsciously overlook the remaining new disciples.

Apart from the five of them, there were many disciples who had a Dual Spirit Root, Triple Spirit Root, or unique skills. They would become the backbone of the Dao-Seeking Sect in the future.

The disciples attending the class were those who had chosen to become disciples of the Pill Cauldron Peak. They had studied for more than a year but were still figuring out the way of pill concoction.

“Many cultivators have the habit of ingesting pills in the heat of battle to unleash strength several times their own. The sudden eruption of power can catch opponents off guard, thereby achieving victory.

“Victory may be a good thing in itself, but such a method causes the amplified strength to surge through the meridians. However, the meridians are only so wide, and this sudden force through the meridians can cause significant damage; in severe cases, it may even be detrimental to one's cultivation.

“As pill-concocting masters, our responsibility is to treat illnesses and save lives, so we must try our best to prevent such situations from occurring. To achieve that end, I have researched painstakingly and visited a good friend specializing in summoning arrays. At long last, I invented this version of Ten-Buffalo Strength Pill.

“The pill contains a miniature summoning array. After one ingests it, it will use their body as a medium to summon ten water buffaloes to aid them in battle.”

An adorable junior female disciple who had been listening intently asked, “Senior Brother Wu, where do the water buffaloes come from?”

Wu Ming smiled. “They're summoned from the spirit fields.”

The food served in the dining halls and restaurants were mostly grown from the Dao-Seeking Sect’s own spirit fields. There were strict requirements to the soil, fertilizer, and farming methods to obtain such high-quality produce.

The Blue-Eyed Water Buffaloes worked hard in tilling the spirit fields. They were an incredibly strong race and consisted of members from the Qi Training to Nascent Soul stages. There was even an old buffalo king at the Divine Transfiguration Stage—a truly terrifying force.

When Third Elder was young, he got carried away by his fervor and shoved the buffaloes in the spirit fields away, plowing through the night. These were the buffaloes from the Blue-Eyed Water Buffalo race.

The Blue-Eyed Water Buffaloes loved to lock horns with one another, so Wu Ming contacted them to see if they were willing to be summoned during battle. They readily agreed.

“As pill-concocting masters, all of you have to be like me and put yourselves in the shoes of those consuming the pills. Think about why they want to ingest the pills, whether there are side effects, and if there is a better solution.”

Wu Ming had written a paper on his results from concocting the Ten-Buffalo Strength Pill and submitted his draft to the leading publication Pill Fire. The person in charge was flabbergasted by Wu Ming’s out-of-the-box ideas and forwarded it to the leading publication in the field of summoning.

And it was successfully published.

Wu Ming was also aware of how ahead of his time his ideas were and that he needed to allow some time for cultivators to adjust, so he set a very low price for the Foundation Establishment Ten-Bull Strength Pill, only requiring a hundred contribution points.

To put that into perspective, even the youtiao in the dining hall cost one hundred and fifty contribution points.

Wu Ming was also thorough in his consideration. He stated the effects of the pill on the redemption list: ingesting this grants the strength of ten buffaloes.

~~~

Lu Yang fell into deep thought.

Even if I say that this pill is fake, it does grant the person who consumes it the strength of ten bulls. The description and its effects align perfectly.

But if I say that this pill is real, it feels like there's something off about it.

What exactly went wrong?

I can't figure it out.

The ten Foundation Establishment water buffaloes were strong and sturdy. In an orderly fashion, they charged toward the tiger demon in a display of power.

Faced against these fierce buffaloes, even if the Half-Step Golden Core tiger demon was at the Golden Core Stage, it still wouldn't dare to take a hit from the herd. No matter how much the tiger demon’s strength grew, it was still not a match for the buffalo demons.

Lu Yang couldn't help but be reminded of the saying again. Although the Pill Cauldron Peak isn't reliable, they have never gone wrong with their pill’s potency. The summoned ten buffaloes can definitely defeat the tiger demon.

Man Gu and Meng Jingzhou subconsciously relaxed.

The outcome was already determined; the tiger demon couldn't turn the tide.

With its eyes widened and hair bristling, it seemed that the tiger demon also knew that it couldn't defeat the ten water buffaloes.

If that's the case, then I'll drag someone down with me!

Just then, a loud crash reverberated through the air. The Mountain God Temple had collapsed. The temple was originally on the brink of collapsing, and the herd of ten water buffaloes took it down with one hit.

For a while, the smoke and pouring rain blended together, obscuring everyone's view.

The tiger demon seized this opportunity, leaping high up and dodging the buffaloes’ attack and springing right towards Lu Yang as swift as lightning!

This human must die!

As the water buffaloes were cumbersome and not adept at jumping, they couldn't react in time.

Man Gu and Meng Jingzhou cried out in shock. They had let down their guard and didn't have enough time to save Lu Yang.

Everyone except Lu Yang was panic-stricken. He remained composed as he had long guessed that the tiger demon would fight to the death and take himself down with it.

After all, a cornered beast is the most dangerous!

Lu Yang didn't dodge. Instead, he used the spell “To Inches,” shrinking himself and the sword.

The tiger demon missed, and Lu Yang appeared directly below it. He returned to his original size, and the cyan spirit energy in his sword concentrated at its tip.

“Break!”

Lu Yang unleashed the Breaking Word Mantra. His sharp Qingfeng Sword was unstoppable, piercing through the tiger demon’s thick hair and right into its abdomen with a squelch. The tip of the sword was covered in blood as it emerged from the other side of the tiger demon.

This was a sword technique he had learned at Heaven’s Gate Peak. Among all sword techniques, this possessed the strongest offense. Just this one blow drained half of his spirit energy. It was to be used with discretion.

During the battle earlier, Lu Yang had already identified the tiger demon’s weakness—only the center of its abdomen had the weakest defense.

Releasing the azure sword qi as fine as buffalo hair, they bloomed within the tiger demon’s body like countless long needles piercing through it. Crackling sounds like fireworks echoed from within the tiger demon, trailing up its spine and rushing toward the top of its head.

With blood flowing from its seven orifices, the tiger demon fell to the ground.

Exhausted and panting, Lu Yang leaned against the wall and signaled for Man Gu and Meng Jingzhou to assist Lan Ting in finishing off the remaining demon.

Upon seeing her husband dead, the female tiger demon became even more ferocious, intent on fighting to the death. Lan Ting could barely suppress this cornered beast.

Before Man Gu and Meng Jingzhou joined in the new battle, the water buffaloes turned to charge toward the female tiger demon. Unable to dodge in time, the female tiger demon was trampled into a bloody mess.

The battle was over.

Lan Ting’s jaw dropped and was reminded of the strange rumors her senior sisters had mentioned about the Dao-Seeking Sect. Initially skeptical, she now believed seven-tenth of it.

Chapter 48: Lair

Seeing that the battle was over and that their mission was complete, the ten water buffaloes vanished into thin air, returning to the spirit fields.

“How are you feeling? Can you stand?” Man Gu asked in concern.

He was fully impressed by Lu Yang’s decisive blue sword strike. Although he and Meng Jingzhou had played an assistive role and injured the tiger demon, Man Gu suspected that even without their help, Lu Yang’s sword alone could still have slain the tiger demon.

Lu Yang swallowed a packet of Qi Restoration Powder, and his breathing soon returned to normal, though his speed of recovery was much faster than what a few doses of Qi Restoration Powder were capable of.

“I should have bought Qi Restoration Pills instead. This Qi Restoration Powder is so dry,” Lu Yang grumbled under his breath. Activating the Water Condensation Mantra, a tiny ball of water appeared at Lu Yang’s fingertips and extended into a two–finger-wide stream, entering his mouth.

“Did you just use Size At Will?” Meng Jingzhou had noticed Lu Yang suddenly becoming small and large again. He found this technique to be very similar to the technique Size At Will an uncle in his clan displayed.

However, based on what he knew, this spell was extremely hard to execute and had a high barrier to entry. One must minimally be at the Golden Core Stage to master it.

“Something roughly similar. What I used was the spell ‘To Inches.’”

“To Inches?” Meng Jingzhou’s head was full of question marks. As a member of the Meng Family, he had heard nearly every spell, but he was totally unfamiliar with this one.

Could it be an exclusive spell created by Big Senior Sister Yun Zhi?

That would make sense.

“Greetings, fellow Daoists, I am Lan Ting.” Lan Ting walked over gracefully.

“All three of us are disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. This is Meng Jingzhou and this is Man Gu.” Due to the urgency of the situation earlier on, Lu Yang had only managed to introduce himself.

“Nice to meet you, Fellow Daoist Meng and Fellow Daoist Man.” It was clear that Lan Ting carried herself well and was polite to everyone. Even when she ran into Qi Wu and the rest, she didn't chase them out just so that she could seek shelter from the rain in the Mountain God Temple.

“Much thanks for lending a hand, Fellow Daoist Lan Ting. It was a headache dealing with the two tiger demons attacking together, and we might even have failed the mission,” Lu Yang expressed his gratitude.

There were just words out of courtesy. In fact, the three of them still had a trump card.

“So this was your mission.” Lan Ting didn't say more.

She had also descended the mountain to complete a secret mission. However, she was unfamiliar with the area. She didn't leave the mountain during the day, and when it was night, she encountered the rain. While finding a place to stay for the night, she had stumbled across this whole situation.

“I know a bit of talisman rune techniques. The hides of these two tiger demons look decent. Would you be willing to part with them and let me have them?”

“Of course,” Lu Yang replied with a smile. “What else do you need, Fellow Daoist Lan Ting? Feel free to take them away.”

The tiger hides were indeed worth much money, but they still couldn't be compared to Lan Ting's aid.

Lan Ting shook her head, not making any further requests.

Having grown up in the wild with his parents, Man Gu was no stranger to skinning. With two fingers pressed together, they became even sharper than a butcher's knife. In a few moves, he has already skinned the two tiger hides whole.

After accepting the tiger hides, Lan Ting bid goodbye to the trio and disappeared into the mountain forest. Her senior sisters had advised her to be cautious about approaching those from the Dao-Seeking Sect until she was mentally stronger to avoid being influenced by them.

“Jingzhou, do you want the tiger bones and tiger whip[1]?”

Meng Jingzhou was befuddled. “What would I do with those?”

Lu Yang grinned mischievously. “To boost your yang, of course.”

“Get lost!”

With my Pure Yang Spirit Root, why would I still need to boost my yang? How can my body possibly take it if I still try to do so?

“Make sure to take good care of these two tiger demons; they’re crucial evidence of us completing the mission.” Lu Yang took out his jade pendant and brushed it with his thumb, absorbing the corpses inside.

The jade pendant could also function similarly to a storage ring.

“Let’s go. The female tiger demon made quite a commotion when it came over, knocking down several trees. We can follow its trail and head in the opposite direction; we should be able to find their lair.”

Having occupied Pine Mountain for many years, the tiger demon certainly had a lair.

The torrential rain didn’t affect them; any rain-repelling chant did its work. The three of them ambled along the fallen trees and shattered boulders, soon finding the tiger demons’ lair.

The cave was three meters tall and was pitch black inside.

“Anyone bring a torch?” Man Gu asked. We can’t see anything inside the cave. Who knows if there are some traps?

He had read in books that mysterious and eerie caves were ideal for installing traps and mechanisms. One might accidentally step onto a brick, and arrows from both walls would turn the person into a porcupine. It was also possible for a sudden gust of poisonous gas to kill them. If not, rolling boulders could crush people to death.

“Who would set so many traps and mechanisms in their home? Are they worried that it’s too convenient to go home?” Lu Yang didn’t know how else to respond. He felt that Man Gu’s thoughts often wandered off in strange directions.

That said, a torch was necessary to create the atmosphere of an adventure. Just imagine. As the rain pelts down outside the cave, the three people in the cave discover treasures while holding torches. Just thinking about this atmosphere is so exciting!

“Who would bring a torch for no reason?” Meng Jingzhou ridiculed. Why would one use torches when there’s fire manipulation techniques?

“Think outside the box.” Lu Yang whipped out a youtiao and lit it with a spark. The whole youtiao ignited.

It looked like the youtiao torch could last quite a while.

Lu Yang held the blazing youtiao, not afraid of being burned. In fact, he was even pleased with himself. The things from the dining hall are really useful. Not only can they be eaten and used in combat, they can even be used as torches.

Man Gu was enlightened. As I thought, I can learn new things by following Brother Lu.

Lu Yang took the lead, holding the youtiao torch up high, while Man Gu and Meng Jingzhou followed behind.

There were no traps from Man Gu’s imagination.

There was only a wild beast’s lair.

And rare treasures from traveling merchants, classic texts from scholars, martial arts secret manuals from martial artists... They didn’t have to hand this over to the sect; they were considered their spoils of war.

“Jewels and antiques...” As Meng Jingzhou had the most extensive knowledge, they let him take on the task of identifying the origins of the items.

“Teacups from a hundred years ago; they’re not worth much.” For cultivators, a hundred years was but a blink of an eye. Even a random item from his house could be more than a hundred years old. In the cultivation world, antiques were almost worthless. Only mortals cared for them.

“A rusty metal knife. Why did the tiger demons keep this? To sharpen their teeth?” Meng Jingzhou shook his head.

Lu Yang thought to himself, Don’t underestimate a rusty knife. Believe it or not, one cut could give you tetanus.

“Animal Form Fist? Isn’t this a type of folk martial art that mimics animals?” Meng Jingzhou flipped through a few pages but wasn’t interested and tossed it to Lu Yang.

The latter was somewhat interested and decided to practice it when he had the time.

“Words of Sages...” Meng Jingzhou snorted. “What use is there for two beasts to hold on to this book? Weren't they still beasts?”

Words of Sages was an introductory book for Confucian cultivators, recording the sages’ earnest teachings. Man Gu had memorized the contents by heart and possessed a deep understanding. He stowed away the book, not because it was particularly valuable but because of its special status.

I should store it properly to show respect to the sages.

“Hmm? There’s a letter here. It’s addressed to the tiger demons?”

Chapter 49: Diabolic Creed

“Who would write a letter to the tiger demons? Haven’t they been hiding from the cultivators so that their whereabouts are unknown?”

The three of them couldn’t make sense of it. Considering how cautious the tiger demons were, there shouldn’t be anyone outside the mountain aware of their existence.

“Why don’t you read out what the letter says?”

Meng Jingzhou cleared his throat, reading out loud with an infectious tone, “Brother Tiger, it’s been a while. How have you been? You have been prudent and unwilling to show yourself, only targeting mortals so that cultivators from the righteous path aren’t aware of your existence. Your cautious approach is admirable, but cultivating like this is ultimately too slow. With the Great Era imminent, factions are beginning to emerge and vie for supremacy, and various parties are eyeing the Central Continent. Didn’t you also seize this opportunity to leave your old home in the Demon Region, break free from the Qiongqi lineage, and thus infiltrate Pine Mountain?

“Being careful...don’t push me. I’m already reading it for you!” Lu Yang and Man Gu sandwiched Meng Jingzhou in the middle so that they could directly see the contents of the letter.

“You read too slow.”

“I’ll read faster; you two move aside.”

Meng Jingzhou pushed the two away and continued reading, “Being careful may not be a major problem in itself, but in this recovering world, one must be bold to grab hold of fortuitous opportunities. Take a leap of faith, refine your bloodline, and transform into a pure-blood Qiongqi. Only then would you have a place in this Great Era.

“May I boldly suggest that you and your wife join me in the Yanjiang Branch? We shall hunt cultivators as prey and plot great deeds together! This envelope contains a token from me. You can come to Yanjiang Branch and use the token to look for me. I can recommend you to become an administrator directly.

“Humble regards, Qin Yuanhao.”

The letter was not long but revealed much critical information.

Lu Yang analyzed, “The letter mentioned that the tiger demons didn't want to let cultivators of the righteous path know of their existence, but this doesn't align with what people would normally say. Most people wouldn't directly say ‘cultivators from the righteous path’ unless the writer of this letter takes the opposite side. Could this Qin Yuanhao be a cultivator from the diabolic path?”

That would also explain why there were cultivators who knew about the tiger demons but didn't report it.

On the Central Continent, the righteous path held an absolute advantage, so demons, devils, and ghosts were natural allies. With the tiger demons as an example, they wouldn't directly attack people but instead get tiger-henchman ghosts to lure them over.

Not only did the male tiger demon possess the Qiongqi bloodline, it was also at the Golden Core Stage. It only made sense for the diabolic path cultivators to attempt winning it over to their side.

“If that's the case, is Yanjiang Branch a diabolic creed’s base?”

Meng Jingzhou nodded. “Diabolic creeds like to name their bases based on their location. It's just that we don't know which diabolic creed Yanjiang Branch belongs to.”

Similar to how righteous path cultivators had the Five Great Immortal Sects, diabolic path cultivators had the Four Great Diabolic Creeds.

Diabolic creeds were cults and not sects. The greatest difference was whether they worshiped a powerful entity. The Four Great Diabolic Creeds held different faiths. Some claimed that their beliefs represented four immortals while others said that they were simply four different incarnations of an immortal. There was no consensus.

The diabolic creeds hardly revealed anything to the outside world, and their whereabouts were elusive. The Great Xia Dynasty and the Five Great Immortal Sects had collaborated on multiple occasions but still failed to locate the headquarters of the diabolic creeds. Whenever righteous cultivators weeded out a large area of the diabolic creeds’ bases, members of the diabolic creeds would pop up again like bamboo shoots growing after a rain. There was no end to killing them.

Although the diabolic creeds were said to be mysterious, using strange and ruthless methods and instilling fear in people's hearts, it was ultimately because the righteous path was too strong. As such, the diabolic creeds didn't dare to reveal themselves, resorting to playing tricks and operating from the shadows.

Anyone who could find the diabolic creeds’ main lair didn't even need to ask the Five Great Immortal Sects to intervene. The Great Xia Dynasty could just dispatch soldiers and turn the diabolic creeds inside out in just five days and eliminate all their bases in a month.

This content is taken from fгeewebnovёl.com.

This was the confidence of the righteous path.

The diabolic creeds were still unpresentable and not up to standards.

Lu Yang shook the envelope, revealing a bone tablet. A special true qi still lingered on it, left behind by the diabolic creed member, Qin Yuanhao. Outsiders couldn't imitate it.

Man Gu wondered, “Can we use this tablet to join the diabolic creeds?”

Locating a diabolic creed’s base was a major achievement, much more valuable than annihilating two tiger demons.

Lu Yang shook his head. “No, if we use this tablet to join the Yanjiang Branch, Qin Yuanhao will definitely find out. Besides, we don't know where the Yanjiang Branch is. How are we going to join them?”

“What should we do then?” Man Gu asked.

“Since they're called Yanjiang Branch, they should be in Yanjiang Commandery. We can go to Yanjiang Commandery and inquire if there is someone called Qin Yuanhao. We'll follow him and find Yanjiang Branch. Since he addressed himself humbly before the tiger demon, his cultivation shouldn't be higher than that of the tiger demon, so we can get rid of him. That way, we can directly use the tablet and say that we are old friends of Qin Yuanhao; we came to seek him out, not expecting that he had died.”

“Good idea.” Meng Jingzhou's and Man Gu’s eyes lit up.

“Rummage through the place once more; see if we can find any other good stuff.” Lu Yang excitedly urged Meng Jingzhou to get to work.

Meng Jingzhou came across a blood-red grass. It was the size of his palm and looked a little demonic. “Why does the Blue-Blood Grass have red veins?” Meng Jingzhou was bewildered. The primary use of Blue-Blood is detoxification, and its veins are cyan and resemble flowing rivers. Why is this particular one red?

Lu Yang crouched down to examine it. “Have you forgotten? The primary use of Blue-Blood Grass for humans may be a key ingredient in detoxification pills, but that isn't the case for demons. As Blue-Blood Grass has the effect of refining blood, the tiger demon could have been using its blood on the Blood-Blue Grass for a long time so that it’d mature and become accustomed to the Qiongqi bloodline. It looks like it’ll take a few more months for the Blue-Blood Grass to become completely ripe. After the tiger demon consumes it, its Qiongqi bloodline will be even more refined, and it can seize this opportunity to form its Golden Core.”

That was how the term “blood” in its name came about. Lu Yang had learned about the Blue-Blood Grass from the little herb kings. He continued, “Now that this Blue-Blood Grass can no longer be concocted into detoxification pills, it can only allow demons to purify their blood when ingested. “

“In that case, you can stow it away and sell it during the sect’s market on the fifteenth of every month. It should be able to fetch a good price.” Meng Jingzhou passed the herb to Lu Yang and Man Gu.

As there was a sizable number of people in the sect who raised demon beasts, herbs that could improve their bloodline had quite a demand.

Lu Yang and Man Gu kept declining the Blue-Blood Grass and offered it to the other party in an exchange of courtesy. In the end, Man Gu couldn’t beat Lu Yang in terms of politeness and accepted the Blue-Blood Grass.

Meng Jingzhou reminded Man Gu, “Don’t eat the Blue-Blood Grass. The Ancient Barbarian Tribe is a branch of humans; the herb has no use on your bloodline.”

“Oh,” Man Gu responded in pity.

Legend said that the Ancient Barbarian Tribe originated from a romantic marriage proposal. In ancient times, humans still lived in scattered tribes. The strongest person in the tribe would be called a warrior.

One day, two tribes met. A male warrior from one of the tribes took a liking to a female warrior from the other tribe and proposed to her. “Hey girlie, smile for me. If you make me happy, I’ll marry you.”

The female warrior laughed mischievously, raising a rock and swinging it back. The two became entangled in a brawl. Finally, the female warrior prevailed and dragged the male warrior into a room.

It was a sleepless night.

Ten months later, the first Barbarian Tribe fighter was born.

Chapter 50: What Did The Sages Say Again?

Meng Jingzhou came across a piece of old tiger hide that looked like it had a hundred years of history. However, it was well-preserved, the tiny and dense characters still clearly visible on its surface. Lu Yang and Man Gu curiously craned their necks, but they didn’t recognize the characters.

“This is the demon script, characters from the demon tribes,” Meng Jingzhou explained.

The Fox Tribe is innately licentious, and it was also reflected in their writing. They often wrote some unhealthy books. If someone did some indescribable acts with these books, the author would be able to collect a trace of yang energy. Therefore, most unhealthy books circulating in the Central Continent were written by the Fox Tribe.

When Meng Jingzhou was young, he was obsessed with such books. However, he didn’t know what the indescribable things were back then. He simply found the books enjoyable. In order to read their original versions, he specially learned the demon script.

“You’re so fond of learning?” Lu Yang and Man Gu were surprised.

Cultivation could enhance one’s memory, so learning a language wouldn’t take much time. However, the thing was that Meng Jingzhou had already learned the demon script before cultivating. That made it very impressive.

Meng Jingzhou didn’t wish to explain the deeper reason, simply stating that he had some interest in demon culture.

Man Gu thought, As expected of Brother Meng. He works hard but doesn’t boast. His humility and noble character are worth learning.

“What’s written on the tiger hide?”

“Let me take a look...ghost beings, with yin and without yang...this is a method to command ghost servants.” Meng Jingzhou swiftly skimmed through it and did some mental calculations, soon deducing the purpose. “The old hunter was probably created this way. There are also requirements for creating ghost beings. The cultivation must be two main stages apart, but mortals are an exception. After one reaches Level Seven Qi Training, they can use the souls of mortals.”

The technique for commanding ghost servants was very impractical. One could only refine someone two stages lower than themselves. Even if a ghost servant was created, it was unlikely for it to be effective in battle.

Take the recent battle with the tiger demons. Had the ghost servant appeared, it probably have been even less useful than cannon fodder.

“Do you need me to translate all of it? This thing doesn’t seem to be limited to race. Humans can also cultivate this, but the results are better for tiger demons.”

Man Gu was about to question the usefulness of this technique when Lu Yang analyzed, “If we join a diabolic creed, we can’t run away from diabolic methods. This ghost servant commanding technique is best for putting up a facade. There are also ready tiger-henchman ghosts at the old hunter’s place. Translate the technique on the tiger hide so that all three of us can learn.”

Lu Yang’s original plan was to eliminate the tiger-henchman ghosts. Now that the situation had changed, it wouldn’t be too late to make use of the tiger-henchman ghosts first before dispelling their souls. According to what the tiger demon implied, the tiger-henchman ghosts were willing to become ghost servants after dying and harm the travelers.

They deserve to die.

“Alright,” Meng Jingzhou agreed. He laid out some paper and ground the ink. With rapid strokes of the brush, he soon wrote down the ghost servant commanding technique.

“I won’t be cultivating it. I have a Pure Yang Spirit Root. When ghosts see me, it’s like snow seeing the sun. I can’t practice this kind of pure yin spell.”

Lu Yang and Man Gu spoke no further and began to cultivate together. Not long after, a cold breeze blew inside the cave followed by the faint wails of ghosts, bringing chills that seeped into the bones.

Lu Yang felt his body becoming lighter. His feet left the ground and he floated in the air like a ghost. He felt like he had never been this awake before. His senses were sharp, detecting any minute details in his surroundings. He even felt that Meng Jingzhou seemed like a blazing ball of fire!

“Hmm? What’s going on?” Lu Yang wondered. Lowering his head, he realized that he was still sitting cross-legged at where he was.

“Hold on, it’s not that I can fly; it’s because my soul has left my body!”

Meng Jingzhou sensed something amiss with Lu Yang and shouted in alarm, “Only those at the Nascent Soul Stage can have their souls leave the body and wander across distances. Why can you do it now?

“Quick, get back! You’re only at the Foundation Establishment Stage and haven’t cultivated your soul. It’s easy for your soul to get damaged, and if it does, it’d be hard to repair it!”

Lu Yang also realized the gravity of the situation. He used the ghost servant commanding mantra, and his soul returned to normal.

“How did you do that?” Meng Jingzhou hadn’t heard of anyone who dared to let their soul leave their body when they were at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

There wasn’t even such a technique.

Lu Yang was also perplexed. “I just cultivated according to what you wrote. I thought that I had understood it completely and I didn’t see any problems, so I figured I’d try it out to see what it’s like, and then it ended up like this.”

Meng Jingzhou looked at Lu Yang with a strange expression. “Could it be that you treated your own soul as a ghost servant and commanded yourself?”

I haven’t heard of such a way to practice, but based on the current situation, this seems like the only explanation.

Lu Yang pondered a bit more but also couldn’t think of other possibilities. He told Meng Jingzhou to stand further away. Despite trying a few more times, the outcome was the same. Lu Yang’s soul would leave his body.

“What’s up with my talent in spells?”

Out of options, the two could only wait for Man Gu to wake up so that they could ask him whether his situation was similar to Lu Yang’s.

When Man Gu woke up, he saw Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou staring expectantly at himself, leaving him utterly confused.

“Have you learned the ghost servant commanding technique?”

“I have learned a little. I should be able to command eight mortal souls.”

“Can you command yourself and let your soul leave your body?” Lu Yang looked at Man Gu eagerly, wishing that Man Gu would say yes so that it would prove that he didn’t practice it wrong.

Man Gu was even more baffled. “How is that possible? This is a ghost servant commanding technique. Don’t tell me that we can treat our soul as a ghost servant and command it?”

Meng Jingzhou glanced at Lu Yang and recounted the latter’s learning journey, leaving Man Gu in awe. Brother Lu is quick-witted and has unparalleled talent in learning spells while Brother Meng is brilliant and well-read.

He had learned many things throughout this journey, as if they were words that had been uttered by the sages.

What did the sages say again?

Oh right! A sage once said, “In a company of three, everyone is my teacher.”[1]

“We should go look for the tiger-henchman ghosts.” With nothing much else left in the cave, Meng Jingzhou beckoned his companions to leave.

Updated from freewebnσvel.cøm.

“You two can leave first. I have to settle a bit of something; I’ll catch up afterward.” Lu Yang told Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu to depart first.

The two didn’t think much of it and left the tiger’s den. After confirming that the two had left, Lu Yang’s smile faded, and his expression became calm once more. He walked to the depths of the cave and saw a small mountain of bones, gently sighing, “It’s indeed here.”

When Lu Yang saw the various items, he had already guessed that based on the tiger demon’s cautious character, he surely wouldn’t throw the bones outside after eating someone. That would expose itself too easily. The safe course of action would be to leave the remains in the cave.

Reality also corroborated his theory.

These pitiful people were deceived and devoured when passing by Pine Mountain. They came from different places and were here for sundry of reasons. However, all of their final resting places ended up in this tiny cave.

Lu Yang didn’t say anything more. The Qingfeng sword effortlessly sliced off a huge rock from the cliff. After smoothening out the rock, he silently recited the Rebirth Requiem and erected a tombstone for these pitiful people.

He fell quiet and became lost in thought for a moment before turning around to leave.

“Thanks for waiting, let’s go,” Lu Yang called out to his companions, ready to leave this bleak place.
